ISETHULO 

Kumafungwase wakwethu uBadumile: 

Ngezwa ngingezwa ngengakuzwayo, 
Ngahluleka ukuphendula ababuzayo 
Ngombik’owusungul’enhliziyweni 
Wokuhlwithwa kukasaziway’endaweni. 

Ngazithola ngilele ngingalele, 
Ngihlezi ngingahlezi ngidangele, 

Ngifile ngingafile kulo mhlaba, 

Ezibilini kuqaqamba sakuhlaba. 


Ngathatha ngibeka ngizibuza, 
Ngizibuza umbuzo wokubuzwa: 
Kufa, awudeli yini? 
Nkosi, uyanqotshwa yini? 


Kwakulukhuni satshe kunguKhisimuzi, 
Usemanzini owakho umuzi 
Ngokuvakashelwa yiNkosi kanzima, 
Yakushiya nemvunulo enzima. 


Lwafik’usuku lokumphelekezela, 

Ngehluleka ngisho nokubekezela, 
Zehla zigeleza zigobhoza 
Bonke benxolombisile sakukhophoza. 


Ngayibuka intombi eyasizalayo 
Yayimemez’uBaba owasidalayo, 
Ngayibuka ngayibheka yabhekeka, 
Namazwi yawabeka abekeka. 


Bambelel’osaneni olukhona, 
Lufundise ngemadlana ekhona, 
INkosi izokwesula izinyembezi, 
Wena hlalela ethembeni. 



AMAZWI OMLOBI 

Le ndaba yakhelwe phezu kwezindawo ezikhona ngempela. 
Izehlakalo, abalingiswa nezenzo zabo, konke kususelwe ekhanda 
nje. Uma kwenzeka ukuba igama lomlingiswa lifana nelakho, 
nxese, phephisa wena weqhawe! 

Ngizwakalisa ukubonga kwami kubashicileli bakwa Shuter & 
Shooter ngakho konke abakwenzile ukuze lo msebenzi ube kuleli 
qophelo. Ngithanda ukuqhakambisa igama, phakathi kwamanye, 
likaDokotela Nakanjani G. Sibiya ngokuhamba ekhomba imifantu 
obekungase kumfininize amanzi kuyo. Ngenxa yezeluleko zakhe 
ezakhayo nezikhuthazayo, ngikwazile ukuyivala ngengcina leyo 
mifantu. 

Ngibonga angiphezi kumkami oyizinto zonke kimina, uLindeni 
Mary-Rose, uMaDlamini, ngeqhaza alibambile kulo msebenzi. 
Kuningi engikucobelele kuyena okwenze lo msebenzi wahlangana 
kahle kanje. Ngithi unwele olude Sibalukhulu! 

Ngibonge futhi kuzinyobulala wethu, uBlessing Sifiso Wanda 
ngeqhaza alibambile ekushicilelweni kwalo msebenzi. Ngithi 
ukhule uze ukhokhobe ndodana! 


ISAHLUKO SOKUQALA 

“Ingane enhle kanjeya! Awu, Ngeke! Ngeke! Ngangithi 
uMisi Hlophe muhle, ngithi sengithandene nentokazi 
yokugcina empilweni yami. Hhayi, akathathi lutho kule ngane 
yakwaKheswa! Lo mntwana muhle madoda! Muhle ethule, 
muhle ekhuluma, muhle ehamba. Kwakufanele abazali bakhe 
bamqambe bathi nguNozifaca. Ithi uma iqala ukuhleka intokazi 
lena, kuthi faca faca izihlathi. Angazi ukuthi babethi uDumazile 
wani. Kuyacaca ukuthi uMdali wayibumba ngodongwe luseva, 
luyinsada futhi enesikhathi sonke sokuyakha. Akukhona ukuma 
kahle komuntu lokhu! Kuzofanele ngithole ithuba elanele ukuba 
ngibonane nalo mntwana sixoxe ngasese. Kungcono ngoba uMisi 
Hlophe akekho lapha, usaye kolindela ukuteta. Savumelana 
naye ukuthi uyothi angabeletha, ahlale unyaka wonke ekhaya 
eBabanango esakhulisa umntwana. Wonke lo nyaka ngizobe 
ngizihlalele ngedwa lapha.” Lona obalisa ekhuluma yedwa 
nguthisha uMoloi ofundisa eZenzele High School eMbumbulu. 
Kwakusanda kuphela isonto lokuqala nje izikole zivuliwe 
ekuqaleni konyaka ngenkathi edliwa wumzwangedwa 
ecambalele ekotishi. 

Phakathi nesonto lesibili zivuliwe izikole, omemu bathuma 
amantombazane ukuba ayohlanza izindlu zangasese. Kwathi 
angaqeda amantombazane, omemu bahamba ukuyobheka 
ukuthi izindlu lezo zazihlanzisisiwe yini. 

“We Memu! Kodwa uyambona uthisha uMoloi ukuthi 


useyaganga manjena?” kusho uMemu Mpungose efile 
wukucikeka. 
“Uganga ngoba yini?” Sekubuza uMemu Ngcamu ehlahle 
amehlo efuna ukuzizwa zonke. 
“Usengaze impela athandane nengane yesikole pho!” 
“Uthandana nayiphi?” 
“Uthandana noDumazile, isidudla lesi sakwaKheswa 
esisekilasini lakhe.” 
“Usho lesi esiyisigqigqi nje, esingandoni yamanzi, esinetsako 
kanye nonwele lwempunzi?” 
“Enganti-ke, uyasazi nje! Usho sona kanye.” 
“Ukushiso yini ukuthi bayathandana?” 

“Ubomqaphela-ke dade uma sekuyisikhathi senhlabakhefu. 
Yisona isikhathi eziduma ngaso leso. Isidudla lesi uvele 
asijikijelele ukhiye wasekotishi bese yena enza lo doti wabo 
wokuthumela maqede balandele ezithendeni.” 

“Hawu! Othisha abakawuyeki lo mkhuba wabo ka send and 
follow?” 
“Cha memu, akubona bonke othisha abonakele. Yilesi 
sikhohlakali nje sakwaMoloi.” 

“Nakho kodwa okungamantombazane kuyabaheha othisha 
besilisa. Akukhona ukugqoka lokhu! Iziketi kube yimihinininjana 
nje! Lezi zinto ziyahluleka nawukuhlala, ziyadunusa nje!” 

“Ngiyakubona-ke okokudunusa, kodwa ukutota kwezingane 
akunankinga memu. Sikhula thina, amantombazane ayetota 
ngempela. Yayithi uma ihamba nje intombi, umamhlongo 
uwubone ngosi. Kwakungekho lokhu konakala ezinsizweni.” 

“Kodwa uthisha uMoloi uyaganga. Ubengasheli ngani omisi 
bebaningi kangaka lapha esikoleni?” 
“Hhayi bo memu! Kusewukonakala kwakhona lokho. 


Angathini nje uMisi Hlophe uma ezwa lokho?” 

“Ngisho phela uma ebona ukuthi uphethwe yisizungu 
nenkumbulo yomuntu wesibhuda. Cha, yena uyakwazi 
ukukhetha. Yintombi ngempela lena. NoMisi Hlophe kodwa 
ukhona, bekuyintombi ziphelele.” 

“Ufanele phela wukuzikhethela. Angithi welekelelwa yile 
mithi ayisebenzisayo.” Athi dlengelele uMemu Ngcamu, bese 

ethatha ethi: 

“Usebenzisa imithi kanti?” 

“Ehhene! Kuthiwa ngenkathi kuvulwa izikole ngesonto 

eledlule, wayebonakala egquma, akhwife, avuke ekuseni 
aphalaze.” 

“Kahle bo! Ephalazela isidudla lesi?” 

“Ehhene, qiniso so! Wena memu awazi! Mubi kabi uthisha 
uMoloi. Awumboni nje nothishomkhulu engamjakajakadi yena 
njengathi? Ucabanga ukuthi wenziwa yini?” 

“Kodwa izifundiswa zaba yinqaba!” 

“Usho ngani?” 

“Ngisho ngoba phela uma sezithe ziyawuphatha umuthi, 
ziphatha umuthi othi thi. Nakuba kunjalo kodwa, uthisha uMoloi 
usengaze akhendlele ingane yesikole? Kusobala ukuthi wahamba 
wajubalala. Uyoze akhohlwa ethole isipatsha esinjena?” 

“Wumkhuba wezishimane kodwa lowo. Ezinye ziyawaphonsa 
amantombazane ahayize. Kuyenzeka futhi ku...” 

Kwabe sekuzwakala ukuthimula komuntu kwenye 
yezindlwana zangasese encikene naleyo ababekuyo omemu. 

“Ngubani lowo?” kubuza uMemu Ngcamu esefile 
wukwethuka. Kuthi nya. Aphinde abuze futhi kodwa do 
impendulo. Bavula kancane isicabha somnyango wasendlini 
encane, baphuma sebenyonyile bephikelele esitafulumu. 


“We memu! Kungathiwani uma bekunguDumazile lowayana 
obethimula endlini encane?” 

“Ukushiso yini lokho?” 

“Awukhumbuli ukuthi besithe kuyena akahambe 
namantombazane ayosebenza nawo bahlanze izindlu zangasese?” 

“Pho ukuthi nguyena obethimula kuhlangana kanjani naye 
lokho?” 

“Ngisho ngoba phela memu abuyile wonke amantombazane 
abesebenza naye lapho. Nguyena kuphela esingambonanga 
ebuya.” 

“O..., ubelibele wukumekhapha, enzela ukuba abonwe kahle 
wuthisha wakhe.” 

“Hhayi bo Memu! Kahle ngamatshe bo!” 

“Hhayi bo kwani? Kufihlwa kufihlwani ibhasi libhaliwe?” 

“Memu! Kufanele sizidlise satshanyana kuDumazile, simbuze 
ukuthi ubekuphi yena ngenkathi amantombazane ebuyela 
emakilasini awo ngemuva kokuhlanza izindlu zangasese.” 

“Ukuze?” 

“Ukuze phela memu sixolise uma bekunguyena ngempela 
lowayana obesendlini encane. Usizwe kahle phela.” 

“Mina anginandaba nje. Yena uthandanelani nothisha 
eyingane yesikole? Ubeswele ontanga yakhe yini? Sesizobanga 
nezingane zesikole manje lapha kothisha? Uyothini nje uMisi 
Hlophe mzukwane ebuyayo?” 

“Memu! Siboqaphela ngokuzayo. Akulungile ukukhuluma 
ngegama lomuntu uma wena usendlini, ehlathini noma 
ebumnyameni. Angazi nje ukuthi ngizombhekelwa ngubani 
uDumazile uma kwenzeka ukuthi bekunguyena ngempela 
lowayana.” 

“Manjena wena sewufuna sikhekhezele-ke siyoguqa 


ngamadolo phambi kukaDumazile sincenge ukuthi uthandana 
nothisha uMoloi? Mina-ke ngeke ngikwenze lokho,” kusho 
uMemu Mpungose ekhombisa ukungayigqizi qakala nje indaba 
yokuyozehlisa kuDumazile. 

UDumazile, iqhathanzipho lakwabo, wayekade esale 
kwenye yezindlwana ngenkathi amantombazane ebuyela 
emakilasini awo ngemuva kokuhlanza izindlu zangasese. 
Wayesazitomota ngenkathi kungena omemu bekhininda 
izindaba. Kuthimula lokho okwasizayo ngokunqamula inkulumo 
yabo, ngokwabo babesaya kude nendaba. UDumazile wake 
wadunyelwa nje engazi okufanele akwenze. Wathula isikhashana 
esendlini encane eninga ngenkulumo yomemu. 

“Kanti abafundi bangikhipha inyumbazane nje yingoba 
kuthiwa mina ngiqome uthisha uMoloi? Bakuthathaphi lokhu 
abakushoyo? Mh, cishe baye babone ngenkathi ngiyokwenzela 
uthisha itiye ngenhlabakhefu! Pho ngalokho sebengaze bathi 
mina ngithandana nothisha?”Wathula isikhashana uDumazile 
esacabanga. Kwathi ngesikade wavula kancane isicabha, wathi 
qala qala, waphuma eseqonde ekilasini. Wangena maqede 
wahlala phansi. 

UDumazile wazithola esehlezi ezweni lemicabango; 
imicabango eyindida engqondweni yakhe. 

“Kanti mina ngenza iphutha yini ukwenzela uthisha itiye? 
Angithi nabanye abafundi bayathunywa nje ezitolo kodwa 
bangakhishwa inyumbazane, pho mina? Bangathini abazali 
bami uma bengase bezwe le nkulumo eshiwo womemu ngami? 
Ngizomtshela uthisha uMoloi. Futhi ngifuna lolu daba luhambe 
luze lufike kuthishomkhulu. Bazongitshela kahle labo memu 
ukuthi ngelikabani leli gama abalihudula phansi kanjena.” 
UDumazile wathuka esehlekwa ngabafundi. Babembona 
esendwazile nje sengathi kade entongela. Uthisha wabakhuza, 
bathula. Baqhubeka-ke nokufunda. 


Kwathi ngenhlabakhefu, uDumazile wathatha izincwadi 
zakhe wakhala wemuka. Endleleni wayehambisa okohlanya. 
Imicabango yayifika igqibelana. 

“Akekho phela umuntu ongabekezelela into enjena. Ubhecwe 
ngobubende inyama ungayidlanga! Ngeke! Kodwa bona 
bazongitshela kahle ukuthi ngelikabani leli gama abalihudula 
phansi kanjena! Ukube lo gogo engihlala kwakhe akayena 
uphoshozwayo, bengizomtshela le nto. Ngizokwenza njani pho? 
Ngihlale nale nto ilokhu iyisilungulela enhliziyweni? Cha ngeke! 
Okungcono angivuke kakhulu kusasa ngiyobikela uthisha uMoloi. 
Ehhe, kungcono ngenze njalo.” 

Wahamba njalo uDumazile waze wafika lapho eqashe khona. 

“Washesha wabuya namhlanjena mntanomntanani, 
kwenzenjani?” 

“Akukho lutho gogo, wukuthi ngijahe ukuzowasha.” Avule 
endlini yakhe uDumazile. Angene, avale, azishutheke engutsheni, 
ziye amasolokohlo. Waphaphama sekuhwalele, nokho wabuye 
waqhubeka nokulala. Ukusa kwabonwa nguyena uDumazile. 
Wavuka, wageza, wagqoka, waphuma esephikelele khona 
ekotishi. 

UDumazile wamfica uthisha uMoloi esagqoke izingubo 
zokulala. Akabange esaphozisa maseko, wahlala phezu kodaba. 

“Thisha, inhliziyo yami ibuhlungu kabi. Izolo ngize ngeqa 
esikoleni yingoba ngihlulekile ukubekezela nokuzibamba.” Athule 
uDumazile, izinyembezi zigcwale amehlo. Akhumbule uthisha 
uMoloi ukuthi uthe uyambheka ngesikhathi senhlabakhefu, 
kwatholakala ukuthi ubesehambile. Waqhuba wathi: 

“OMemu Mpungose benoMemu Ngcamu bathi mina ngijola 
nawe. Bathi abazi ukuthi ubayekelani omisi bebaningi kangaka 
kulesi sikole?” Athule uDumazile. Kwathi cosololo esebhodlile. 
Lwamuthi heqe uvalo uthisha uMoloi. Wathula naye isikhashana 
ethatha ebeka. 


“Labo memu baze kanjani ukuthi ngiyamncanywa lo 
mntwana? Kungenzeka yini ukuthi kukhona obonayo kumbe 
oyisangoma phakathi kwabo? Kungaba phela ibhemile. Kusobala 
baye bambone ngesikhathi senhlabakhefu eyongishisashisela 
isibindi, ubhekeni namaqanda! Eyi madoda, kusho ukuthi 
sekubhedile-ke! Ngiyophinde ngilitholephi futhi ithuba lokuxoxa 
nalo mntwana sisobabili?” 

Kwezwakala ukunxapha, wathatha wathi, “Labo memu 
baxhumaphi bona?” 

“Angazi Sir.” UDumazile esho ngezwi elipholile namehlo alele. 
Kuqale kuthuleke isikhashana. Kuzwakale uthisha ethi, “Uthi 
bayangazi kahle mina ukuthi ngiqhamuka eMsamu? Sengathi 
abangazi kahle. Ekis ‘n ntwana van Joburg af.” UDumazile 
walinda nje esafuna ukuzwa ukuthi lolu daba luzoqulwa kanjani 
nokuthi omemu laba bazojeziswa kanjani ngokukhuluma 
ngamagama abantu. Uthisha waqala wathula esaxakwe wukuthi 
uzoyikhipha kanjani ingonyuluka yakhe. Wayefa ngoDumazile 
kodwa engakaze ayithi vu kuyena. Kuthe ukuba uDumazile 
alwethule ngale ndlela lolu daba, wabona sekufanele ukuba 
angene ngalo kuhle kwempethu yona engena ngenxeba. 

Wazijuba-ke owengwazi, “Uyabona-ke, asibahlabekise. 
Ehhene asibahlabekise labo memu. Sengathi basinakile.” Aqale 
athule nje uDumazile ekhungathekile, engazi ukuthi omemu laba 
bazohlatshekiswa kanjani. 

“Labo memu bacabanga ukuthi mina lo ngingaqonywa 
yile mijendevu yomisi balapha esikoleni? Ngeke bakubone 
lokho. Angiyona mina into yokuhamba ngiqoqana nayo yonke 
imisalazabiwa lena.”Washo waze wanikina ikhanda. Athule nje 
uDumazile. 

“Uyabona-ke baby, akuvele kucace ukuthi kukhulunywa ngento 
ekhona ngempela. Azivele zilime ziye etsheni.”Wazithulela nje 
uDumazile. Uthisha wabona ukuthi inkukhu sengathi ayiwuboni 


umgqakazo. Waphumela obala, wathatha wathi: 

“Ngithi mina asivele sijole ngempela, futhi siswinge into 
ehambayo ukuze onondaba bakhulume into abayaziyo.” 

“Hhayi bo Sir!”Washo uDumazile wajikisa intamo yabheka 
lena, ekhombisa ukuthi unamahloni ngale nto eshiwo nguthisha 
wakhe. Inhliziyo yakhe yashayela phezulu. “Hamba uyocabanga, 
ucabangisise,” kuqhuba uthisha uMoloi. Bavalelisana uDumazile 
edumele. 

Bawuqala-ke umsebenzi wabo abafundi, kodwa uDumazile 
wayesenkingeni. Imicabango yayimdida ingqondo. 

“Kodwa kungathiwani nje ngithandana nothisha? Abazali 
bami bangangibuka njengomntwana onjani nje? Umama yena 
angathini nje ayengiyala kanjena? Mina uthisha ngimthatha 
njengomzali wami. Pho ngithandane nomzali wami? Kufanele 
ngivele ngiqunge isibindi ngimtshele uthisha ukuthi makakuyeke 
lokhu kungcola kwakhe.” UDumazile wezwa esemenyezwa 
nguthisha ethi makaphumele phandle ashaywe ngumoya. Uthisha 
wayembona uDumazile ukuthi akekho ekhona ekilasini. Nebala 
wenze njalo, waphuma. Wahlala phandle kwaze kwashaya 
isikhathi senhlabakhefu. 

UDumazile wabona kungezukumsiza ngalutho ukuhlala 
esikoleni. Wangena ekilasini maqede wadumela izincwadi zakhe, 
zaya. Wafika emqashweni ngesikhathi esifanayo nesangayizolo. 
Wangena endlini yakhe, wahlala phezu kombhede, wacabanga: 

“Ngiye noma ngingayi ukuyomtshela uthisha ngala manyala 
awakhuluma kimina? Uma ngingayi, uzongijwayela kabi lo thisha. 
Mina ngizele ukuzofunda lapha, hhayi ukuzoqonyiswa nguyena. 
Kuzofanele nakanjani kusasa ngimtshele ukuthi uma eqhubeka 
nale nkulumo yakhe, ngizomceba kuthishomkhulu.” Kwathi 
kusenjalo kwangqongqoza isalukazi esicabheni, sangena. 

“Awu mntanomntanami! Kanti akusafundwa yini lapha 
eZenzele?” 


“Usho ngani gogo?” 

“Ngisho ngoba nayizolo ubuye ngaso lesi sikhathi.” 

“Ngicelile kuthisha ukuba ngizo-ayina izingubo zami lezi 

ebengiziwasha izolo.” 

“Hhayi, ngiyezwa mntanomntanami. Nomakoti wendodana 
ubesekhathazeke kabi. Besithi mhlawumbe kukhona yini into 

ekhona eyingxaki esikoleni.” 

“Cha gogo, akukho lutho.” 

“Siyazi yini izingane sezaba wosiyazi njena.” Bazixoxela 

nezinye izindaba baze bahlukana ngemuva kwesikhathi. 

Ngakusasa esikoleni, njengenjwayelo ngesikhathi 
senhlabakhefu, uthisha uMoloi wanikeza uDumazile ukhiye 
wendlu yakhe. Wamcela ukuba ayomenzela itiye, amshisashisele 
amavosi namaqanda. Nebala uDumazile wawuthatha ukhiye, 
wahamba ngomude umzimba lo. Wafika ekotishi, wangena, 
wahlala phansi esihlalweni. Kwathi esadidekile, esazibuza ukuthi 
kusamfanele yini ukuba enzele uthisha ukudla njengoba kunalezi 
zinkulumo ezinjena, memfu uthisha uMoloi. 

“Kanti bewungakabeki namanzi etiye nje?” Anikine ikhanda 
uDumazile. Uthisha wafunda kwezakhe ukuthi akuzi kahle. 

“Thisha, ngiyakuhlonipha. Isenzo sakho siyayiphazamisa 
inhlonipho enginayo.”Wathi dlengelele uthisha. Kwacweba 
izinyembezi emehlweni kuDumazile, zathi qatha qatha. 
Waqhuba wathi: 

“Abazali bami bangiyala ngenkathi ngisuka ekhaya. Ubaba 
yena wayengafuni sampela nje ukuba ngiqhubeke nesikole ngoba 
imali yokungiqhuba yayingekho. Ngancengelwa ngumama, 
kwadayiswa izinkomo ezimbili zokugcina nakuba uyangibona 
lapha. Ngabathembisa abazali bami ukuthi ngiyoziphatha kahle 
lapha ekuhambeni. Uma wena usuqala inkulumo yokungonisa, 
inhliziyo yami ivele iphatheke kabuhlungu. Ngithi angikwazise-ke 


thisha ngoba le nto ngizoyibikela uthishomkhulu uma iqhubeka.” 

“Uthishomkhulu uxhumaphi kule nkulumo yethu? Futhi 
angithandi ukuba ufake umuntu wesithathu ngoba naye 
uziphathelwe yizinkinga zomuzi wakhe.” 

“Thisha, wena ungathanda nje ingane yakho uma ishelwa 
nguthisha?” 

“Ayikho inkinga lapho. Empeleni yithina bothisha okufanele 
sizikhethele omkethu kuqala, izinsalela-ke sezingathathwa

Lokho kuzokube kungaqali ngawe.” Kukhale insimbi. UDumazile 
waphuma esephikelele ekilasini labo. 

Uthisha yena wake wahlala nje isikhashana enzela ukuba

UDumazile walithatha leli pheshana kanye nesithombe sakhe 
wakufaka emvilophini maqede wayivala. Wayibhala imvilophu 
ngaphandle. Kwake kwaba yinkinga kuDumazile ukuthi 
uyokumnikeza kanjani uthisha le ncwadi. Wazibona engasenaye 
umngani ongase amenzele lo msebenzi. Wagcina ebone kufanele 
ukuba azihambisele yena mathupha. 
NgoMsombuluko ekuseni uDumazile wavuka waqonda 
ekotishi. Wangena maqede wabeka incwadi phezu kwetafula, 
waphuma engazange athi vu ngomlomo. Uthisha waxakeka 
nje ukuthi wokunjani-ke lokhu. Kwathi noma ethi uzama 
ukumlandela ngenhloso yokubuza okuthile, lutho ukuma 
uDumazile. Uthisha wabuyela endlini ukuyozwa ukuthi incwadi 
imfikela naziphi. Wayivula-ke imvilophu. Wathi nhla phakathi, 
wacishe waquleka ebona isithombe sepentshisi lentokazi imise 
amabele. Walibuka nepheshana liqukethe izindaba ezimnandi. 
Kwathi cosololo. Walungiselela ukuya emsebenzini, waphuma. 
Ngesikhathi senhlabakhefu, uthisha wanikeza uDumazile 
ukhiye ukuba ayomenzela itiye ekotishi njengenjwayelo. 
Nempela kwaba njalo. Uthisha wabuye walandela ngemuva 
kwesikhashana nje. Wamfica uDumazile ematasatasa. Wathatha 
wathi, “Ngiyitholile incwadi ongibhalele yona. Ngijabule kabi. 
Ngiyabonga kakhulu mntakwethu.” Lwamuthi heqe uvalo 
uDumazile ukuzwa igama likamntakwabo. Wayengalindele neze 
neze ukuthi lase lingashesha kangaka ukuba lisetshenziswe. 
“Uyabona-ke mntakwethu, kuzofanele ukuba umfundi 
kube ngumfundi esikoleni, nothisha kube nguthisha, ukuze 
kunganakeki. Uma ngikubiza ngegama nje, wena usabele uthi, 
Sir! Kuyothi-ke uma sesizihlalele sobabili, sibizane ngamagama 
ethu ezithopho. Angithi uyezwa sweetheart?”

emaphepheni ngonyaka owedlule; abafundi bezitshela ukuthi 
sebezokhulelwa ngonoqhakala ngoba bejahe imali yeqolo. 
Awulwazi usizi engaluthwalayo ngenkathi umfundi esebelethela 
ngaphakathi kwamagceke esikole! Nani bomemu nangiyekelela 
nje ngithi lekelelani.” 

“Thishomkhulu, ukukhulelwa akuyona ingozi, kodwa 
kungamabomu nje. Umuntu osuke ekhulelwa usuke azi kahle 
ukuthi wenzani. Angazi ukuthi abafundi bamantombazane 
banconywe kuphi ngalokhu kukhulelwa kwabo. Thina 
thishomkhulu safundela ukufundisa, hhayi ukubelethisa. Sabona 
ukuthi asinalo ikhono, isineke kanye nobizo lobuhlengikazi. 
Futhi-ke thishomkhulu, lo msebenzi wokubelethisa ubucayi 
kabi! Kunezinto zakhona ezisetshenziswayo ezandleni ukuvikela 
amagciwane. Sekwasabalala nezifo ezinjengomashayabhuqe, 
kulula kabi ukuthelelana ngaso.” 

“Uqinisile memu. Yiqiniso lelo. Abantu abaningi bacabanga 
ukuthi ingculazi ithathelwana ngokocansi kuphela, kanti cha.” 
Uthishanhloko watshela umemu ukuba abize uDumazile. 
Waphuma. Kwathi nya nya wabuya naye. Bangena, bahlala 
phansi. Uthishanhloko akabange esachitha sikhathi, wahlala 
amagqozo odabeni. 

“Dumazile, sekufikile ezindlebeni zami ukuthi wena 


sewukhulelwe. Kuyiqiniso lokho?” 

UDumazile abheke phansi. Izinyembezi zigcwale amehlo. 
Uthishanhloko aqhube athi: 

“Ngizwa ngidabuka ndodakazi! Qiniso, ngiyadabuka. 
Inqubo nenkambiso yesikole ayingivumeli ukuba ngikugcine 
lapha esikoleni. Le ndawo ingeyabafundi abazofunda. Wena 
sewuzikhethele omunye umunxa wempilo. Ngaleyo ndlela-ke 
ngiyadabuka ukusho ukuthi thatha izincwadi zakho ugoduke. 
Utshele abazali bakho ukuthi awuxoshiwe yimina, kodwa 
uzixoshe wena. Kuyezwakala?”Wathula uDumazile wabheka 
phansi. 

“Uthishomkhulu ukhuluma nawe wena! Wabheka umhlabathi 
nje, awuzwa yini?” kwenanela uMisi Hlophe. Uthishanhloko 
waphendukela ngakumemu, wathatha wathi: 

“Siyabonga memu! Siyabonga ukuba nibe yihlo esikoleni. 
Ngihleze ngibatshela abafundi ukuthi baziphathe kahle kulo 
mhlaba ngoba uyahlaba.” 

“Yebo thishomkhulu, siyabonga nathi,” kubonga uMemu 
Mpungose. 

 Uthishanhloko wadonsa ibhuku lakhe, wabhala phansi 
isehlakalo sosuku. Kwathi angaqeda, watshela uDumazile ukuba 
aphume. Nempela kwaba njalo. 

“Kunjalo nje memu, ayikho futhi enye indlela. Kufanele 
agoduke lo mntwana.” 

“Thishomkhulu, awusabi yini ukuthi uzokumangalela 
uDumazile ngokumxosha kwakho esikoleni?” kubuza umemu 
ecabanga izinkulumo zabanye othisha abaphikisanayo 
nokuxoshwa komfundi esikoleni. 

“UDumazile akaxoshiwe esikoleni. Ugodukisiwe nje 
ukuba alande abazali bakhe ukuze bazochazela umkhandlu 
owengamele isikole ukuthi kuyokwenziwa njani uma umntwana 


wabo eseficwa yisikhathi sokubeletha esemagcekeni esikole 
njengoba singenayo i-ambulense njena. Yilokho nje memu.” 

“Cha ngiyezwa thishomkhulu,” kusho umemu besukuma. 
Bavalelisa, baphuma. 

UDumazile wathatha konke okungokwakhe wakhala wemuka. 
Kwasuka igidigidi kubafundi esikoleni ngenkathi uDumazile 
eseyophuma ngesango. Kwezwakala abanye abafundi bethi: 

“Aphume nobomvu!” Kwathi ngqoklo insini! Ngenkathi efika 
emqashweni uDumazile, wacabanga wajula ngokushiya kwakhe 
isikole. Yayingasekho enye indlela, kodwa kube wukusishiya 
ngempela; asishiye nabafundi abasazimisele ngokufunda. Yena 
wayeseqala impilo entsha; impilo yokuba ngumama oyingane. 
Wathatha izimpahla zakhe, waqonda emgwaqeni omkhulu. 
Ngokuphazima kweso yaqhamuka ithekisi, washo phakathi. 
Yasuka-ke seyiphikelele khona eThekwini. Yafike yamlahla 
ebhasini elihambela kwelakubo. Wagibela, wahlala phansi. 
Akuphelanga mizuzu mingaki, lasuka ibhasi seliphikelele 
eMzimkhulu. Endleleni uDumazile wayebukeka elusizi. Iziyalo 
zikanina zabuya ngothi lwazo: 

“Lalela lapha-ke mntanami, intombi iyintombi ngobuntombi 
bayo. Inkomo kamama isebuntombini bentombi. Usize 
ungelusele yona inkomo yami mntanami. Uma uke 
wangaziphatha kahle Dumazile, kuyobe ungithele ngehlazo.” 

“Ngiyezwa mama. Futhi ngiyathembisa ukuthi ngiyoziphatha 
kahle.” 

Wakucabanga konke lokhu qede washaywa yinzululwane, 
zehla izinyembezi. 


ISAHLUKO SESIBILI 

“Yise kaDumazile, ake ulunguze! Sengathi ikhona into 
ekhonkothwa nguBahlangene phandle!” Athi lacu uKheswa, 
alunguze ngewindi. Abone isithunzana somuntu siza. Athule 
asibukisise. Size kancane isithunzana lesi size sisondele eduze 
kwendlu. 

“UBahlangene ubona umuntu!” 

“Umuntu?” esho kakhulu uMaNdovela. 

“Shh...! Kahle, useseduze!” kusho uKheswa ethulisa umkakhe 
ngokuswebeza. Wamhlalisa phansi njengoba wayeseqala 
ukusukuma ezama ukulunguza naye. Waya ngokuya lo muntu 
esondela ngasesicabheni, wangqongqoza. Ukukhonkotha kwenja 
akubange kusaqhubeka, kodwa yabonakala seyitshikizisa umsila. 

“Ngubani lowo ongqongqozayo?” kubuza umnumzane 
uKheswa. 

“Yimina uDumazile.” 

“UDumazile?” 

“Yebo baba!” 

“Ebekwa yini lapha ngalesi sikhathi?” UMaNdovela ayizwe 
inkulumo bese ecikeka. 

“Vulela umntwana yise kaDumazile! Ingane seyingaze idliwe 
ngamankentshane phandle?” 

UKheswa waqonda esicabheni wafike wavula. Kwabe 


sekungena indodakazi yabo ixhake izimpahla zayo ngapha 
nangapha. Yafike yazithi nzi phansi ngasesininini sawomame, 
yahlala phansi. 

“Hawu mntanami, kanti nguwena?” kusho uMaNdovela 
ebukeka ethukile. Ahleke inhlinini nje uDumazile. Uyise ahlale 
phansi esigqikini sakhe. 

“Sawubona-ke mntanami!” kubingelela uMaNdovela esathukile 
ebona indodakazi yakhe ifika ngalesi sikhathi. 

“Yebo!” 

“Siphuthume mntanami, kwenzenjani?” 

“Eyi mama, siphume ngesamagundane esikoleni! Akuliwa 
akuliwa endaweni yaseMbumbulu! Kubulawa wena nkosikazi, 
wena ngane, wenani nani! Abanandaba nakhehla nasalukazi!” 

“Obani abalwayo?” 

“Mina mama ngivele ngingazi nje ukuthi ngizothi obani 
abalwayo. Selokhu kwaqala lezi zinto zepolitiki nje, abantu 
sebephambene amakhanda. Akufiwa akufiwa eMbumbulu! Nathi 
sizwe ngandlebenye ukuthi sebefuna ukungena bahlasele abafundi 
esikoleni, sabe sesiyaphulukundlela-ke thina zihambi. Hha mame, 
sihlalele izimpi zakoMbumbulu!” 

“Nenze kahle mntanami nabuya ningaze nifele lena emazweni. 
Nibuye nonke nabantwana bakwaMadikizela?” 

“Yebo mama, nakuba singagibelanga ibhasi elilodwa! Ngenkathi 
sihlakazeka, bathe oDayisile bazogibela UTHANDO ngoba lona 
lubehlisa eduzane nakubo.” 

Kuthi xhifi enhliziyweni kamnumzane uKheswa. Azwakale 
esethi: 

“Ngangivele ngishilo kodwa MaNdovela!” Asukume, aphume 
esecikekile eya endlini yabo yokulala. Basale bexoxa oDumazile 
benonina. 


“Umbona ephuma nje uyihlo mntanami usecasukile.” 

“Ucasulwa yini mama?” 

“Ucasulwa wukuthi awusaqedanga ukufunda eMbumbulu 
phezu kwemizamo yethu engaka siwa sivuka, silala singadlile 
ngoba sithi senzela wena ukuba uqhubeke nokufunda. Uyihlo 
wayesenqumile ukuba ungaphindeli esikoleni ngonyaka odlulile.” 

“Wayethi ngizohlala ekhaya ngenzeni?” 

“Wayethi sewukhule ngokwanele manje.” 

“Okusho ukuthini lokho?” 

“Oyihlo laba baye bathathe wonke amawongowongo 

abawezwa ematshwaleni. Phela kule ndawo intombazane ithi 
ingahlosa amabele nje bese becabanga izinkomo.” 

“Izinkomo zani mama?” 

“Ukugana!”

 Ahleke uDumazile. Wabe esethatha ethi, “Pho wamguqula 
kanjani kulowo mqondo ma?” 

“Ngavele ngabhoka ngakhahlela, ngathi mina anginayo nje 
ingane ezolindela umendo incane kangaka! Ngamtshela ukuthi 
umendo omuhle kufanele uyifice ingane ibe ifunda. Wabe 
eseyathamba-ke, wavuma ukuba uqhubeke nesikole. Kodwa yena 
wayefuna ukuba uyofunda eMzamo eXobho. Wayethi uyohlala 
kwababekazi wakho.” 

“Egqilazana kanje ngomsebenzi ubabekazi ma!” 

“Yingakho nje ngenqaba kuyihlo mntanami.” 

“Wenza kahle ma!” 

“Ngenza kahleni njengoba ungasaqedanga nje eMbumbulu? 

Ngiyazisa! Angizukulala-ke namhlanje ngiqula amacala, uyihlo 
esina ngethambo lakho!” 

Kuthuleke isikhashana, bese kuzwakala uMaNdovela ethi, 


“Thatha nantiya ipuleti uziphakele imithanjana kabhatata 
ebhodweni.” 

“Ngisuthi kabi ma! Wukuthi kade ngizigcingca ngamagwinya 
ebhasini!” 

“Woshi bo! Bewuwathathephi?” 

“Bengiwathenge ngasemakethe komunye u-anti obewadayisa. 
Ngiwadle kakhulu ngacishe ngayokoza. Manje inhliziyo imnyama.” 

“Washo ngabona khona mntanami ukuthi usuthi.” Lwamuthi 
heqe uvalo uDumazile. Wahleka inhlinini. Wacabanga ukuthi 
kufanele asibophisise isisu ukuze singabonakali ukuthi sesiqala 
ukuba sikhulu. Babe sebezixoxela nezinye izindaba kwaze 
kwashaya isikhathi sokuba baye kolala.

 UMaNdovela wamfica umyeni wakhe engakazumeki. 
Kwakubonakala nje bo ukuthi uThukela lugola izintethe. 

“MaNdovela, ngangivele ngiyibonile mina le nto ukuthi ingane 
idweba umhlaba nje, ishiya izikole lapha endaweni, iyozifaka 
obishini. Awubheke manje akusafundwa koMbumbulu. Ukube 
nangilalela MaNdovela, ngabe ayikho yonke le nto. Wukuthi 
nina bantu besifazane nibuswa yingqondo yokuthi thina bantu 
botshwala asazi lutho. Nx, demiyu!” Asho maqede abheke 
ngasodongeni. Inkukhu yanqunywa umlomo kuMaNdovela. 
Kwathi ngesikade wangena engutsheni, walala.

 Ngakusasa ekuseni uMaNdovela wavuka maqede waqonda 
ekhishini ukuyophemba umlilo. Kwathi angaqeda, wabeka amanzi 
etiye. UDumazile akavukanga kwaze kwaphuma inhlamvu 
yelanga. Unina wabe eseqonda endlini yakhe, wangqongqoza, 
wangena. 

“Hawu mntanami, kanti usuzolala ilanga lize lingene 
entazingeni yini? Hhayi, hhayi hhayi bo!” Avuse ikhanda 
uDumazile, bese ezama ukuvuka kodwa kubonakale nje ukuthi 


akaphilile kahle. 

“Yini, kwenzenjani mntanami?” 

“Ubonani mama?” 

”Watshoda nje?” Ahlekele phansi uDumazile. 

“Mntanami ngeke phela, uyagula wena. Inkosi, uyagula 
ngempela. Kuzofanele uye kudokotela edolobheni. Vuka, vuka bo 
ulunge ngikukhaphe!”Asho uMaNdovela avule isicabha, aphume 
eseyobikela umyeni wakhe. Wathi angangena endlini, wathatha 
wathi: 

“Yise kaDumazile, umntwana sengathi akaphilile neze. 
Ngisamyisa kudokotela edolobheni eMzimkhulu.” 

“Akaphilile unani?” 

“Angazi yise kaDumazile. Ngimbona entshwamile nje. 
Ngiyabona ukuthi uhabule lolu bhubhane lomkhuhlane oluthe 
chithi saka kulo lonke leli laseMzimkhulu. Kuthiwa lo mkhuhlane 
ukhona futhi naseThekwini. Kusobala-ke ukuthi ukhona kuyo 
yonke indawo.” 

“O...!” Aqhubeke nokucambalala uNozulu. UMaNdovela 
alungise ingubo yakhe yokugqoka, agqoke. Abheke imadlana, 
ayithole maqede ayithathe ayishwatheke esikhwameni. Kwathi 
angaqeda konke, wamemeza uDumazile ukuba bahambe. 
Nempela kwaba njalo. Balushaya phansi baze bayongena 
edolobheni. Indawo lena yayingekude kakhulu, kwakuhambeka 
ngezinyawo. 

Ngenkathi befika kwadokotela, uDumazile 
wayengasayithandi indaba. Wayephefumulela phezulu ngenxa 
yesifociya ayezikinatele ngaso esiswini. Ingubo ayeyigqokile 
ngaphezulu yayenza ukuba ingabonisi ukuthi isisu sinomkhuba 
phakathi. Wangena kudokotela. Umhlengikazi wamthatha igazi. 
Kwathi angaqeda, wabatshela ukuthi basazolinda-ke isikhashana 
ngoba imiphumela yegazi ithatha isikhathi eside ukuphuma. 


Lahanjiswa-ke igazi ukuyohlolwa. UMaNdovela wabona kungcono 
ukuba baphumele phandle bayoshaywa ngumoya. Sekuthi-ke 
ebona omunye umame edayisa inyama ‘yewangu’ ngentengo 
ephansi, wayithenga, wayidla. Akuthathanga sikhathi esingakanani 
eyidlile, samphendukela isisu. Waphuthuma endlini encane. 

Kungale nkathi-ke lapho uDumazile wasale wabizwa khona 
ukuba angene endlini kudokotela. Wagibela embhedeni, 
udokotela wamhlola. Kwathi angaqeda, watshela umhlengikazi 
ukuthi uDumazile uphethwe yini. Umhlengikazi watolika-ke: 

“Uthi udokotela ukhulelwe, izinyanga zinhlanu. Uthi futhi 
uphelelwe yigazi emzimbeni. Ngakho-ke kufanele udle isibindi 
kanye nesipinashi.” Udokotela wabe esemjova. Wamnikeza 
umuthi namaphilisi. Ngenhlanhla enkulu isikhwama semali sasisale 
kuye uDumazile. Watomula imali leyo eyayifunwe ngudokotela, 
wakhokha. Waphumela phandle-ke ukuyolindela unina 
owayesahujwa yisisu. 

Kwathi ngesikade,waphuma. UMaNdovela wafisa ukungena 
kudokotela ukuze ezwe umphumela wokugula kwendodakazi 
yakhe. Umhlengikazi wamchazela ukuthi udokotela usematasatasa 
ushanguza umuntu olunywe yinja ebinamarabi. Naye uMaNdovela 
wabona ukuthi kuzokuba uyaphazamisa. Ngenxa yokuyethemba 
indodakazi yakhe uMaNdovela, wazitshela ukuthi useyozwa ngayo 
konke okushiwo ngudokotela. Bangena indlela ebheke ekhaya. 
Besasuka nje, uMaNdovela wabe esebuza ethi: 

“Uthe uphethwe yini udokotela mntanami?” 

“Mama, akazange asho udokotela ukuthi ngiphethwe yini. 
Into akhale ngayo kakhulu uthe ngiphelelwe yigazi emzimbeni. 
Ungijovile, wanginikeza namaphilisi. Uthathe iphepha elibomvu. 

Uthe kufanele ngidle isibindi kanye nesipinashi zonke izinsuku.” 

“Uthe isibindi uyosithathaphi?” 

“Angazi ma.” 


“Khona singatholakala isibindi, uthi kodwa uyihlo angayivuma 
le ndaba yokuba isibindi sidliwe nguwena wedwa? Angiboni.” 
Ahleke uDumazile. 

“Okwesipinishi khona kulula. Ngiye ngizwe kuthiwa siyefana 
nje nemifino. Ngaleyo ndlela singavele sikhe imbuya noqadolo 
laphayana ngasesibayeni. Futhi intshungu yiningi kabi ngalena 
eqeleni.” Babe sebezixoxela nezinye izindaba baze bafika ekhaya.

 Izinyawo zikaDumazile zabe sezivuvukele sekungamagqikolo 
nje. Wayesehamba ebathazela njengekewu. Uyise wathi nhla, 
wayesephendukela ngakuMaNdovela, wathatha wathi: 

“Umeqo phela lo! Awubuzwa nakubuzwa, umeqo ngempela 
lona! Uma singathathi izinyathelo ezisheshayo, igazi sizolibona 
seliza ngamakhala khona manje nje. Ngiwazi kahle umeqo. Bake 
bangigadla ngalona abathi wusinga. Babethi bayangisusa. Nokho 
oZombe, oMvelo benoTholwayo abavumanga.” 

“Konje yise kaDumazile waze wasizwa yini?” 

“Ngasizwa wugedla lolu lwakwaNtombela. Uyayazi ngempela 
imithi uGubeshe.” 

“Sukumani-ke nihambe naye umntwana.” UDumazile wabe 
esezikhalela ngokuthi izinyawo zakhe azisavumi ukuba ahambe. 
Wabika ukuthi umjovo umcobe kabi. Kwabe sekuhamba uyise 
yedwa ukuyofuna amakhathakhathana enyangeni. UDumazile 

wasala nonina ekhaya. 

“Mntanami, uwuthathaphi lo mbhulelo ongaka?” 

“Angazi mama! Mhlawumbe ngawubekelwa ngezinye izingane 

esikoleni. Bese zingizonda kabi!” 

“Zikuzondelani mntanami?” 

“Zingizondela isikhundla mama. Awazi wena ukuthi 
zazisigaqele kanjani isikhundla engangisiphethe esikoleni. 
Kwakuyimina kuphela ezinganeni owayenelungelo lokuyokhuluma 
nothishomkhulu ehhovisi.” 


“Kanti kufanele mntanami ukuba zikuzonde. Ehhene kufanele. 
Noyihlo njengoba umuzwa ekhala ngomeqo nje uwazi kahle. 
Bamgadla ngawo ngenkathi eyinduna emsebenzini. Yena-ke 
wayezwana kakhulu nomlungu wakwabo. Abantu babethi 
uyincethencethe yomlungu. Wena bese uyingede kathishomkhulu 
yini?”

 Ahleke kancane uDumazile. 

“Bengingeyona.Kodwa mama bekungemina ngedwa 
ebengigula esikoleni. Ezinye izingane beziquleka, uthishomkhulu 
aziphuthumise ngemoto kudokotela.” 

“Miningi imigilingwane eyenziwa ngabantu lapha emnyango. 
Uma umntwana elula nje, uyihabula kalula leyo mimoya.” 
Dukuduku kwangena uyise esehefuzela. 

“Awu washesha kangaka ukubuya yise kaDumazile, uthi 
umficile nje uGubeshe?” 

“Cha ngimficile. Ngimphuthume ngokumtshela ngenkinga 
engize ngayo. Ube esengenzela masinyane. Nansi-ke insizi 
ozokumhlikihla ngayo ezinhlangeni,” esho elula isandla ezama 
ukunikeza umkakhe. 

“Kanti akazukugcatshwa nguwena yise kaDumazile 

umntwana?” 

“Wake wakuzwaphi ukuthi indoda igcaba umuntu wesifazane?” 

“Hhayi bo! Yilumbo yini? UDumazile ngumuntu wesifazane 

kuwena?” 

“Cha, bengisho nje ngoba nawe ungamgcaba. Khona akulutho 
nje ukugcaba.” 

UDumazile wakhombisa ukwesaba ukugcatshwa nguyise. 
Yingakho-ke nje kwaphoqeka ukuba agcatshwe ngunina. 
Wamqala emaphabeni, weza emaqakaleni, wakhuphuka waya 
nasemadolweni. Kwathi dli igazi ezithweni. Kwathi angaqeda, 


wamgcoba insizi emnyama ezinhlangeni. 

“Angazi-ke MaNdovela, kodwa uGubeshe akawubheki umeqo.” 

“Asethembe yise kaDumazile.” Babe sebeqhubeka nezingxoxo 

befisela indodakazi yabo ukwelulama okusheshayo. 

Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi kwezwakala ukuthi uDumazile 
uyagula, futhi usebuya kudokotela nasenyangeni. Omakhelwane 
bafika ukuzombona. Indaba yokusuka kwakhe eMbumbulu 
ayibange isaphathwa. Into eyayisematheni nje kwakuyikho ukugula 
kwakhe. Nakuba uDumazile wayegula, kodwa wayengalele phansi. 
Kwakuye kwenzeke ukuba atotobe aye emfuleni ukuyohlanza 
izingubo zakhe. 

Ngelinye ilanga oMaJwara benoMaMpukunyoni, omakhelwane 
bakwaKheswa, badlula emfuleni uDumazile ekhumulile egeza 
umzimba. Baqhamuka kabi engalindele neze. Wathuka sebethi 
thushu nje ngemuva kwakhe, wangabe esakwazi ukufihla 
umzimba. Nabo bashaya sengathi ababonanga lutho. Kwathi 
sebebuqamamana nje, baqala ukuzikhininda. 

“We ntombi kaJwara! Wake wawabona kuphi amabele entombi 
eme njengakamame oncelisayo?” 

“Shiya wena okwamabele! Wake wasibona kuphi isisu sentombi 
esimise okwethuna lengane? Ubengenjena phela lo mntwana.” 

“Kodwa uke wazibona izinqe? Bekuyintshoshovela, ungafunga 

ukuthi yindlovu iyosithela.” 

“Ngoba lo mntwana wayedudule nje, zishonephi izinqe?” 

“Uthi kodwa azingenanga esiswini, zasikhukhumalisa njengoba 

sesiyintaba nje?” Bahleke baze bampansane. 

“Awubheke nje, uMaNdovela usebuya kudokotela 
nasenyangeni; wehlulwa wukubona ingane lena ukuthi ikhulelwe. 
Balokhu bethi ingane iphethwe wumbhulelo. Akukho mbhulelo 
lapha, yisisu lesi.” 


“Kwenziwa yini ukuba umuntu angayiboni eyakhe ingane uma 
seyikhulelwe? Ngikhuluma nje uMaNdovela nguyena ozibona 
kuqala izingane zabantu ezikhulelwayo kule ndawo. Okuxakayo 
nokumangalisayo dade wukuthi yena uyahluleka ukubona le 
mbudlubana yakwakhe. Impela kuyiqiniso ukuthi indlu yegagu 
iyanetha.” 

“Induku ishaya imviki. Sibajwayele abafazi abafana noMaNdovela; 
abafazi abahlala nezingane zabo zikhulelwe zize zizale bengaziboni. 
Umamezala wayefana nse noMaNdovela. Indodakazi yakhe, 
lena eyelama umyeni wami, yabeletha ebusuku kungazi muntu 
ukuthi beyikhulelwe. Wabe eseqamba umzukulu wakhe ngokuthi 
uCashephi, okungukuthi phela besicashe kuphi lesi sisu?” 

“Kodwa ntombi kaJwara, ungeke wakwazi ukuba umlume 
indlebe omunye umfazi?” 

“Ngimqale ngakuphi nje uMaNdovela? Phela ngabe ngiqonde 
ukuzincisha itiye kwakhe.” 

“Abafazi bayavusana kodwa Jwara.” 

“Wothi babevusana. Ungake ulinge namhlanje uthi ingane 
yomuntu ikhulelwe? Angavele ayeke lowo muntu owayenzayo 
adubele kuwena.” 

“Hho…, lafa elihle kakhulu!” 

“MaMpukunyoni, asithule ngoba kuzothiwa sikhininda izindaba 
zabanye nje, ezethu ziyasehlula.” 

“Kunjalo khona Jwara.” Bahamba njalo bezixoxela baze 
bahlukana enhlukanandlela. 

Kuzo lezo zinsuku uMaNdovela wavuka ekuseni waya 
empeshenini ukuyodayisa amahluzo, izicephu, izinkezo, izikhetho 
kanye nezithebe. Wayekuchaye phansi konke lokhu, yena ehlezi 
eduze kwakho. Wezwa esebingelelwa nguMaNyawuse, unina 
kaDayisile. 


“Sawubona we MaNdovela! Awu, siyizwile indaba yakwakho 
ntombi!” 

“Awu yebo! Cha kunjalo khona. Ubambekile yena umntwana. 
Ehhe.” 

“Awu bandla, uthole mntwana muni uDumazile?” Avele 
asangane ukusangana lokhu uMaNdovela. 

“Umntwana obenzenjani?” Bese kuba yima ethuka 
uMaNyawuse ukuthola ukuthi inkulumo yakhe iyashayisana 
nolwazi abanalo abakwaKheswa. 

“Cha MaNdovela, kufike uyise kaDayisile evela eThekwini 
waxoxa ukuthi utshelwe ngabantwana bakwami, laba abebefunda 
nendodakazi yakwakho, ukuthi icishe yabelethela esikoleni. 
Mathishelakazi lawo asizile ngokuba nesibindi ukunqanda isimo!” 

“ Awu Nkulunkulu! Ungilahlelani na? Ngizokuba yini 
nguNozulu?” 

Wathi lacu, waqoqa konke ayekuchaye phansi, wangena 
indlela ngaso leso sikhathi esephikelele ekhaya. Ababehlangana 
naye endleleni uMaNdovela, babengakholwa kahle ukuthi nguye 
lowayana. Wayehambisa okomuntu onomsangano ngempela. 

Wathi efika nje ekhaya uMaNdovela, waqonda ekhishini lapho 
kwakuhlezi khona indodakazi yakhe. Akabange esaphozisa maseko 
kodwa wakhwela wadilika: 

“Awu Dumazile! Ukhulelwe? Awu mntanami, kodwa manyala 
mani lawa owenzayo? Ngizoba yini kuyihlo? Ngitshele, ngizoba 
yini?” Asho akhihle isililo uMaNdovela. Athule uDumazile 
abheke phansi. Kwabe sekubonakala izinyembezi nakuyena 
zigeleza ezihlathini ziyowela ocansini. Aphume uMaNdovela 
eseyohlanganisa uzalo. 

Babuthana ngokuphazima kweso abesimame. Kwafika ngisho 
omakhelwane bezobakhalisa kulesi sehlo. UMaNdovela wabe 
esechaza ukuthi amakhosikazi uwabizeleni. 


“Makhosikazi, kuthiwa ukuzala wukuzelula amathambo, kodwa 
mina angizalanga ngabola amathumbu. UDumazile ungidumazile 
umntanami! Njengoba nimbona nje ubuya nesisu eMbumbulu!” 
Asho akhale uMaNdovela. Wabheka ngasendodakazini yakhe, 
wathi: 

“Dumazile, usithathephi lesi sisu?” Esikhundleni sokuba 
aphendule unina uDumazile, wavele wabathela ngemvula 
yezinyembezi. Kwabe sekuzwakala enye inkosikazi ithi: 

“Udinga ukushaywa phela lona. Uhluleka ukuphendula 
umbuzo olula kangaka, kodwa ebe ekwazi ukwenza into 
ejule kanjena. Ukweyisa phela lokhu. Ngeke thina sidlale le 
nto. Mbambeni makhosikazi simtitinye!” UDumazile wezwa 
elokushaywa, wathula du, wasula nezinyembezi. Wathatha wathi: 

“Nguthisha.” 

“Hawu, ihlazo elingaka! Bewumfunani kodwa uthisha 
mntanami?” Kumangale wonke umuntu endlini. Babuzana ukuthi 
luhlobo luni lukathisha lolo? 

“Uyena lona owangi….” Ahluleke ukuqedela inkulumo 

uDumazile ngenxa yokuxinwa wukukhala. 

“Nguthisha ubani yena lowo?” 

“Nguthisha uMoloi.” 

“Hawu, waze wangilaya uMloyi! Ngizoba yini kuyihlo?” Athule 

uDumazile. Amakhosikazi amphenya isisu namabele. Kwezwakala 
enye ithi: 

“Sesibomvu! Usengayishaya phansi noma nini! Hhawu, 
imikhuba yezingane!” 

UMaNdovela wayibuka indodakazi yakhe seyisiqhunsulile isisu. 
Ngaleli langa uDumazile wayengasibophile isisu njengemihla, 
kodwa wayesidedelile nje. Yingakho-ke nje emihleni kungabanga 
lula kunina ukuba asheshe ambone ukuthi usezithwele. Futhi 
uMaNdovela wayengazitsheli nje ukuthi neyakhe ingane 


seyingaba sesimweni sokukhulelwa ngenxa yokuyethemba. 

“Uhlala kuphi yena lo Mloyi?” 

“Ubehlala ekotishi esikoleni. Ngithe ngishiya kodwa 

ubengasekho lapho.” 

“Ubengasekho eseye kuphi?” 

“Angazi.” Amakhosikazi abukana nje exakekile ukuthi into 

enjena yenziwa njani. 

“Makhosikazi, ake ningiphe ikhambi,” kusho uMaNdovela 
kubonakala nje ukuthi usedidekile. Enye inkosikazi yathatha yathi: 

“Mina ngokubona kwami MaNdovela, bengibona kufanele 
uvuke kusasa ekuseni uqhube uDumazile ayobika isisu lesi. 
Bekungaba kuhle ukuba uhambe nozakwenu uMaMdinsilwa; 

ningamshiyi noMaJwara umakhelwane wakho.” 

Kubonakale ukuthi amakhosikazi ayavumelana. 

“Niqikelele ukuthi aniyi nje ukuyolanda inhlawulo kuphela, 

kodwa nifike nifune namazolo kanye nomgezo wezintombi,” 
kusaqhuba yena umame. 

“Uthi kodwa izifundiswa ziyawazi wona amazolo nemigezo 
yezintombi?” 

“Cha phela Jwara, niyozichazela izifundiswa lezo ukuthi nina 
nivuke ekuseni ngovivi nabhula amazolo niyolanda inhlawulo. 
Kubalulekile-ke ukuba amazolo akhishwe. Nisichazele isifundiswa 
ndini leso ukuthi izintombi zakule ndawo zithukekile, ngakhoke 
kufanele zigezwe.” Amakhosikazi avumelana ngalo mbono. 
OMaNdovela benoMaMdinsilwa kanye noMaJwara bavumelana 
ngokuthi ukusa sekuyobonwa yibo. Bahlakazeka. 

Ngenkathi amakhosikazi ehlakazeka, umnumzane uKheswa 
wayeza nganeno, egcakela eqeleni elingaphesheya kwakwakhe. 
Wawabona amakhosikazi lawa kodwa waxakeka nje ukuthi 
umkakhe usevule umdlalo uFafi yini emzini wakhe! Nakuba 


wayethe ukuthintathinta kancane ezinyembezini zenkosazane, 
kodwa umqondo wakhe wawungaphazamisekile. Wayekubona 
kahle konke okwakwenzeka. Wakhabuzela waze wayofika ekhaya 
kwakhe. 

UMaNdovela wayesanda kungena ekhishini, kade eqeda nje 
ukukhipha amanye amakhosikazi, ngenkathi kungena umyeni 
wakhe. UNozulu wathi efika, engakahlali naphansi, wayethatha 
ethi: 

“MaNdovela, bebezofunani labaya bantu ebebelapha?” Aqale 
athule uMaNdovela engazi ukuthi uzoluqala kanjani lolu daba. 
Wabuye wacabanga ngokushesha ukuthi ukuthula ngeke kwamsiza 
ngalutho, wabe esethi: 

“Ngicela uhlale phansi Nozulu ngikuchazele.” Nempela 
umnumzane uKheswa wathatha isigqiki sakhe wahlala phansi 
ngasensikeni. 

“Yise kaDumazile, wozakwethu kanye nomakhelwane laba 
abebekade belapha.” Athi ukuthula kancane uMaNdovela. 
Umnumzane uKheswa aqhwaye ilahle eziko, bese okhela inqawe 
yakhe. Ayidonse kabili kathathu bese ethi: 

“Ngilalele.” Avele asikhihle isililo uMaNdovela. UDumazile 
waphuma ephaphatheka naye endlini yakhe, waqonda ekhishini 
efuna ukubona ukuthi unina uhayiza nje ngakube udliwa yini. 
Wathi gagaga wazithela kuyise. Akabange esaphozisa maseko 
umnumzane uKheswa kodwa wathatha wathi, “Dumazile, 
kwenzenjani kunyoko?” NoDumazile futhi wenza lokho okwabe 
kwenziwa ngunina, naye wasikhihla. Umnumzane uKheswa 
waxakeka nje ukuthi kwenzenjani emzini wakhe. Waphumela 
phandle esafuna ukuyobuza kwamakhelwane wakhe ukuthi bona 
abanalo yini ulwazi ngale nsambatheka yakwakhe. 

UMaJwara wayesesizwile isililo esabe siqhuma phezulu 
kwaKheswa. Waphuma ngokushesha kwakhe ukuyokuzwa ukuthi 
ngakube uDumazile usale wavelelwa yini? Wathi ethi thushu 


ebaleni, wahlangabezana nomnumzane uKheswa. 

“Yini Nozulu, kwenzenjani makhelwane?” kubuza uMaJwara 
ngokwethuka okukhulu. 

“Nami bengithi ngizobuza kwakho ukuthi awunalo yini ulwazi 
lokuthi kwenzekeni kwami. Ngithe ngithi ngiyabuza kuMaNdovela 
ukuthi leya nkumbula yabantu ebeyilapha kwami beyizofunani, 
wavele wangithela ngemvula yezinyembezi. Ngithe noma ngithi 
ngiyabuza endodakazini yami, nayo futhi kwayileso, yangithela 
ngazo.” 

“Cha makhelwane, yehlisa umoya Nozulu. Ehhene, yehlisa 
umoya bandla ngiyakuncenga.” Athele phansi umzimba 
umnumzane uKheswa, alalele. Athi ukuthula kancane uMaJwara 
esacabanga ukuthi uzoyiqala kanjani indaba yabantu uma bona 
ibakhalisa. Wabe esethatha ethi: 

“Indodakazi yakho ikhulelwe. Kusasa siyovuka ngovivi 
siphelekezele uMaNdovela ukuyiqhuba ukuyolanda inhlawulo 
eMbumbulu.” 

Kwathi xhifi, kwathi fithithi enhliziyweni kamnumzane 
uKheswa. Wezwakala esebhovumula ethi: “Umithi, unondindwa?” 
Aphimise amathe phansi uKheswa ukukhombisa ukuthi 
uyasenyanya isenzo sendodakazi yakhe. Kwathi akadumele induku 
aqonde kubona bobabili afike ababhambabule ngayo, kodwa 
wabuye wacabanga ngomonakalo ongase wenzeke. Usakhumbula 
kahle ngelinye ilanga eshaya umkakhe maqede waquleka waze 
waphaphama esibhedlela. Wazwakala esethi: 

“Uze utshele uMaNdovela ukuthi ngithe akolibamba lingashoni. 
Angidlali mina. Kungakuhle basale sebeqhubana baqhubekele 
phambili. Angibafuni nokubabona kulona kababa umuzi.” 
Washingila, wadlwathizela eseqonde endlini yabo yokulala. Wathi 
efika nje wayevula isicabha, wangena. Akazange ayikhumule 
i-ovaloni ayeyigqokile, kodwa wangena nayo engutsheni. Inhliziyo 
yayibila kuthi ayiphume ngomlomo. 


UMaNdovela benendodakazi yakhe babesalokhu bekhala 
ngenkathi kungena uMaJwara ekhishini. Wazama ukubathulisa, 
wabanxusa ukuba bayolala kwakhe. Wababonisa ingozi eyayingase 
ibehlele uma belala lapha ekhaya kwakhe uMaNdovela. Baqoqa 
masinyane izingubo zokugqoka kanye nokunye ababeyokudinga 
phambili. Ngenhlanhla enkulu imali yayisemshuqulweni ekhanda 
kuMaNdovela. Baphuma belandelana sebeya kwaMaJwara. 

Balala bengalele ebusuku bethatha bebeka. UMaNdovela 
wayecabanga ngomyeni wakhe, abuye acabange ngoMloyi. 
Wasiqalekisa isikhathi ayekuso. Wafisa sengathi ngabe uDumazile 
akazalwanga. Wayesezibona eyinhlekisa kwamanye amakhosikazi 
nasemphakathini jikelele. Amakhosikazi angazalanga wona 
ayeseqalile ukutshikida ngokuthi ukuzala nokungazali kuyefana 
nje. Wayethi uma eyihlanganisa yonke le micabango, kuvele 
kuthi akazibulale. Kwaze kwathi phakathi kobusuku wezwa 
isithongwane sithi lelele, zaya amasolokohlo. 

Kwathi ngesikhathi sokukhala kwezinkukhu zesithathu, bavuka, 
bageza, bagqoka. Baphuma-ke ukuyolindela ibhasi esitobhini. 
Ngaleso sikhathi ikhwezi lase liphezulu. Akuthathanga sikhathi 
eside laqhamuka ibhasi. Lathi lingama, basho phakathi. Lasuka 
seliphikelele eThekwini lapho babezothola khona amathekisi 
ahambela eMbumbulu. 


ISAHLUKO SESITHATHU 

Kwathi kungena isikole ekuseni, oMaNdovela base befikile 
eZenzele High School eMbumbulu. Uthishanhloko wabangenisa 
ehhovisi lakhe, wayesebatshela ukuba balinde kancane ngoba 
yena wayesaya kothandazisa abafundi. Nempela bangena ehhovisi. 
Bahlala phansi, balinda. 

Uthisha uMoloi wazidlulisa ngasehhovisi likathishanhloko 
ngenkathi eya emthandazweni ehholo. Wayekade embonile 
uDumazile eyongena ehhovisi, kodwa wayengabazi labayo mame 
ayehamba nabo. Wabona kuyisu elihle ukuba azidlulise ngakhona 
ukuze ababukisise kahle. Wathi nhla phakathi ehhovisi, wathola 
ukuthi kanti nabo bagqolozele ngasemnyango. Wabheka eceleni 
njalo, wenza sengathi kukhona umuntu ombizayo ngakulelo cala. 
Kwathi angaqeda ukudlula uthisha, kwezwakala uDumazile esethi: 

“Nguyena-ke lowayana.” 

UMaNdovela wathi lacu, wathi nakanjani uyamlandela. 
Kwasiza uMaJwara owamdonsa ngelokwe wamhlalisa phansi. 
“Kahle MaNdovela bo! Kahle mfazi kaKheswa! Uyabona 

ukuthi uzosishayanisa nabantu bakule ndawo? Yihlazo phela leli 
osufuna ukulenza manje! Asilindele uthishomkhulu kube nguyena 
ozosixhumanisa nalesi sigebengu.” 

“Sengathi nalo thishomkhulu wenza kancane thumashi. 
Yini nje ayihlalele laphayana nezingane?” esho uMaNdovela 
engasacasukile umshuqulo sewutshekile ekhanda; ejuluka bume 


kungathi uphethwe yisifo ihayihayi. Wabuye waqhuba futhi 
wathi: 

“Niyothini uma uthishomkhulu esesifihlile lesi sigebengu 
sakhe?” 

“Siyomangalela yena phela thina. Yinja yakhe lena edle 
amaqanda,” kusho uMaMdinsilwa. 

“Kahleni bo bakithi! Uthishomkhulu akahlangene nakancane 
nemikhuba eyenziwe yilo thisha wakwaMloyi. Thina okufanele 
sikwenze wukuba sifune abazali bakhe ukuze sikhulume nabo,” 
kusho uMaJwara. 

Kwabe sekuzwakala umculo wabafundi ehholo. Babelokhu 
beshintshanisa amaculo. 

UDumazile waphatheka kabi ukubona ukuthi wayengaseyona 
ingxenye yalabo bafundi. Kwathi ngesikhathi beqala iculo 
elalivame ukuqalwa nguyena, wavele wachiphiza izinyembezi. 

“Yehheni bo! Unani lona osevukwa wumunyu? 
Wawusiyekelani isikole uma kanti wawusasithanda? Ngiyabuza?” 
kusho uMaNdovela efile wukucikeka. Kwathi bangaqeda 
abafundi ukucula, bathandaza. Uthishanhloko wabeka izeluleko 
ezinohlonze kubafundi, wenza nezimemezelo. Baphuma ehholo, 
baqonda ezindlini zabo zokufundela. Othisha balandela nabo 
ukuyofundisa abafundi. 

Uthishanhloko yena waphuthuma ehhovisi lapho ayekade 
eshiye khona abazali belindile. 

“Asibange sisabingelelana kahle. Sanibonani!” 

“Yebo sawubona!” Besho kanyekanye. 

“Mina nginguMzobe, uthishomkhulu waso lesi sikole.” 

“Thina singabakwaKheswa eMzimkhulu.” 

“Awu, oNozulu ngabantu abangenza umuntu! Ngathatha 
khona kwaKheswa!” Asho uthishanhloko asukume abambe 


ithambo, ahlale phansi endaweni yakhe. 

“Wathatha kwaKheswa kuyiphi indawo?” 

“EMgwenya, ngaphansi kwentaba iNgilanyoni. Niyayazi leyo 

ndawo?” 

“Cha! Ikuphi yona iNgilayenyoni?” 

“IseMid-Illovo.” 

“Nayo iMidilova leyo siyizwa ngendaba. Siyathokoza-ke 
mkhwenyana,” kusaqhuba yena uMaJwara. 

UMaNdovela yena wayebukeka engungununu nje. 
Ukubingelelana lokhu wayekubuka njengento engenamsebenzi 
walutho; into echitha isikhathi. Wayesejahe kabi ukuba 
kungenwe odabeni. 

“Pho ekuseni kangaka nisihlasele ngani kodwa?” 
uthishanhloko ebuza ibhasi libhaliwe. Wayembona kahle phela 
uDumazile ukuthi nguyena lona ayesanda kumxosha esikoleni. 
UMaJwara wahlala amagqoza odabeni. 

“Thishomkhulu, silethe lo mntwana ukuba azokhomba uthisha 
owammekezayo. Ngenhlanhla enkulu umntwana usesikhombisile 
yena lowo thisha. Udlule wathi pheshe phambi komnyango 
lapha.” Aqale adideke uthishanhloko ukuzwa ukuthi kanti 
umkhuba usekhaya. UMaNdovela wabe eseyiqala ukusuka 
nokuhlala indaba. Uthishanhloko wayelalele, ebukeka edangele. 
Kwathi angaqeda ukuchaza uMaNdovela, uthishanhloko 

wathatha wathi: 

“Ngubani yena lo thisha owenze amanyala anjena?” 

Kwaphendula uMaJwara ngoba uMaNdovela wayesasula 

izinyembezi ezase zigcwele amehlo. 

“Bathi ngubani, bathi nguMloloyi!” 

“O, cishe nguthisha uMoloi! Eyi uyangihlupha lo thisha! 

Ngikhuluma nani nje uyafika, kade enyamalele izinyanga ezimbili 


zonke. Bengisathi ngizombizela umhlangano womkhandlu 
owengamele isikole ukuba bamyale. Akukapholi maseko, nakhu 
nani seniyafika futhi. Angazi ukuthi yinto engizoyithini lena. 
Angazi impela.” Asho aze anikine ikhanda, achaye nezandla. 
Kubonakale ukuthi uyahlupha ngempela lo thisha. Aqhube athi: 

“Ake nginibizele yena ukuze azoziphendulela.” Asho 
asukume uthishanhloko, abuke oqwembeni olulenga odongeni 
lapho kunohla khona oluhleliwe lokulandelana kokungena 
kothisha ukuyofundisa emakilasini. Wathola ukuthi uthisha 
uMoloi kwakufanele ukuba abe sekilasini okwakufundela kulo 
uDumazile. Waphuma maqede waqonda khona. 

Ngenkathi engena ekilasini uthishanhloko, akazange amfice 
uthisha uMoloi. Wathi uma ebuza kubafundi ukuthi ukuphi 
uthisha, bathi abamazi futhi bathi akazange angene ekilasini 
labo. Waphuma engena emakilasini uthishanhloko, kodwa lutho 
ukutholakala uthisha uMoloi. Kwathi noma ebuza kwabanye 
othisha ukuthi abazange yini bona bambone, nabo balandule 
impela. Kwahlulekwa ngisho sekuyobhekwa ekotishi, kodwa do 
ukutholakala. Kwathi ngesikade isikhathi kwaqhamuka umfundi 
owayesanda kufika nje wathi umbonile uthisha uMoloi egibela 
ithekisi elibheke eSiphingo. Kwazimuka ikhanda kuthishanhloko. 

“Mh, useshaye wachitha ebalekela la mahlazo akhe! Ayikho 
kodwa impunga yehlathi.” 

UThishanhloko wabuyela ehhovisi lakhe ukuyobikela abazali 
bakaDumazile ngalesi simanga. 

“Indaba ithi ingaba nkulu ingazekeki! Uthisha uMoloi 
akasabonwa nangalukhalo. Sengimbheke yonke indawo kodwa 
lutho ukumthola. Kuyacaca ukuthi igazi limtshelile, washaya 
utshani.” 

“Awu Nkulunkulu wami, bengivele ngishilo kodwa! Uyabonake 
MaJwara? Akasekho lo muntu!” 

“Yehlisa umoya MaNdovela. Yehlisa umoya mfazi kaKheswa. 


Uyabona manje akusafuneki ukuba sixhamazele. Kufanele ukuba 
lolu daba siyolwethula emaphoyiseni ukuze siboshwe isigebengu 
lesi.” UMaNdovela naye abone ngaso linye noMaJwara. 
Akabanga esachitha sikhathi, wathatha wathi: 


“Thishomkhulu, sizithola siphoqekile ukuba siyobika 
emaphoyiseni. Ayikho futhi enye indlela. Sukumani sihambeni 
makhosikazi!” Asho maqede bathi lacu. 

Kuthe sebeyophuma ngomnyango, kwezwakala uMaJwara 
ethi: 

“Ikuphi yona ishantshi-hhovisi kule ndawo?” 

“Yithani nginikhombise.” UThishanhloko esho esukuma. 
Waphumela phandle, wakhomba ngomunwe wathi: 

“Niyawubona lowaya mgwaqo osithela kuleliya cholo? 
Niyohamba ngawo njalo nize nithole impambanamgwaqo 
ngalena. Niyothatha umgwaqo wangakwesokudla, nihambe 
ngawo njalo. Kuyothi uma seniphambili impela, niyolubona 
uphawu lwasemaphoyiseni, bese niyangena.” 

“Siyabonga!” Bangena indlela. 

Aholobha-ke amakhosikazi ngomgwaqo. Wawulokhu 
ubabizile nje notalagu lulokhu luthi ngibambeni phela. 

“Unonya kodwa lo mkhwenyawenu MaNdovela. Usengaze 
asidedele sihambe phansi indlela ende kangaka!” kusho 
uMaJwara. 

“Awungiyeke wena ngalowo. Mina ngibona befana nje 
noMloyi.” 

“Akanabo ngempela ubuntu. Bekufanele asithi shwi nje 
ngemoto. Yinde kabi phela le ndlela ngezinyawo!” UDumazile 
wayengasathandi lutho, esebathazela kuhle kwekewu. 

“Hawu, nantuya uphawu lwasemaphoyiseni! Sesifikile!” 
Sekusho uMaMdinsilwa. 


Dukuduku bafika. 

“Sanibonani bomama!” kubingelela iphoyisa ngomoya omuhle nje. 

“Yebo sawubona mntanami!” kuvuma uMaNdovela ngomoya 

okhathazekile. 

“Omama singathi bakhala ngani?” 

“Mntanami, sizobopha uthisha uMloyi ofundisa eZenzele. 

Uyazenzela nje ezinganeni zethu. Wakhulelisa umntwana wami 
lo.” UMaNdovela esho ekhomba indodakazi yakhe. 

“Ineminyaka emingaki indodakazi yakho le?” 

“Iminyaka cishe yevile emashumini amathi.” UMaNdovela 
emisa iminwe emibili. 

“Ngakube mhlawumbe uthisha wayibamba ngenkani yini 
indodakazi yakho we mama?” 

UMaNdovela aphendukele ngasendodakazini yakhe, wathatha 
wathi: 

“Phendula wena!” esho ngokufutheka. UDumazile wanikina 
ikhanda ukukhombisa ukuthi akabanjwanga ngenkani. 

“Senike nambikela uthishomkhulu waseZenzele?” 

“Sivela kuyena sikhuluma nawe nje.” 

“Utheni yena?” 

“Naye uvele waxakeka nje ukuthi le ndaba uzoyenza njani. 
Yingakho nje sibone kufanele ukuba size kwabomthetho.” 

“Lalela-ke we mama. Sengathi sizokuba nenkinga lapha. 
Uthisha akazange ayibambe ngenkani indodakazi yakho. 
Ngaleyo ndlela asikwazi ukumbeka icala lokudlwengula. Thina 
bantu bomthetho asingeni ezindabeni zabantu abathandanayo 
uma konke abakwenzayo bekwenza ngesihle, ngothando 
nangokuvumelana bebambisene. Thina singena uma sekukhona 
ingxabano, umbango kumbe ukungavumelani ngokuthile. 


Ngasohlangothini lwethu thina njengamaphoyisa, akukakabi 
bikho okusidingayo kulolu daba.” 

Abukane amakhosikazi engaqondi kahle ukuthi umngqayi 
uthini. Iphoyisa libone ukuthi omama laba badidekile, bese 
liqhuba lithi: 

“Uma wena mama ukholelwa wukuthi uthisha kufanele 
aboshwe, ngiyakuvumela nami, kodwa nendodakazi yakho 
ngokunjalo kufanele iboshwe.”Wahlahla amehlo okwenkomo 
izohlatshwa uMaNdovela. 

“Cha phela we mama, uthisha kanye nendodakazi yakho 
banephutha elifanayo. Laba bantu bobabili abaphulanga nje 
umthetho wakuleli zwe kuphela, kodwa baphule omunye 
wemithetho emikhulu eyashaywa yiNkosi yamakhosi kuMose. 
Yingakho-ke nje kufanele baboshwe ngendlela efanayo. Thina 
asisebenzi ngomthetho obukhali nganxanye njengomthetho 
wasezweni limbe lapho owesifazane ezithola ebhekana nobunzima 
bokukhandwa ngamatshe aze afe uma nje ezithola ekhulelwa 
engashadile ngoba kuthiwa uphingile, kodwa ube ungezwa lutho 
olushiwoyo kumbe olwenziwayo kowesilisa obekade ebambisene 
naye ekuphingeni. Thina-ke bomthetho sithi kufanele baboshwe 
bobabili njengokuvumelana nokubambisana kwabo ukuya ocansini 
baze bakhiqize umuntu bengashadile.” 

“Hhayi kanti mntanami, awume siyoluthathisela kuyise 
womntwana lolu daba.” Baphuma belandelana. 

Kwathi sebesemgwaqweni omkhulu, babonisana. 

“Cha MaJwara, bengibona ukuthi nina ninoMaMdinsilwa 
gibelani nigoduke. Ehhe. Mina noDumazile sizodlula 
kwaMpanza, lapho kade ehlala khona, ukuyothatha izimpahla 
ezasalayo. Mhlawumbe siyogoduka kusasa.” 

“Kuyiqiniso khona MaNdovela, yiqiniso lelo. Ngeke silokhu 
sihlezi sonke lapha singasenzi lutho; kanti nakho nje ukuhlala 
lapha kuyizindleko.” Akuphelanga sikhathi esingakanani bemile, 


laqhamuka ithekisi, basho phakathi. Labathatha lashosholoza nabo 
njalo laze layobalahla eThekwini lapho babezothola khona ibhasi 
elihambela kwelakubo eMzimkhulu. UMaNdovela benendodakazi 
yakhe bewusa umgwaqo njalo baze bafika kwaMpanza. 

UDumazile waphathwa ngamahloni ngenkathi befika 
kwaMpanza. Wayengazange abatshele iqiniso ngenkathi 
ehamba lapha. Nokho wazithola ephoqekile ukuba abazise 
abakwaMpanza ngonina. Nabo bandla bajabula kakhulu 
ukubona unina kaDumazile. Bafisa ngisho nokubeka amazwana 
ngoDumazile. 

“Nathi besihlezi kahle nendodakazi yakho. Beyingeve 
ihlonipha! Sayitshela ifika nje lapha ukuthi umthetho wethu 
asibafuni abafana abazolokhu begcalugcaluza phakathi komuzi 
wethu. Nokho bandla wasihlonipha umntwana. Wayeze 
azithele hulukuqu nje ngezimpelasonto ntambama aze abuye 
ngoMsombuluko ekuseni. Nalapho futhi wayefika yedwa 
engalandelwa mpukane; azithathele izincwadi zakhe aqonde 
esikoleni. Impela singofakazi bokuthi wayengabalethi lapha 
abafana.” 

UDumazile wayengasazi nje ukuthi uzoyinqamula kanjani le 
nkulumo, eseswele umgodi wokucasha. UMaNdovela wayilandake 
indaba. Bathuka kabi abakwaMpanza ukuzwa ngesimo 
esingesihle sikaDumazile. Bamduduza. 

“Sekwajika kwaba yifashini nje ukukhulelwa 
kwamantombazane. Intombazane engakaze ikhulelwe yona, iye 
izibone sengathi ayizali. Kudingeka sikwamukele lokho njengoba 
kunjalo. Kuzofanela uma esekhululekile uDumazile, alushiye 
kuwena usana aphindele esikoleni. Maningi kabi amantombazane 
angamagqinkehli ezikoleni, kuzokube kungaqali ngengane yakho.” 

“Wu…, sengibona ntombi kaNdovela! Ngenzeni, ngiphathe 
usana? Sesayeka thina ukuthola abantwana sinoyise kaDumazile. 
Ngakho-ke akekho omunye umntwana oyophinde agonwe yilezi 


ezami izandla.” Bahleke abakwaMpanza, bese bezixoxela nezinye 
izindaba. 

Ngenkathi uthishanhloko waseZenzele High School esele 
esikoleni, wabona kufanele ukuba ahlanganise othisha ukuze 
abazise ngodaba lukathisha uMoloi. Wabanxusa ukuba 
bahlanganele ehhovisi lakhe ngesikhathi senhlabakhefu yokugcina 
yosuku. Nempela kwaba njalo. Kwathi bangagcwala ehhovisi 
lakhe, wavala isicabha, wathatha wathi: 

“Mathishela, nizongixolela impela ngokuba nginithathele 
isikhathi senu sokuphumula. Ngiyazi ukuthi yisikhathi senu sokudla 
lesi, kodwa ngibona kubalulekile ukuba sihlanganise amakhanda 
sibhunge.” Kuthule kuthi cwaka ehhovisi. Othisha babexakekile 
nje ukuthi kwenzenjani uthishanhloko wababizela emhlanganweni 
ophuthumayo ongenaluhlelo lwezinto okuzokhulunywa ngazo. 

“Ngiyathemba ukuthi niwabonile amakhosikazi amathathu 
abelapha ehhovisi lami ekuseni ehamba nentombazane.” Bavume 
othisha. 

“Lawo makhosikazi abeqhuba umfundi walapha osesiyekile 
isikole ngenxa yokuganga komunye wozakwenu. Umfundi lowo 
uthi wakhuleliswa nguthisha uMoloi. Ngenxa yokungatholakali 
kwakhe uthisha ukuba aziphendulele, omame laba sebeze 
baphoqeka ukuyobika kwabomthetho. Ngakube ukhona phakathi 
kwenu obenolwazi lokuthandana kukathisha uMoloi nomfundi?” 
UMemu Mpungose waphakamisa isandla.UThishanhloko 
wamgunyaza ukuba akhulume. 

“Thishomkhulu, besinalo ulwazi lokuthandana kukathisha 
uMoloi noDumazile. Ngiyathemba ukuthi uthishomkhulu 
uzokhumbula ngenkathi sifika lapha ehhovisi sinoMisi Hlophe 
sihamba naye uDumazile.” Avume uthishanhloko. 

“Thishomkhulu, asithandanga thina ukugeqa amagula 
singemuki. Esabona kubalulekile nje kwakuwukuzinquma 
amakhanda sizishiye. Ukungena shi ezindabeni zabantu 


thishomkhulu kuyahlupha. Ugcina nawe sekuthiwa fakaza

mikhuba. Lokho-ke kuyinto ebucayi kabi futhi nengathandeki 
ukufakaza ngayo. Kwakungelula-ke ukuba kube yithina esasizosho 
ukuthi nguMoloi owakhulelisa uDumazile. Ngiyabonga.” 

Wathula kancane uthishomkhulu. Wathatha wathi: 

“Nokho ngiyabonga bothisha ngokuqaphela kwenu nakwazi 
ukubona izambane elibolile esakeni. Ngiyathemba ukuthi nami 
ngathatha isinqumo esifanele sokuba ngilikhiphe izambane

sami sakoMzobe, kodwa kwakuyisinqumo esathathwa ngabazali 
behlangene emhlanganweni ngonyaka odlulile. Amaminithi 
alowo mhlangano nginawo akhona. Isinqumo sabazali 
ngisihlonipha kakhulu. Lesi sinqumo bafinyelela kusona kunzima 
kakhulu, isikole sisehlazweni elinyanyisayo. Ngiyathemba 
nisakhumbula bothisha ukuthi kwakwenzekeni.” Bavume othisha. 
UThishanhloko waqhuba wathi: 

“Ngithanda ukuninika izwi eliyisexwayiso bothisha. Uma 
abazali belethe izingane zabo lapha esikoleni, basuke bezilethele 
ukuba zizoqeqeshwa ngokwemfundo, hhayi imikhuba. Thina 
singabazali lapha esikoleni. Akukhathaleki noma ubukeka 
uyingane kangakanani ngenxa yokushesha kwakho ukungena 
esikoleni, iqiniso wukuthi wumi endaweni yomzali. Yiba 
ngumzali-ke thisha. Umzali wangempela uyayinakelela futhi 
ayithande ingane yakhe. Uyithanda ngothando lobuzali. 
Uyayikhulisa, ayikhombise indlela enhle ebheke ebudaleni.” 

Athi ukuthula kancane uthishanhloko esafuna ukubona ukuthi 
le nto ayishoyo iyayithola yini indawo. Kubonakale abanye 
othisha besilisa begwajaza sakukhophoza. Aqhubeke futhi 
uthishanhloko: 

“Umphakathi ulindele ukuba senze umsebenzi wokufundisa 
abantwana babo ukuze babe ngabaholi abaqotho bakusasa. 


Thina kufanele siziphathe kahle, sibe yisibonelo esihle kubantwana. 
Uthisha uMoloi akakwazanga ukusimela kahle njengothisha 
esikoleni. Mina, njengothishanhloko wakulesi sikole, ngiyaphoqeka 
ukuba lolu daba ngilubikele amalungu omkhandlu owengamele 
isikole. Sekuyiwona-ke ayokhipha umhlahlandlela. Ngiyabonga, 
seningakhululeka.” Basukuma othisha, baphumela phandle. 

Ngakusasa ekuseni uMaNdovela wavuka waphikelela

Babingelelana, baphilelana. UMaNdovela wake wangabaza

wabuye wabona kufanele ukuba axoxe ngoba uthishanhloko 
wayeyogcina ebuzile. 

“Nathi sifikile emaphoyiseni izolo. Ngingathi nje sihambe 
kahle.” 

“Awu, kube kuhle-ke.” Sekwenanela uthishanhloko. 

“Bese ngithi-ke angizobheka ukuthi ubengakabuyi yini 
uthisha?” Aqale axakeke nje uthishanhloko ukuthi uma udaba 
selusezandleni zabomthetho, pho usadingeka ngani yena

“Ubengakafiki. Futhi angithembi ukuthi uzosheshe abuye

abafundi bahlezi dengwane. Kwamina lo sengiyaphoqeka ukuba 
ngimthathele izinyathelo ezinqala. Yisizwe lesi asibulalayo. 
Ngikhuluma nje amalungu ekomiti asefikile ukuzobhunga ngalo 
thisha. Ngiyathemba ukuthi isinqumo esizothathwa ngesokuba

UMaNdovela wathi ephuma ehhovisi, wayeselindelwe

uMaNdovela, izingane zathi: 

“Uthe umama asizokulanda. Uthe ubophuthuma ngoba 


uDumazile uyapaquza ekhaya.” UMaNdovela wafunda 
kwezakhe ukuthi kwenzenjani. Wakhabuzela ewusa umgwaqo

UDumazile wayesenqaphaza ngekhanda wena owabona 
imamba ibhajwe kwesingezansi odakeni. Amakhosikazi 
ayezimisele ukuwenza wonke umsebenzi wabahlengikazi. 
Ekugcineni kwatholakala ukuthi ayingangawo, umsebenzi udinga 
ochwepheshe abawufundelayo. Babe sebeqasha isigeqevana 
seveni lakwamakhelwane ukuba limphuthumise esibhedlela 
eMshiyeni. Ngokuphazima kweso labe selifikile. Wehliswa, 
waphuthunyiswa egunjini labantu abanjalo. 

UMaNdovela akaphindelanga emuva neveni, kodwa wahlala 
emabhentshini asesibhedlela elindele ukubona isiphetho. Wahlala 
kwaze kwaba yisekuseni. Kwathi sekuzokusa kwafika umhlengikazi 
ezomtshela ukuthi indodakazi yakhe seyikhululekile. Wachaza 
ukuthi ihlinziwe ngoba isimo besisibi kakhulu, umntwana ubemilile. 

“Kodwa nesi mntanami, angeke wangivumela ukuba

“Ngeke ngakuvumela mama, uxole. Usewodini labantu 
abagula kakhulu, akekho neze esimweni sokuba angabonwa. 
Udokotela uthe kufanele anikezwe ithuba elanele lokuphumula 
ngoba umqondo awukabuyi kahle.” Lumshaye kakhulu uvalo

“Cha nesi mntanami, nami ngingumfazi nje, noma ngakube

“Mama, ngeke ngikwazi ukuphula isinqumo nomthetho 
kadokotela. Phela ngabe sengifuna ukuzixoshisa lapha 
esibhedlela.” 

“Uthole mntwana muni kodwa umntanami?” 

“Intombi.” 


“Awu Nkulunkulu onamandla, uyingcwele Simakade!

sengilinda khona lapha emabhentshini kuze kuse.” Umhlengikazi

Ngokuhamba kosuku uMaNdovela wavunyelwa ukuba 
ayobona indodakazi yakhe. Wayifica iwubhaca embhedeni, 
ingakwazi ngisho ukunyakaza. Yayithi uma ikhwehlela nje kube 
sengathi kuthunukala umzimba wonke. Ukukhuluma kukodwa

“NguLerato.” 

“Hawu! Useqanjwe negama? Uliqanjwe ngubani?” 

“Habe, kanti akananina yini? Uliqanjwe ngunina.” Lwamuthi

“Lisho ukuthini lona leli gama?” 

“Igama layo uyolizwa kahle hle ngonina wayo. Sithe uma 
simbuza ukuthi lisho ukuthini, wathi lisho uthando. Ngamanye 


amazwi igama lomzukulu wakho uNoluthando noma uNontando

UMaNdovela wafikelwa yizinyembezi, wakhala. Umhlengikazi

“Hawu mntanami, kanti bekufanele ukuba uhlinzwe!

“Kwakuyigama likadadewabo kathisha.” Amoyizele

UMaNdovela wagibela ithekisi kulawa ahambela eSiphingo. 
Lafika ngokuphazima kweso eSiphingo, wehla. Wagibela ithekisi

“Wayethukuthele kakhulu yini?” kubuza inkosikazi kaMpanza. 


“Kwakungekhona ukuthukuthela komuntu lokhuya, 
kwakuyisimanga!”

ngithi hulukuqu ngiyobheka uyise kaDumazile.”

“Elokugcina lisuka ngofayifi ntambama.”

 Babuka iwashi elalilenga odongeni, babona ukuthi ngeke

UDumazile wahlala isonto lonke elele esibhedlela. Wathi

UMaNdovela benendodakazi yakhe babonisana besesendleleni 


ukuba bafikele kwaMaJwara. Babesaba ukumane bathwale

“Cha MaNdovela, nathi sasenziwa wukuxakeka nje ukuthi

ngivele ngisobishini.”

manje kuyena?”

“Ngilalele.” 

“Isiphetho-ke kuvunyelwane ngokuthi uyise kaDumazile 
avuke ngomhlomunye ayonibheka eMbumbulu. Ubezohamba 
nomyeni kaMaMdinsilwa, bese mina ngibaphelezela. Kodwa 
MaNdovela, okwakobani nje ukuziphekela uyindoda?” 

Kwabe sekukhala usana lukaDumazile, baphazamiseka. 
Wakhipha ibele uDumazile waluncelisa. 

“Sesilibele wukucevuza izindaba. Ngumuntu muni bantu?” 

“Intombi,” sekusho uDumazile. 

“Kwakuhle bandla!” UMaJwara wathatha isikhwama sakhe, 
wakhipha amarandi amabili wakhunga usana. 

“Ngiyambongela bo uzakwethu,” sekusho uMaNdovela. 

“MaNdovela, sukumani ntombi nginikhaphe! Ehhe, 


keniyofudumeza umuzi ekhaya.” Basukuma. Bathatha izimpahla 
zabo, baphuma sebebheke kwakhe. 

Ngenkathi oMaNdovela bengena ebaleni, uBahlekile 
weyezihlalele nje nezinye izingane. Kwathi ukuba abone unina, 
weqa amagqanqu ephikelele kuyena. Wasondela maqede 
wabambelela kuyena, wasikhihla isililo. Nonina wabonakala 
esesula izinyembezi emehlweni. Umntwana wayesephelelwe 
yithemba lokuthi unina wayesayophinde abuye. Kwase kudume 
ukuthi uKheswa wabaxosha benoDumazile. Izinyembezi nomunyu 
kwaphenduka intokozo nenjabulo. Bangena endlini, babeka 
phansi izimpahla zabo. Baqala ukudludluzisa izimbiza. UMaJwara 
waphindela kwakhe. 

UKheswa waqhamuka ezinkalweni kungakahwalali evela 
ematshwaleni. Wahlangatshezwa nguBahlekile ngesikhulu isivinini 
lesi. Wathi efika nje wayebambelela kuyena, ezikhuhla ngaye, 
wayesethi: 

“Umama benosisi sebefikile ekhaya.” Kwabonakala uyise 
ethuka kodwa wangaphendula. Wayenqena ukuphawula ngoba 
wayecabanga ukuthi ingane iyamkhohlisa. Bahamba ngokushesha, 
uBahlekile elokhu egxumagxuma ngaphambi kukayise sengathi 
udlala umdlalo umagalopha. UKheswa wayehamba ecabanga: 

“Ngoba kungase kwenzeke ngempela nje madoda ukuthi 
uMaNdovela ukhona ekhaya? Ngizovele ngingabe ngisasho lutho. 
Ehhe, okwakobani nje ukuba yimpohlo?” Bahamba njalo oBahlekile 
noyise baze bafika ekhaya. 

UKheswa wangena ekhishini, wadonsa isigqiki sakhe, wahlala 
phansi. 

“Awu, senibuyile MaNdovela?” 

“Yebo!” esholo phansi. 

“Khona bese ngizwile ngendodakazi ukuthi senifikile. Hhayi-ke 
siyabonga.” UKheswa wabe esecela umkakhe ukuba baye koxoxela 


endlini yabo yokulala. Lwamuthi heqe uvalo uMaNdovela, 
wacabanga: 

“Mhlawumbe le ndoda seyifuna ukuyongiqoba amaphisisi 
nje, kwazi bani?”Wayengaqondi kahle ukuthi umyeni wakhe 
wayekusho ngomoya okhululekile yini lokho. Nokho wama 
isibindi, wamlandela baze bayongena endlini. Kwathi bangahlala 
phansi, uKheswa wathatha wathi: 

Nathi lapha MaNdovela besihlangene izolo. Sibonisene 
siwuzalo ukuthi kufanele ngikulande eMbumbulu. Wukuthi nje 
kwasuke kweqa amazwi nkosikazi ngenxa yentukuthelo.” Athule 
kancane uMaNdovela ebheke phansi. Kuthi ngesikade bese ethi: 

“Ngiyezwa yise kaDumazile. Ngiyabonga uma usuwahoxisile 
amazwi akho. Ngiyabonga Nozulu.”

 UMaNdovela wamlandisa-ke umyeni wakhe ngohambo 
lwaseMbumbulu. Nakuba kwakubuhlungu nokho, kodwa indoda 
yayisibhodlile. 

“Ngubani igama lomntwana?” 

“Batheni konje onesi? O, bathe nguntasika nguLilatho.” 

“Uliqanjwe ngubani umntwana leli gama?” 

“Uliqanjwe nguDumazile. Ugange kabi yena, usekwazi 

ukuqamba ingane naye ebe eyingane!” 
“Lolu hlobo lwegama alwandile lapha ezansi. Ungumhlobo 

muni yena uthisha?” 

“Sengathi ungumSuthu. Ehhe.” 

“O, kusho ukuthi yilaba bakaMshweshwe! Cisho impela. 
Hhayi-ke akulutho phela ngoba nabo ngabantu. Umzukulu 
sengiyomkhunga kusasa.” 

Bathi ukuxoxaxoxa nezinye izindaba. Bathi bangaqeda, 
uMaNdovela wabuyela ekhishini lapho kwakuhlezi khona 
uDumazile. Wamxoxela-ke ukuthi bebexoxani noyise. UDumazile 


wajabula kakhulu ukuzwa ukuthi uyise wayengasabathukuthelele. 
Balungisa ukudla, badla, bahlukana yilowo nayilowo 
eseyozishwatheka egunjini lakhe. Ngakusasa ekuseni, uMaNdovela 
esathi uvula isicabha nje, thushu uMaKheswa evela eXobho. 

“Hawu MaNdovela! Sewubuyile mfazi womfowethu?” 

“Yebo!” esholo phansi ngenxa yamahloni. 

“Ubuye naye uDumazile?” 

“Yebo!” 

“Uphi yena umfowethu?” 

“Usacambalele. Ake ngiyombiza.” 

Asuke angene ekamelweni uMaNdovela bese etshela umyeni 
wakhe ukuthi udingwa ngudadewabo phandle. UMaNdovela 
wabe eseya kovula ekhishini, waphemba umlilo. UKheswa wathi 
ephuma nje endlini, wazithela kudadewabo phandle. 

“Hawu mnta kababa, uJehova unamandla! UMaNdovela 
usebuyile? Ngiyathokoza kakhulu mfowethu. Bese ngibona nje 
umuzi uvalwe thaqa sengathi kufiwe!” Bahamba bexoxa baze 
bayongena ekhishini. UKheswa wadonsa isigqiki sakhe wahlala 
phansi. Udadewabo yena wahlala ocansini esininini sawomame. 
Wathatha wathi: 

“Siyabonga MaNdovela! Siyabonga mfazi womfowethu! 
Awu siyabonga! Bavimbile oSombazwana, oNgenetsheni 
benoQhosheyiphethe. Awu siyabonga!” UMaNdovela wayelokhu 
ethule ebheke phansi. Wabe esesukuma, wathela amanzi 
eketeleni, walibeka eziko. UMaKheswa wabheka ngakumfowabo: 

“Kodwa mina mfowethu ngisola uMaJwara kulolu daba. 
Nguyena lona ocishe wahlakaza umuzi wakho. Yonke imizi 
kuyaxatshanwa, kodwa kubuye kuxolelwane. Uma wena 
wawukhulunyiswa wukuthukuthela, sasingekho nesincane 
isidingo sokuba yena athathe ukuthukuthela kwakho ayokuthi nzi 
kuMaNdovela.” 


Anqekuzise ikhanda uKheswa ekhombisa ukuthi uyahambisana 
nenkulumo kadadewabo. UMaKheswa wabe eseqondana ngqo 
noMaNdovela: 

“Mfazi womfowethu, uboqaphela ngokuzayo. UMaJwara 
ubefuna ukunixabanisa ninoMjanyelwa.” 

“Ngangizothini phela mina uma uMaJwara engitshela ukuthi 
uyise kaDumazile usengilolele imbazo yokungigenca?” 

“Yena wagencwa ngubani ngenkathi eyakhe ingane ibuya nesisu 
ekolishi? Ubefuna ukuba nihlukane ninoMjanyelwa, bese yena 
enzani? Awumboni kodwa MaNdovela ukuthi lo mfazi uyinyoka? 
Uma ungakamboni, asazi! Abahlakaniphile kodwa bathi utshani 
obulele buvuswa ngomlilo.” UMaNdovela waqala naye manje 
ukumbona ngelinye iso uMaJwara, wafikelwa wukungamethembi. 
UMaKheswa walanda-ke ukuthi wayevuke ekuseni kangaka nje 
kwakwenzenjani. 

“Nami bengithi ngizokwenzela umfowethu umphako njengoba 
bebezokuba nohambo lokuyolanda wena MaNdovela kusasa. 
Kuthe uma sekuqediwe ukuxoxa emhlanganweni, kwathiwa 
uMaJwara nguyena ozokwenzela umfowethu umphako. Ngibhoke 
ngakhahlela, ngathi ngeke owakwethu umntwana enzelwe 
nguMaJwara. Igomondela alifukuthe?”Wabe esezikhipha-ke 
izimpahla ayeziphethe ezokwenzela ngazo umfowabo umphako. 
Kwakukhona nesiteki senyama. Wathatha wathi: 

“Sala usushisela umfowethu le nyama MaNdovela ngoba 
uhambo alusekho.” Nempela uMaNdovela wenza njalo. 

Kwabe sekungena uDumazile egone usana lwakhe. 
UMaKheswa walula izandla, uDumazile wamnikeza umntwana. 

“Hawu, kwaze kwakuhle bantu! Insizwa, intombi?” esho 
ekwanga. 

“Intombi,” kusho uDumazile. UMaKheswa wabe 
esephendukela ngakumfowabo: 


“Mfowethu, kuzofanela usale usuhamba khona kusasa 
ukuyolanda isephulo sakho kusashisa nje. Abafowethu 
abebezokuphelekezela kufanele basale sebeyokulandisa inkomo 
yakho. Ehhe Nozulu.” UMaNdovela wabe esexoxa ngobunzima 
obukhona kule ndaba kaDumazile. Athi dedelele uMaKheswa. 
UDumazile wasukuma wenza itiye. Kwathi angaqeda, 
wabanikeza baphuza. Wathatha ingane yakhe kuyisekazi. 

“Woza kumama wakho wena muntu-muntu kama!” esho 
eteketisa. 

“Uma umntwana esethe dlwe kancane, ubokuza 
uzozibambela itoho esitolo sakwami.” Ahleke kancane 
uDumazile, akhumbule futhi ukuthi konje uyisekazi wayekade 
efisile nakuqala ukuba ayohlala kwakhe. 

Kwathi ukuba aqede ukuthwithwa itiye uMaKheswa, 
wasukuma, wavalelisa, waphuma. UKheswa wamkhapha 
udadewabo waze wambeka ngaphandle kwegceke. OMaNdovela 
basala bexoxa benoDumazile. 

“Uyamuzwa-ke futhi uyihlokazi esethi ubofika uzozibambela 
itoho esitolo sakwakhe? Uthini wena kulokho?” 

“Angazi mama. Ngizobona uma uLerato esekhulakhulile.” 
Asho uDumazile kuze kubonakale nje ukuthi useyakucabanga 
ukuya kotohoza. 


ISAHLUKO SESINE 

Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi umntwana kaDumazile 
wayengasakwazi ukusuthiswa wubisi lukanina. Kwase kufanele 
amthengele ukudla kwabantwana ukuze adle asuthe. Nezingubo 
zokugqoka zazingasamlingani, sekufuneka ezinye. Ingane 
yakhe wayeyibona seyihlubule impela. Imikhuhlane yayithe 
chithi saka! Umntwana wakhe wayehlala njalo engaphilile. 
UDumazile wayesedinga imali ethe xaxa ukubhekana nazo 
zonke lezi zindleko. Wabona kufanele ukuba ayofuna umsebenzi 
ukuze akwazi ukubhekana nezidingo zokukhulisa umntwana 
wakhe. Imisebenzi emihle yayingabonwa. Kwakuze kube 
khona imisebenzi yokuxebula amaxolo kawatela emapulazini. 
Kwesinye isikhathi kwakuye kwenzeke ukuba amaNdiya aqashe 
amantombazane okusebenza ezindlini kanye nokusebenza 
ezingadini. UDumazile wayengasakhethe luhlobo lomsebenzi. 
Wayethi inqobo nje uma ewutholile kulungile. 

Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi uDumazile wazijuba wakhuluma 
nonina. 

“Mama, bengicela ukuba ngihambe ngiyobamba itoho ukuze 
ngikwazi ukuthengela umntwana wami izinto azidingayo.” Aqale 
athule nje uMaNdovela esacabanga. Kwathi ngesikade wathatha 
wathi: 

“Mntanami, uthi uyihlo uzovuma kodwa?” 

“Uyongincengela phela mama, ulalise ulimi.” 


“Uthi uyamazi kahle uyihlo wena? Awazi yihlo ngiyakubona. 
Khona-ke uma ekuvumela, ufuna ukuyosebenza kuphi?” 

“Ngingawufuna khona lapha eMzimkhulu mama umsebenzi.” 

“Hawu mntanami! Awufuni ukuyosebenza esitolo 
sikayihlokazi eXobho? Angithi wayaleza kuwena nje ukuthi uma 
uLilatho esekhulakhulile ubofika uzozitohozela esitolo sakwakhe. 
Awusafuni?” UMaNdovela esho ngoba ebona ukuthi indodakazi 
yakhe ayithandisisi kahle ukuya eXobho. 

“Ayi ngeke mama, ubabekazi ugqilazana kabi ngomsebenzi! 
Okwakobani nje ukuvuka ngovivi? Abasebenzi basesitolo baqala 
emasimini bonke ekuseni anduba bayovula esitolo ngehora 
lesikhombisa. Mina mama angiseyena umuntu wokusebenza 
kanzima emasimini. Ngiyathemba ukuthi nawe uyazi ukuthi mina 
sengaba yisikilebha nje.” 

“Uqinisile khona mntanami. Ehhe yiqiniso lelo,” kubeka 
uMaNdovela ekhombisa ukuvumelana nokuzwelana 
nendodakazi yakhe. 

“Uma izulu lizophenduka nje khona, ngizwa ngawo 
umthungo, uqaqamba kabi! Kuye kudingeke ukuba ngigqoke 
izingubo ezifudumalayo, futhi ngihlale endaweni efudumalayo. 
Ubabekazi ngeke akwazi ukungibekezelela kuleso simo. Angavele 
nje athi ngiyazenzisa, yiJuda leliya!” 

UMaNdovela wasibona isidingo sokuba indodakazi yakhe iye 
kofuna umsebenzi kwenye indawo. 

“Sesikhulume saqeda-ke ngokuyofuna umsebenzi mntanami, 
kodwa awukayithi vu indaba yomntwana. Uyosala nobani 
uLilatho?” 

“Bengithi ngizocela wena bandla mama ukuba ungisalele naye 
uzakwenu. Awu bandla ma,” esho ngezwi elipholile elikhombisa 
ukuzehlisa nokuzithoba. 

“Hhayi, hhayi, kade zangiqala izingane zingihlupha! Wena 


futhi wawuhlupha kabi useyingane. Manje sewufuna ngihlushwe 
yingane yakho? Nayo futhi iyofuna ngihlushwe yizingane zayo? 
Ngeke, ngeke!” Ahleke uDumazile ngenkathi unina enikina 
ikhanda. 

“Uthi uyobe usaphila kodwa mama ngezikhathi zezingane 
zoLerato?” 

“Kanti kungenzeka nje ukuthi ngiyobe ngisekhona. Ukufa 
akukhethi. Kudla fumuka kudle silaza. Ngakho-ke ungacabangi 
ukuthi yimina engiyokufa kuqala kunawe mntanami.” 

“Singabonga kuMdali mama uma uhlala uphila uze uphathe 
izingane zoLerato.” 

Kubonakale nje ukuthi bayasilangazelela leso sikhathi. 
UMaNdovela wakhombisa ukuthamba. 

“Cha-ke mntanami, ngingakusalela nozakwethu. Uma 
engihlupha-ke, ngiyomnikeza lo muthi,” esho ekhomba uswazi. 

“Ngizoke ngikhulume noyihlo ngimazise ukuthi sewufuna 
ukuya kosebenza.”Wajabula uDumazile ukuzwa lawo mazwi 
evela kunina. Kwathi ntambama, uMaNdovela walubeka-ke 
udaba kumyeni wakhe. UKheswa wabhoka wakhahlela. 

“MaNdovela, uDumazile ufuna ukuyosebenzelani?” 

“Cha Nozulu, uthi ufuna ukuthengela umntwana wakhe izinto 
zokwembatha. Usehlubule kabi umntwana.” 

“MaNdovela, uDumazile akathathe ibhasi athi hulukuqu 
eMbumbulu ayolanda imali kuthisha. Le ngane inoyise, futhi 
yiseduze kabi lapha eMbumbulu,” kunxapha uKheswa okhela 

inqawe yakhe. 

“Kanti ubezotohoza lapha eduze nje Nozulu.” 

“Umntwana lona asale nobani?” 

“Kanti bengingasala nje naye, ehhe akulutho.” 

Anikine ikhanda uKheswa ekhombisa ukuthi akahambisani 


nombono kaMaNdovela. Kuthi ekugcineni azwakale ethi: 

“MaNdovela, nizokwenza ngendlela enibona ngayo nale 
ndodakazi yakho. Angithi ningabafazi nobabili phakathi kwalo 
muzi?” Ahlaba ephukela lawo mazwi kuMaNdovela. 

“Yise kaDumazile, kodwa wabiza ingane ngomfazi, yenzeni 
kuwena?” 

“Ngiyaxolisa. Yintombi konje?” esho embheke ezinhlamvini 
zamehlo. Acikeke uMaNdovela ukubona ukuthi umyeni 
wakhe uyambhinqa. Asukume, aphumele phandle. UDumazile 

waqonda kunina, wathi: 

“Utheni ubaba ma?” 

“Uyihlo uyanqaba mntanami. Uthi hamba uye kuthisha 

uyolanda imali yokondla umntwana.” 

“Uthi kodwa ubaba uyazi ukuthi uyise kaLerato ihuzu 
elinembobo ekhaleni? Akamazi kahle.” 

“Uyihlo uyaganga. INkosi uyaganga. Akazi nje ukuthi 
wenqabelani, akazi nje.” 

“Mama, ngizovele mina ngihambe ngenkani-ke. Ningashoke 
ukuthi ngiyadelela.” Athanda ukumethusa uMaNdovela lawo 
mazwi avela endodakazini yakhe. Wayeluleka ukuba izinto 
ingazithatheli phezulu. Wayiduduza indodakazi yakhe ukuthi 
usazophinda futhi akhulume nobaba wekhaya. 

Bagcina bevumelene oMaNdovela benendodakazi yakhe 
ukuba iye kofuna umsebenzi esitolo sikamnumzane uSithole. 
Lesi sitolo sasisanda kuvulwa kule ndawo. Umnumzane 
uSithole wayeqhamuka e-Adams Mishini kude buduze 
naseManzimtoti. Wayenesinye futhi isitolo kuleyo ndawo. 
UDumazile waba nenhlanhla yokuba aqashwe. Kwathiwa yena 
uzophatha umntwana kankosikazi kaSithole owayeshaya isisefo. 
Wayezomphekela ukudla, abuye futhi ahlanze namanabukeni 
akhe. Bavumelana ngokuthi uDumazile uzosebenza izinsuku 


eziyisithupha: kusukela ngoMsombuluko kuya eMgqibelweni. 
Bavumelana ngokuba aqale umsebenzi ngomhlomunye. 

Wathi efika ekhaya uDumazile, waxoxela unina ukuthi 
uwutholile umsebenzi. Uyise wayekhona endlini ngenkathi 
ixoxwa le ndaba. Wayeyizwa kahle yonke inkulumo. Nokho 
ulaka lwakhe lwase lwehlile. Naye wezwakala esethi: 

“Cha-ke kanti ndodakazi, kulungile uma uzoya kosebenza 
kuMatshana. Yiseduze futhi lapha. UMatshana lona ubukeka 
engakabi mdala kangako, kodwa cha yindoda emadodeni. 
Wake wasibusisa kabi mzukwane efika okokuqala kule ndawo. 
Wasenzela izoso, sayidla inyama saze sayibeka ingqotho. 
Sehlisa amaqatha ngobubabayo utshwala lobu.” Kuthi cosololo 
kuDumazile. 

“Hhayi-ke ndodakazi usuzokuba nesitoko sokubuya nekhasi 
lomdloti zonke izinsuku ukuze ngicobelele ipipi lami leli.” Esho 
ekhomba ingobela yenqawe yakhe. Ahleke kancane uDumazile, 
bese ethi: 

“Phela baba ngeke ngibe nayo imali yokuthenga ugwayi zonke 
izinsuku.” 

“Cha ndodakazi, bengingasho ukuthi uzowuthenga. Bengithi 
kuyothi uma senishanela ntambama, ucoshe imvithi phansi. 
Ehhe, ndodakazi.” Ahleke kancane uDumazile. 

“Uyavuma nawe Dumazile ukuba uyihlo abheme imvuthu 
ecoshwe phansi?” Kuphendule uyise kuqala.
