“Uzokwenzenjani phela umntanami uma engakaholi?” 
Bazixoxela nezinye izindaba kwaze kwashaya isikhathi sokuya 
kolala. 

Lwashaya-ke usuku lokuba uDumazile aqale emsebenzini. 
Wathi efika nje wanikezwa umntwana ukuba amphathe. 
Kwakungekhona ukulunga komntwana lokhuya, kwakuyimvu. 
Wayehlala ezilalele nje, ekhala ngoba evuswe singakashayi 


isikhathi sakhe sokuvuka. Kwakuye kuthi uma umntwana esalele, 
kuthiwe uDumazile akasize esitolo. Wayevama ukupakisha 
izimpahla emashalofini, asule izintuli emawindini, akale imboza, 
athele uphalafini emabhodleleni bese eshanela phansi njalo 
ngantambama. Washesha ukuwujwayela lo msebenzi wasesitolo. 

Ayikho indawo engenabo abantu bakhona abacabanga 
ukuthi bahlakaniphile kunabanye abantu. Ngobunye ubusuku 
umnumzane uSithole wabamba izigebengu zigqekeza esitolo 
sakhe. Wazamulisa kabili kathathu izulu lezandla, ishoba 
lalala amazolo komunye. Kwathi uma sekubhekisiswa kahle, 
kwatholakala ukuthi omunye walezo zigebengu kwakuyindodana 
yesikhulu sendawo. Umnumzane uSithole akabanga esaba muhle 
emphakathini. Wathola izinsongo nemikhonzo yokumenzakalisa. 
Wabona kufanele ukuba asidayise isitolo sakhe. Sathengwa 
ngumnumzane uGwabinde, umzala kanina kaDumazile owakhile 
naye endaweni. Umnumzane uSithole waphindela kwelakubo 
e-Adams Mishini. 

Ngenkathi uSithole ebuyela kwakhe, wahamba naye 
uDumazile. Nakuba uKheswa wayengathandisisi kahle 
ngendodakazi yakhe, kodwa wagcina evumile ngoba yayizohamba 
nomuntu emethembayo. Kwavunyelwana ngokuthi uDumazile 
uyovakashela ekhaya kubo ngemuva kwezinyanga ezintathu. 

Umuzi kaSithole wawubuqamamana nasesitolo sakhe. 
Kwakuhambeka ngezinyawo. Isitolo sona sasisendaweni ebanzi 
futhi evuleke kahle. Ngemuva kwaso kwakunezindlwana 
ezintathu ezahlukene: ngeyokuphekela ukudla, ngeyokuhlala 
yena uSithole uma evakashelwe ngabanye abalingani 
kwezamabhizinisi kanti enye kwakungeyokuhlala uMthovovo 
Mkhize, iphoyisa elabe liqapha isitolo. 

UDumazile wayengasezokuphatha umntwana, kodwa 
wayesezosebenza esitolo. Ngaphambi kokuba ayoqala umsebenzi 
wosuku, wayevuka ekuseni apheke itiye. Lalithi lingalunga nje, 


anikeze uSithole ukuba aphuze, naye futhi azithelele elakhe. 
UMaNzimande, inkosikazi kaSithole, wayengasahlupheki 
ngokutatazelela umyeni wakhe ekuseni. Lowo msebenzi 
wawusuhlalele uDumazile. Yena wayezilalela nje aze avuke 
seliphakeme ilanga. Wayengasiboni isidingo sokuba avuke 
ekuseni kakhulu ngoba wayengajahe ndawo. Wayehlezi phakathi 
komhlane nembeleko; ehlala nomntwana wakhe ekhaya kanye 
nomzanyana wakhe. Wayeqashe nomsebenzi owayemenzela 
yonke into. Ukudla wayengasakupheki. Ayisaphathwa-ke 
eyokuyokukha amanzi emfuleni, kwakungabakhwekazi labo. 

UDumazile wakhombisa ukukhuthala kanye nekhono 
emsebenzini wakhe. Wayethi uma esesebenza nje, awenzisise 
umsebenzi wakhe futhi abe nesineke nawo. Wayengalandelwa 
ngemuva. Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi, uSithole wabona kufanele 
ukuba uDumazile abe ngomunye wabathengeli esitolo. 
Nakhona lapho futhi wakhombisa ukwethembeka okukhulu. 
Akenzanga njengabanye abasebenzi laba abathatha ngozwani 
kumbe abenzelelayo kubangani babo nasezihlotsheni zabo. 
Ukukhwabanisa imali kumbe impahla esitolo wayekuthatha 
njengehlazo. 

Yingakho-ke uSithole abuye futhi wabona kufanelekile ukuba 
amkhuphulele esikhundleni sokuba ashaye isisefo. Babelekelelana 
nenye intombazane. 

UDumazile wazakhela ugazi. Wayeseyisilomo engaconsi 
phansi kuSithole. Wabuye futhi wamnikeza umsebenzi wokuba 
ngumabhalane wezimpahla ezidinga ukuyothengwa. Wayesehlala 
egaxe ipeni endlebeni. Kwakuthi uma edlula ngaseshalofini, efica 
izimpahla sezikhophekile, aqobele phansi. Uma esezicobelele 
kahle phansi izimpahla ezidinga ukuyothengwa, uSithole wayevele 
athathe iveni bahambe naye uDumazile ukuyothenga. Ekubuyeni 
kwabo nazo izimpahla, uDumazile nguyena owayebhala amanani 
okuthi impahla ngayinye izobiza malini. Uma uSithole engekho 
kumbe ezokuba nohambo oluthile, wayeshiya zonke izihluthulelo 


zasesitolo kuDumazile. Wayesemethembe ngisho ngaphezulu 
komkakhe. 

Ngelinye ilanga uMaNzimande wacela umyeni wakhe ukuba 
amthumelele amaphilisi ezinhlungu. Wayezizwa ephethwe 
kabi yikhanda. Nempela kwaba njalo. USithole wathi efika nje 
esitolo ekuseni, wathumela uLizy, omunye wabasebenzi, ukuba 
aphuthumisele umkakhe amaphilisi ekhaya. Kwathi nya nya nya 
kanti uLizy ufike kwaSithole maqede walibala wukukhininda 
izindaba: 

“We MaNzimande! Ubovuka futhi uvule amehlo. Thina 
bothina nje kade sasibona abafazi bepheshukelwa yimizi yabo.” 
Ilalelisise inkosikazi kaSithole ifuna ukuzwisisa kahle. 

“Nihlobene ngani ninoDumazile?” 

“Asihlobene ngisho nakancane nje. Wukuthi wayesiphathela 
umntwana ngenkathi sisenesitolo eMzimkhulu. Yilokho nje 
kuphela.” 

“Ohho…! Ubobheka-ke ntombi, sengathi kukhona okudla 
amantshontsho emsamo. Impatho enhle kanjeyaya angikaze mina 
ngiyibone! Ngisho nawe ungumfazi wakhe nje uSithole, angikaze 
ngikubone uphethwe kahle ngaloluya hlobo! UDumazile 
phela usungafunga ukuthi nguyena umedemu walapha esitolo. 
Usehlala eqhoqhobele isisefo ntombi! Kwesinye isikhathi baye 
bavalelane ehhovisi noSithole sekubalwa yona phela imali, uzwe 
ubuswebeswebe sebekhulumela phansi. Uma uthi uyangena 
lapho, inkulumo ivele inqamuke. USithole usevamile futhi 
ukuthatha uDumazile bahambe naye usuku lonke bethi bayooda. 
Uma uthi ubuka impahla abafika nayo, umuntu uvele 
angaboni nje kahle. Angisho ukuthi ngithini MaNzimande, kodwa 
ngithi uboqaphela.” 

Ikhanda elalimphethe uMaNzimande laqala phansi. Inhliziyo 
yashaya ngamawala, wajuluka bume. Wagwinya amaphilisi 
ezinhlungu. ULizy wavalelisa, waphuma esephikelele esitolo 


eshiya uMaNzimande owathukuthela kamuva. Kwake kwathi 
akaphikelele khona esitolo kodwa wabuye wazikhuza. Wasala 
ebambelele ezihlathini ecabanga: 

“Nakanjani kuzofanele uDumazile athuthe lapha 
kwami. Angikwazi mina ukuhlala nenyoka endlini, inyoka 
engangingqofoza noma nini! Lutho, ngiwafunge aMaphephethwa 
ehlangene! Ngeke nje!”Wasukuma, wadlwathizela eqonde 
endlini yabo yokulala. Wafika wazitshinga phezu kombhede 
maqede wathi bukululu. 

ULizy wafika esitolo kungasazi muntu. Wayesenesikhathi 
eside kabi ehambile. USithole wayesexakekile nje ukuthi uLizy 
akamficanga yini umkakhe? Khona engamficanga, pho akasabuyi 
ngani? Kwathi ngesikade waqhamuka uLizy ezishayela kancane 
nje. 

“Wahamba ijuba likaNowa nje Lizy sewukhohliwe yini ukuthi 
uyasebenza?” 

“Cha bhuti wukuthi ngimfice uMaNzimande ecambalele. 
Ngibe sengiyamvusa ukuba agwinye amaphilisi. Ube esethi 
angime angenzele itiye.” 

“Ohho…, bewulibele wukuphuzana netiye wakhohlwa 
wumsebenzi?” 

“Ngiyaxolisa bhuti,” esho uLizy esehlanganise izandla 
sengathi uyathandaza. USithole wamtshela ukuba aphuthume 
ukuyolekelela abanye emsebenzini. Nempela kwaba njalo. 
Basebenza-ke kwaze kwashaya intambama, bavala. Bahlukana. 

Bafika-ke oSithole benoDumazile ekhaya. Ulwandle lwabe 
lugubha amagagasi. Imanzi yakhe uSithole yayikhaba kwasantoni 
nje eyifica phansi. Kwakungathi ikhanda likaMaNzimande 
lisangene. Wake wakhahlela umshanelo kwacishe kwawa 
isitofu kuphekiwe. Naye uSithole waxakeka nje ukuthi 
sekwenzenjani phakathi komuzi kaMondise. Kwathi noma ethi 
uzama ukumncokolisa njengemihla, wamane wanyipha nje 


uMaNzimande sengathi udle inhlaba. Nokho-ke indoda yagwinya 
itshe nje kwaze kwashaya isikhathi sokuba kuyiwe kolala. 
Ithumba laze labhoboka ngenkathi sebesezingutsheni ebusuku. 

“Yise kaMpisendlini, angisamfuni uDumazile lapha kwami.” 

Kuthi nya nya isikhashana, kuzwakale uSithole esethi: 

“Ngoba yini MaNzimande?” 

“Angikwazi ukuhlala naye, angikwazi nje! Ngihlale nemamba 

endlini? Awu, ngeke yise kaMpisendlini, ngeke nje!” Isho imanzi 
yakwabo ize inyiphe. 

“Wenzeni?” 

“Ubuza ngoba ungazi ukuthi wenzeni uDumazile yise 
kaMpisendlini? Uzobuye uthi uyadlala. INkosi, uzobuye uthi 
uyadlala. Angisona isilima sakho mina, angisona nje.” 

“Ngithi wenzeni uDumazile?” USithole esho ngokufutheka. 

“Ukuqomile,” kusho uMaNzimande isifuba sesigubhazela. 
Aqale athule uSithole esadla amathambo ekhanda. Wathi 
uyakhuluma, ulimi lwavele lwagcwala umlomo. Kwathi fithithi, 

wathatha wathi: 

“Uyithathaphi le nto oyishoyo MaNzimande?” 

“Izimpahla lezi ezigcwele esitolo ziyakhuluma. Ihhovisi-ke 

lona leli enivalelana kulona lixoxa izimanga zodwa.” 

Wathi ukuthula kancane uMaNzimande esehlisa igwebu. 
USithole wavele waxakeka nje ukuthi umkakhe uyithathaphi 
inkulumo enjena. Kwathi ekugcineni wasola ukuthi ikhona into 
efike yaxoxwa nguLizy kumkakhe ngenkathi emthumele kwakhe 
ekuseni. Kwabe sekuthuleka endlini, ungafunga ukuthi abantu 
sebezumekile kanti phinde. Yilowo nalowo wayequdule umlomo 
nje, kwaze kwathi ngesikade labazuma iqhawe. 

USithole wavuka ekuseni watshela uDumazile ukuba 
angamenzeli itiye njengemihla. Wathi akazenzele yena yedwa. 


Nempela kwaba njalo. UDumazile wasola ukuthi kukhona 
okushaya amanzi. Wathula ecabanga: 

“Izolo sifike uMaNzimande ebila ukubila lokhu. Futhi size saya 
kolala engakhulumisi muntu. Namhlanjena uSithole usevuka uthi 
angingamenzeli itiye. Kudalwa yini lokho? Mhlawumbe indaba 
ingami nje, kwazi bani? Kusho ukuthi beyimvimbezele ubusuku 
bonke imanzi yakhe. Ehhene, akakwazi uSithole ukungaliphuzi 
itiye ekuseni, nokwenza elithanda kangaka!” Ekuqedeni 
kwakhe ukuphuza itiye uDumazile, waphuma endlini, wangena 
emotweni eyayisiduma phandle. Yasuka seyiphikelele esitolo. 

Bafika esitolo oDumazile, uSithole wavula. Abasebenzi 
bangena. Wavula nehhovisi lakhe elingaphakathi esitolo. 
Wangena, wahlala phansi maqede wabiza uLizy, wafika. 

“Lizy, umkami ungixoxele yonke into ofike wayisho kuyena 
izolo. Bewuyithathaphi yonke le nto obewuyisho kuyena?” 
Athuke kuphele ngisho nasozwaneni uLizy. Wavele wasangana 
ukusangana lokhu engazi ukuthi kufanele athini manjena. 
Wayelokhu echobana nezinzipho, uSithole elokhu emgqolozele 
emehlweni. Kwathi ekugcineni wabona ukuthi akekho umasiza, 
kufanele alikhulume njengoba linjalo iqiniso. 

“Mina bhuti bengithi ngiyamncokolisa nje uMaNzimande. 
Eqinisweni bekungamancoko nje, hhayi ngoba bengithi 
mhlawumbe kukhona into ekhona ngempela phakathi kwenu 
ninoDumazile. Bekungamancoko nje.” Asho aze abumbe 
umlomo. USithole engasacikekile inhliziyo sekuthi ayiphume 
ngomlomo. Kwake kwathi akamyabule ngengalo amjikijele 
phandle ngewindi. Wafikelwa ngumcabango wokuba avele 
amxoshe emsebenzini ngaso leso sikhathi. Wabe esethi: 

“Kodwa uyawubona umonakalo osuwenzile ngala mancoko 
akho?” 

“Yebo bhuti!” esho kubonakala nje impela ukuthi unakho 
ukuzisola. 


“Kuzofanela uxolise kuDumazile. Kuyothi uma sewuqedile, 
bese ulanda uMaNzimande ekhaya ukuze lukhulunywe luphele 
lolu daba. Biza uDumazile.” Nempela wenza njalo. 

Kwathi angangena ehhovisi uDumazile, wahlala phansi 
eduze kukaSithole. ULizy yena wangena maqede wathi futhatha 
ngasemnyango wehhovisi. USithole wathatha wathi: 

“Lizy, ake uphinde amazwi akho.” Inhliziyo seyithi du du du 
kuLizy, enamahloni ngisho okukhuluma. Wazithola nokho ukuthi 
uphoqekile ukuba akhulume. 

“Dumazile, ngiyaxolisa kakhulu ngokukhuluma ngegama 
lakho kuMaNzimande izolo. Lokho kukhuluma kwami naye 
kube nomphumela wokuba uMaNzimande akuzonde. Kodwa 
mina Dumazile bengingaqondile neze ukuba nginixabanise 
ninoMaNzimande; bengizincokolela nje kanti uMaNzimande 
usezodinwa ngempela.” UDumazile waqale waxakeka nje engazi 
ukuthi uLizy ukhuluma ngani. 

“Khona ngempela utheni ngegama lami kuMaNzimande?” 

“Ngithe uSithole ukuphathisa okukamedemu wakwakhe lapha 
esitolo. UMaNzimande uyithathe ngamawala leyo nkulumo yami. 
Ucabange ukuthi mina ngithi uSithole uthandana nawe.” 

Avele aqhumuke akhale uDumazile. Wafikelwa ngumcabango 
wokuthi konje futhi nasesikoleni yake yamehlela into enjena 
lapho abhecwa khona ngobubende inyama engayidlanga. 
Abanye abasebenzi bake bathi ukuphazamiseka ngenkathi 
bebona uDumazile ekhala. Ukuthukuthela kwaya ngokuya 
kugqibelana kuSithole. Wazwakala esebhavumula ethi: 

“Lizy, landa uMaNzimande ubuye naye khona manje!” 
Waphuma ehhovisi esenyonyile uLizy, wanyobozela okwenja 
idle amaqanda wayophuma ngomnyango esephikelele emzini 
kaSithole. 

UMaNzimande wayehlezi ekhishini ngenkathi uLizy engena. 


Babingelelana. ULizy kwakungavumi ngisho ukuba akhulume. 
Wathi lapho evula khona umlomo, wathatha wathi: 

“MaNzimande, waze wangingcwaba! Awu, waze 
wangingcwaba ngiphila! Umyeni wakho usengiqulise amacala 
amaningi kabi!” 

“Amacala? Macala mani lawo?” 

“Uthi utshelwe nguwena ukuthi mina ngithe yena uthandana 
noDumazile. Hhawu MaNzimande! Umuntu ngeke akulume 
indlebe! Awuyena neze umuntu wokuvuswa wena!” 

“We Lizy! Lalela lapha: USithole ubemane ekushansa nje! 
Mina angizange ngisho kuyena ukuthi ngizwe ngawe. Ngithe 
mina kuyena yonke into ayenzayo esitolo sengiyayazi. Ngathi 
izimpahla lezi ezigcwele emashalofini ziyakhuluma. Umake 
wena uyizimpahla lezi ezisemashalofini, angazi-ke.” Asho 
maqede umlomo awuthi pheku njengokakotshi. 

“Uthe angizokulanda-ke ukuze lolu daba lukhulunywe luphele 
khona namhlanjena.” 

“Ini? Angizwa? Angilubeki lapho mina! Wena hamba umtshele 
uSithole ukuthi ngithi angizi lapho. Angiyona into yokuganga 
yena mina. Uma yena ecabanga ukuthi mina ngiyithoyisi lakhe, 
klibhi klolo! Lingcono neklolo ngoba liyadliwa!”Yasho imanzi 
yakwabo kwabonakala nje ukuthi ayiyi ngempela lapho. ULizy 
wavalelisa, waphuma esephikelele esitolo. 

Wangena ehhovisi uDumazile esalokhu echiphiza. Kodwa 
kwathi ngokungena kwakhe, kwaya ngokuya ukukhala kukhula 
kwaze kwagcina sekungumhayizo. Abathengi baxakeka nje 
ukuthi isavela kuphi insizwa esaphonsa intombi ngofufunyane 
olunjena? Kwathi noma bethi bayabuza abantu beNkosi kodwa 
bangaphendulwa ngumuntu. USithole wayesefile wukucikeka. 
Wezwakala esethi: 

“Wafika wedwa, uphi uMaNzimande?” 


“Uthe usaxakekile ekhaya okwamanje, kodwa wathi 
singaqhubeka nodaba, yena useyoluzwa ngawe ntambama ukuthi 
luhambe kanjani.”Wanikina ikhanda uSithole, wayesethi: 

“Kusho ukuthi siyoluqula kusasa lolu daba; ngeke luvele luphele 
nje.” USithole wabe esencenga uDumazile ukuba ehlise umoya. 
Kwaya ngokuya igwebu lagcina selehlile, wathula. Baqhubeka-ke 
nomsebenzi. UDumazile wayengafuni kukhuluma namuntu kwaze 
kwashaya isikhathi sokuvala ntambama. Wayephendula lokho nje 
okubuziwe, bese ethula. Ngesikhathi senhlabakhefu yasemini, 
akazange akuthi mbibi ukudla emlonyeni. Bathi bayamnikeza, 
wakuthatha wakumboza, wakubeka eduze kwamabhodwe. 
Kwahlala lapho ukudla kungadliwe muntu kwaze kwashaya 
isikhathi sokuvala esitolo ntambama. Abasebenzi bahlakazeka. 
UDumazile benoSithole bona baya ekhaya kwakhe. 

UDumazile wathi efika nje wayeqonda endlini yakhe yokulala. 
Wavula isicabha, wangena maqede wahlala phezu kombhede. 
Kwathi noma umashayandawonye usubhokile, wazitshela ukuthi 
ngeke akulokothe ukudla kwakaMaNzimande. Wazisonga 
ngengubo yokulala, wabeka phansi uhlangothi njengomuntu 
ocambalalayo. Zwi, laliyane yena egqokile. 

USithole yena wathi engena ekhishini, imanzi yakhe 
yayisimcuphile. Yayingathukuthele yayiqhuma. NoSithole ngapha 
wayengazibekile phansi. Wezwakala esebhavumula ethi: 

“MaNzimande, awuzanga ngani ngikubiza esitolo?” 

“Nx!” kunxapha uMaNzimande. Wathi lacu, waphuma 
waqonda endlini yabo yokulala. Wafika wangena maqede 
wazivalela. Kwake kwathi akasikhiye ngaphakathi isicabha, 
kodwa wabuye wayeka. Wazihlalela kuleyo ndlu kwaze kwashaya 
isikhathi sokulala. 

USithole wagcina ephumile naye ekhishini ukuya endlini 
yokulala. Wathi engena nje uThukela lwabe selugola izintethe. 
Umkakhe wahluleka ukubekezela. Wathatha wathi: 


“Yise kaMpisendlini, ufunelani ukungenza isiphukuphuku 
mina? Bewungibizela ukuzobukisa ngami ezintombini zakho? 
Hhi? Angiyona into yokudlala wena mina.” 

Asho maqede azigubuzele ngengubo. USithole wazikhuza 
sekuthi akamyabule, amsonge kanye nezingubo, amjikijele 
phandle umkakhe. Wacabangela umntwana wakhe ukuthi 
uzosuke abe yintandane kanti usemncane. Wathula isikhashana 
esadla amathambo ekhanda, wangena embhedeni. Kwathi 
ngesikade bafika ubuthongo. Walala zwi kwaze kwasa. 

Ukusa kwabonwa nguye uMaNzimande. Igwebu lemfezi 
lalisalokhu lithe ciki entanyeni kuyena. Wazithola ephoqekile 
ukuba akhiphe ingonyuluka yakhe: 

“Yise kaMpisendlini, vuka uhambise uDumazile. Angisamdingi 
nje lapha kwami. Angisamdingi nje.” Athi ukuthula kancane 
uSithole, bese ethi: 

“Ngimhambise ngimyise kuphi?” 

“Wabuza kimina, awazi yini lapho wamthatha khona?” Isho 
imanzi yakhe ingamnike thuba. Athi ukuthula kancane futhi 
uSithole. UMaNzimande aqhube futhi: 

“Uma ungamhambisi, ngizomhambisa mina. Uzobona 
isimanga! Angibhenywa mina! Angibhenywa nje!” USithole 
wafikelwa wumcabango wokuzisola ukuthi wayechanguzelani 
nalesi similamongo somfazi ongunompempe. 

USithole waphumela phandle, wamemeza uDumazile. Kwathi 
angavela emnyango wendlu yakhe, wamtshela ukuba athathe zonke 
izimpahla zakhe azifake emotweni. Kwathi cosololo kuMaNzimande 
ukubona ukuthi intando yakhe iyenzeka ngempela. UDumazile 
wayifunda ivaliwe, wenza njengoba kuthiwa makenze. Yasuka-ke 
imoto seyiphikelele esitolo. Kuthe besesendleleni, uSithole wathi: 

“UMaNzimande unezimpawana zokungakhululeki 
ngobukhona bakho phakathi komuzi wakhe. Manje ngibona 


kungcono ukuba wena uyohlala kule ndlu yami engemuva 
kwasesitolo.”

 Kumethuse lokho uDumazile. 

“Ungethuki, ukhona uMthovovo oqaphe isitolo. Awuzukuhlala 
wedwa. Nami futhi ngizolokhu ngivela nje ngizonilunguza.” 
Abuye abone uDumazile ukuthi yikhona okungcono ukuyohlala 
esitolo kunokuba ahlale emzini kaMaNzimande. 

Yathi ingafika imoto esitolo, uSithole wanikeza uDumazile 
ukhiye waleyo ndlu ukuba avule afake izimpahla zakhe. 
Nempela kwaba njalo. Wandlala umbhede, wafaka amashidi 
amabhangqubhangqu, wathi bhu isibhalala ngaphezulu. Kwathi 
angaqeda, wavala endlini, waya esitolo ukuyoqala umsebenzi. 


ISAHLUKO SESIHLANU 

UDumazile wacabanga, wacabanga wabona kufanele 
ukuba athi hulukuqu ekhaya eMzimkhulu ukuyobikela abazali 
bakhe ngesigcwagcwa ayesenaso emsebenzini. Wayibeka kahle 
inkulumo kuSithole. Wabika ukuthi uthole umbiko wokuthi 
ingane yakhe iyagula, ngakho-ke ucela ukuyolunguza ekhaya. 
USithole akanqabanga. Ngokwesicelo sikaDumazile, wayezohlala 
ekhaya impelasonto kuphela bese ebuya ngoMsombuluko. 

Ekufikeni kwakhe ekhaya uDumazile, walubeka-ke udaba 
lwakhe kunina. Indaba wayiqala lapho uLizy ekhuluma ngaye 
kuMaNzimande, waze wagcina lapho eba nyamanambana 
khona. UMaNdovela washesha ukuyibona imbangela yenkinga 
yendodakazi yakhe. 

“Ngeyakwabani yona le ntombazane ekugilela lo mhlola 
mntanami?” 

“NgeyakwaMzelemu mama.” 

“Ikuqala ngaphi nje ukuthi wena uthandana noyihlo? Hhawu, 
uSithole emdala kangaka kuthiwe uthandana naye!” 

“Yibhadi lami nje ma. Nakuqala yangehlela le nto esikoleni.” 
Athi ukuthula kancane esacabanga ukuthi kufanele yini amxoxele 
unina inkulumo yoMemu Mpungose benoMemu Ngcamu 
abambheca ngayo. Wafikelwa ngamahloni, wayeka. 

“Uyabona mntanami, kusemhlabeni lapha. Abantu baphatha 
imithi emibi kabi lapha emsebenzini! Imithi iyasetshenziswa 


ngempela ayidlaliswa! Kuyenzeka-ke kodwa ukuthi abanye basuke 
bengaqondile ukuthakatha, basuke beqonde ukuziqinisa nokuthi 
bathandeke kubasi wabo emsebenzini. Uma-ke wena ulula, 
ungasebenzisi makhathakhathana, isigcwagcwa abasuke besikhipha 
siphuma nawe. Lapho unukisa okomzondo qiniso. Akekho umuntu 
obe esathanda ukukhuluma kumbe ukusondela kuwena.” 

“Njengoba mama ngingakaze mina ngiwuphathe umuthi ngalezi 
zami izandla, sekusho ukuthi kufanele ngisebenzise umuthi manjena 
ukuze ngingabi naso isigcwagcwa?” 

Ahleke kancane uMaNdovela. 

“Cha mntanami, akukhona ukuthi uzosebenzisa imithi. Kufanele 
uthole izintwana nje ezincane zokuhlanza igazi. Kufanele ligezeke 
igazi lentombazane. Ehhe mntanami. Kusobala ukuthi wena 
ulula kakhulu. Imimoya uyihabula kalula. Uma ungabhekile, 
uzokulahlekela lo msebenzi wakho.” Kumethuse uDumazile ukuzwa 
indaba yokulahlekelwa ngumsebenzi, wathanda manje ukuthola 

usizo. 

“Zona izintwana eziyizaba zingatholakala kanjani, kuphi?” 

“UMaKhwashube yena uyawazi amakhathakhathana. Ngisho 

namadoda anezinkinga ezithenjini zawo, asizwa nguyena. Unayo 
ngempela imithi yokuzwanisa abantu.” 

“Ngubani lowo MaKhwashube mama?” 

“UmkaGubeshe, ugedla lolu lwakwaNtombela olusanda 
kushona. Awusayikhumbuli inyanga lena uyihlo aya kuyona 
ukuyofuna insizi yomeqo ngenkathi wena usisanganisa uvela 
eMbumbulu nesisu? UMaKhwashube ngumkayo leyo nyanga.” 
Akhumbule uDumazile. 

“Kuzofanela ngisheshe ngibonane naye-ke umama 
uMaKhwashube ngingaze ngiphelelwe ngumsebenzi.” 

“Uma uyihlo efika, ngizomxoxela-ke naye.” 

UDumazile akaphozisanga maseko, waphikelela khona 


kuMaKhwashube. Ngenhlanhla enkulu wamfica ekhona ekhaya. 
Babingelelana, baphilelana. Esezichazile uDumazile ukuthi 
ungubani wakwabani, wayilanda-ke inkinga yakhe emsebenzini. 
Kwathi angaqeda, umame lona wathatha wathi: 

“Kuyacaca ukuthi kukhona umuntu okumele kabi. Ufuna 
uphume uphele emsebenzini. Ehhe, uphume uphele. 
Amathambo ekhanda angitshela lokho. Nokho-ke akukakabi kubi 
kakhulu uma ngizwa uchaza.”Waba nethenjana uDumazile. 

“Angazi-ke noma uzofuna ngikunike izincweba bese 
ungikhokhela, noma ngikwelaphe ngize ngikuphothule anduba 
ngihole inkomo yami?” UDumazile wayengenalo ulwazi 
lokuthi kufanele kwenzeke kanjani. Wacela iseluleko kuyena 
uMaKhwashube. Babonisana kahle, bavumelana ngokuthi 
bazokhokhelana kanjani. Wayilungisa-ke imithi umame 
lona, wayibeka phambi kukaDumazile, emchazela nokuthi 
isetshenziswa kanjani. 

“Awubongwa,” kusho uDumazile ethatha imithi yakhe, 
ephuma. Wahamba njalo waze wafika ekhaya. Wamazisa 
unina ukuthi uhambe kanjani. Waqala-ke ukuyisebenzisa imithi 
njengoba kade etsheliwe. 

UDumazile wayekade ecele izinsuku ezimbili ukuba angabi 
bikho emsebenzini. Yena wathatha amasonto amabili wonke 
esasebenzisa imithi ekhaya. USithole kwamkhathaza kakhulu 
ukunyamalala kukaDumazile emsebenzini. Wake wacabanga 
ngisho ukuyombheka, kodwa wabuye waphazanyiswa 
wukuthi umsebenzi wawuzosala nabantu ayengabathembile 
kahle. UMaNzimande yena wezwa ngabasiki bebunda ukuthi 
uDumazile akasekho emsebenzini. Wajabula kakhulu, wabona 
ukuthi intando yakhe yenzekile. Waqala ukuncibilika. 

Kulezo zinsuku uLizy wabambeka kakhulu wukugula. 
Waphoqeka ukuba awuyeke umsebenzi. Wayephethwe 
yikhanda elaliqaqamba liphume ngamehlo. Kwathi kusenjalo 


wagwazwa yizibhobo zamncisha umoya. Lokhu kwenzeka 
ngesikhathi esifushane impela. Abomndeni bahamba ukuyokuzwa 
kwabanamanga. Kwathiwa uLizy uphethwe ngabangasekho. Bathi 
ugogo wakhe uhlezi kuyena, ufuna ukudla. Babeluleka-ke ukuthi 
uma bengenawo amandla enkomo okwamanje, bangahlaba 
izinkukhu ezingamashumi amabili ukuphuthuma isimo. Nempela 
kwaba njalo. Ukufa kwadlonga kakhulu kunakuqala. Baphindela 
kuyena lowo obonayo. Bachaza ukuthi umsebenzi wezinkukhu 
bawenze kanjani. Wabasola. Wathi abenzanga njengoba 
wayebatshelile. Ngaleyo ndlela umsebenzi wonakalile, kufanele 
baqale phansi. Amandla okubuye kwenziwe omunye umsebenzi 
ayengasekho. Izimali zase ziphelile. ULizy wayesephethwe 
yiphika muva nje, ekhala ngesifuba esibuhlungu kanye nezinyawo 
eziqaqambayo. Umndeni wahlanganisa amakhanda, waphuma 
nesixazululo. ULizy waphuthunyiswa esibhedlela. 

Phakathi nesonto lesithathu, uDumazile wabuyela emsebenzini 
wakhe esitolo. Kwamjabulisa kakhulu uSithole ukubona uDumazile 
esebuyile. Akabange esathanda ukumbuza ipasi nesipesheli. 
Omathand’ezabanye balala sebemtshelile uMaNzimande ukuthi 
uDumazile usebuyelile emsebenzini. Ulwandle lwaqala ukugubha 
amagagasi. 

Ukuba uDumazile wayeyinyoka, bekungathiwa 
wayesebuzile. Isimo sokubukeka komzimba wakhe sase 
siguqukile. Wayeyisibutubutwana esihle ongafunga ukuthi 
yitshitshana eliselincane. Wayesho ngezinwele zakhe ezimnyama 
bhuqe ekhanda. Unwele lwempunzi luthe lungu ebusweni 
obuntothombela. Isho ngamehlo athambe njengawenkehli ibuka 
abasemzini. Kuthi uma iqala inkulumo nje, imoyizele kancane, 
kufacake izihlathi, bese iyakhuluma. Intokazi lena yabe idudule, 
inyathela ngabantwana, kuphambene umnyama ngemuva. 
Wawungaphika ukuthi kwakuyiyona leyayana eyayisimathanjana 
ngenkathi isengumdlezane. 

UDumazile wayesenezesheli eziningi kakhulu kunakuqala. 


Kwakuthi kusa nje ezinye zazo zibe sezime phuhle esangweni 
lasesitolo. Kuthi kungavulwa nje, zingene, zizithengise ugwayi 
nomentshisi. Zazijatshuliswa yikho nje ukuthi zimbonile, zaxoxa 
naye umlomo nomlomo. Kungalesi sikhathi-ke lapho zazicela 
khona ukumbona ngesikhathi senhlabakhefu yasemini. Ezinye 
zazifika ntambama ukuze zimbone eseshayisile emsebenzini. 
Zizodwa ezazishaya ucingo zifuna yena uDumazile. Zaziba 
nenkinga-ke lezo zesheli. Ucingo lwalungena ehhovisi likaSithole 
bese lubanjwa nguyena. Izikhathi eziningi wayengambizeli 
ocingweni uDumazile ukuba akhulume nezesheli. Wayebona 
kuwuphazamisa umsebenzi wakhe lokho. 

Nakuba uSithole wayejabula ngokungena kwemali esitolo 
ngenxa yamaxila kaDumazile, wagcina engasakhululekile kahle 
uma uDumazile eselandelwa yizinsizwa ngaloluya hlobo. Wazama 
isu elithile lokuphazamisa. Kwakuthi uma sekushaya isikhathi 
sokuvala esitolo ntambama, athi kuDumazile abasale naye balungise 
amabhuku ngoba kuzofika abacubunguli bawo bevela emnyangweni 
kahulumeni. Nempela kwakuye kwenzeke njengokusho 
kwakhe uSithole, basale. Izesheli zaqala ukusokola; zakhononda 
ngokuncishwa ithuba nelungelo lokushela ‘entombini’. 

Ngelinye ilanga uSithole wathatha uDumazile wahamba 
naye ukuyothenga izimpahla zasesitolo. Bahamba nje endleleni, 
uSithole uyacabanga: 

“UMaNzimande unesikhwele kufanele. Muhle phela lo 
mntwana! Muhle uqedile! UMaNzimande ucabanga ukuthi 
sesiyathandana. Hhayi suka, akudedwe mani uphondo luvele 
lugcwale amanzi. Mh, kepha ngizomtshela kanjani ukuthi 
ngiyamthanda? Eyi madoda!” USithole wezwa sekubabaza 
uDumazile ebona imoto seyigibela esihluthu. Kwabe sekucaca 
ukuthi ushayela nje kodwa umqondo wakhe awukho 
emgwaqweni. Wayigwebula imoto uSithole maqede wayibuyisela 
khona futhi emgwaqweni. Wayincenga njalo baze bayofika 
eSiphingo. 


“Asiqale singene laphaya esitolo sezingubo.” Nempela kwaba 
njalo. USithole wakhithiza izingubo zikanokusho ethengela 
uDumazile. Wamsusa phansi esicathulweni waze wamkhipha 
phezulu. Wathenga nobucwebecwebe bemigexo namacici 
newashi legolide. Kwathi bangaqeda, badlulela embonini lapho 
bethenga khona izimpahla zasesitolo. Ababange besalibala 
kakhulu lapho, babuyela emuva. 

UDumazile waxakeka nje ukuthi uzobonga athini. Wavele 
wafikelwa wumunyu nezinyembezi. 

“Kanti ungakhali Dumazile. Kusekuningi engisazokwenzela 
kona.” USithole wabona kufanele ukuba ayibeke inkulumo yakhe 
kuDumazile. 

“Manje Dumazile bengifisa ukuba wena ube ngumamncane 
kaMpisendlini.” 

“Hhayi bo! Kodwa athini nje umama kaMpisendlini?” 

“Athini kwani, kanti wena uyohlala phezu kwakhe yini?” 

“Hhayi bo! Bese kugcwaliseka izinsolo zakhe?” 

“Izinsolo zani?” 

“Izinsolo zokuthi siyathandana njengokusho kukaLizy. Angifuni 
neze nje ukuzixabanisa nomkakho.” 

“Ngizokwakha uhlelo lokuba kube nguwena undlunkulu, yena 
ngizoyibona indaba yakhe.” 

“Mina ngiseyingane bantu.” 

“Ikhona ingane enengane? Musa ukuganga wena.” 

“Hhayi bo! Futhi wena umdala kabi kimina! Kungathiwani nje 
ngithandana nomuntu ocishe alingane nobaba wami?” 

“Ukuthandana akudingi sayizi kungesicathulo.” 

“Uyazi bengingalindele neze ukuthi ungakhuluma kanjena!” 
UDumazile athi ukubuka izimpahla zakhe ayezithengelwe 
nguSithole. Nokho wathanda ukujabha ukubona ukuthi 


ubondlozelwa kanjena nje kanti imbuzi igudle iguma. 

Yahamba njalo imoto yaze yayofika esitolo, behla. Izimpahla 
zathulwa emotweni, zangeniswa ezindaweni zazo. Akuthathanga 
sikhathi eside besesitolo, kwashaya isikhathi sokuvala. USithole 
wabona indlela ebheke ekhaya. UDumazile wasala edidekile. 
Wake wathula ecabanga: 

“Yini lena ekhulunywa nguSithole kimina? Ungihlolela bhadi 
lini nje? Yimihlola phela lena. Qiniso! Ngithandane nobaba 
wami? Sekuphele ontanga yami yini?” Athule kancane. 

“Uthi kodwa le nto ayenziwa yimithi kaMaKhwashube? Uthi 
kodwa isimonyo angisisebenzisanga nje kakhulu kwaze kweqa? 
Ngiyasola. Washo uMaKhwashube ukuthi ngingasisebenzisi njalo 
kumbe kakhulu ngoba kuyokwakheka uthando okungelona 
lolu mina ebengiluqondile lokuba ngithandwe ngubasi 
nje ngokomsebenzi. Mh, bakithi! Yinto ezothiwani lena? 
Ngizoluphala kanjani manje lolu thando uSithole asengithanda 
ngalo? Angingabazi ukuthi yisimonyo lesi esidale yonke le 
nyakanyaka. Kusobala-ke ukuthi ngasisebenzisa kakhulu kwaze 
kweqa. Mh…!” 

Kanti uDumazile ubalisa yedwa nje, uSithole-ke yena 
uyabaliselwa: 

“Yise kaMpisendlini! Ngakhipha imamba ekamelweni, wena 
wayithatha wayoyifukamela ekhishini, ukwenzelani lokho?” Aqale 
athule uSithole esacabanga inkulumo yomkakhe. Kuthi ngesikade 

athathe athi: 

“Angikuzwa ukuthi uqonde ukuthini.” 

“Uyezwa! Wena, uzwa kahle! Ngithi wenziwa yini ukuba 

uqhubeke nokuhlalisa uDumazile esitolo ekubeni ngathi kuwena 
angisamdingi yena lapha?” 

“Wena wathi uDumazile awusamfuni emzini wakho. 
Ngangithi ngikuhloniphile kulokho. Ufunani pho manjena?” 


“Yise kaMpisendlini, isitolo kanye nezindlu zaso 
kusengokwakwami. Uma uDumazile esahlezi kwenye yezindlu 
zasesitolo, akuhlukile nokuthi usahlezi phakathi komuzi wami. 
Ngangithi wamsusa njengoba ngangishilo, usubuye wamlanda 
futhi?” 

“Ngangingamhambisanga. Wayevakashele kubo, 
wahlangabezana nezinkinga kwalibaleka-ke.” 

“Awu, uyinuku yise kaMpisendlini! Uyinuku myeni wami! 
Indoda enjena! Phu!” esho uMaNzimande ephimisa amathe 
phansi. Axakeke nje uSithole ukuthi uyinuku uma kwenziwani. 

Yaqhuba futhi imanzi yakhe: 

“Uxova uxove udaka ngezinyawo, usuke lapho uyongena 

emashidini amhlophe qwa ungagezile!” 

“Ukhuluma ngani MaNzimande?” 

“Yise kaMpisendlini, uthi uyazi ukuthi uDumazile, lona 

osumlande kubo ngoba nithandana naye, uthandana nephoyisa 
lasesitolo uMkhize?” 

“Ukuthathaphi lokho?” 

“Yise kaMpisendlini, musa ukuthi ngikuthathaphi lokho. 
Babevele beqhathwe nguwena ngamabomu. Wake wakuzwaphi 
ukuthi igundane lake lahlala ndawonye nekati? Wena ngokwakho 
wawuqondeni ngempela?” 

“Ngithi uzwe ngobani ukuthi bayathandana?” 

“Kusobala ukuthi nguwena wedwa-ke obungakezwa ukuthi 
bayathandana. Mina anginandaba-ke nokuthandana kwabo, 

enginendaba nakho yimpilo yami.” 

“Impilo yakho ihlangene ngani nale nto oyikhulumayo?” 

“Uyabona yise kaMpisendlini, aphelile amadoda eqedwa 
yilabo nonkiloshi abachithiwe ezweni. Nihamba nibhabhabala 
nje lapho kubhabhabala khona oMthovovo. Nizoyithola into 


eniyifunayo. UMthovovo akadiyi ngasiketi; ungathi wagcatshwa 
ngabantu besifazane. Akanandaba namfazi wamuntu yena. 
Uthandana nabo bonke omatapudaka laba.” 

“Ngixhumaphi pho mina kotapo bakhe labo?” 

“Uyaxhuma yise kaMpisendlini. Uyaxhuma nje. Into ozogcina 
uyenzile wukubuya nokufa uzongithelela ngakho. Okungcono 
sizohlukana ngezindlu zokulala. Mina ngizolala ekamelweni 
lami nengane yami. Wena uzozibonela ukuthi uzokwenzenjani. 
Angikwazi ukufa ngibhekile mina ngishiye ingane yami isencane 
kangaka!”

 Athule nje uSithole esacabanga ukuthi uvelelwa yini 
ngempela? Iqhube futhi imanzi yakhe: 

“Ngikunikeza usuku lwakusasa ukuba umhambise uDumazile, 

kungenjalo….” 

“Ake ungenzele inkomishi yetiye.” Kwabe uyinyathele emsileni. 

“Awu! Kwenzenjani wafuna itiye kimina namhlanjena? 
Akakwenzelanga yini uDumazile umfazi wakho?” Kuthi xhifi 
kuSithole. Wathi lacu, waphuma eseqonde endlini yabo yokulala. 
UMaNzimande wasala walenza itiye. Walithatha waliyisa 
kumyeni wakhe ekamelweni. USithole akabange esaliphuza lelo 
tiye ngenxa yokunengwa. Wamane walijamela nje laze laphola. 
UMaNzimande walithatha waphuma nalo, walimbumbuthela 
lonke phansi phandle. Wangena endlini esefile wukucikeka. 

“Yise kaMpisendlini, wenziwa yini uthi angikwenzele 
itiye, kodwa ungabe usaliphuza? Usaphinda usaqhuba le nto 
yakho yokucabanga ukuthi mina ngiyisidwedwe sakho?” Avele 
awuhlabe inhlali owakhe uSithole. 

“Ngikhuluma nawe yise kaMpisendlini, wathula nje ngibe 
ngikhuluma nawe?” 

“MaNzimande, angikufuni ukukhuluma mina.” Asho uSithole 
maqede athule futhi. Wake wacabanga ukuba amsuse uDumazile 


endlini yasesitolo, kodwa inkinga yakhe kwaba wukuthi 
uzokumbeka kuphi? Baqudula imilomo bobabili baze bazunywa 
wubuthongo.

 Ngakusasa ekuseni uSithole wavuka maqede waqonda 
esitolo. Wathi efika nje wafunda iphephandaba langalelo langa 
ayelithenge endleleni lidayiswa. Engosini ethile kwakubhalwe 
uhla lwezindlu ezidayisayo elokishini laseMlazi. Akabanga 
esananaza, wahlala ocingweni: 

“Nkri nkri nkri…, nkri nkri nkri…, nkri nkri nkri…” 

“Ezindlini Ezinhle eMlazi, Hallo!” 

“Hallo! NguSithole lona okhulumayo lapha e-Adams. Angazi 

noma yikhona yini emahhovisi abadayisi bezindlu eMafezini 
eMlazi lapho?” 

“Yikhona ngempela mnumzane wami.” 

“Manje kunendlu eseMafezini evele ephephandabeni 
lanamuhla, angazi noma bese ithengiwe yini?” 

“Awuthi ngibo….!” esho edonsa ibhuku efuna ukuthola ukuthi 
indlu leyo ayikakadayiswa yini. Wathatha wathi: 

“Beyingakadayiselwa muntu. Kodwa ngiyakucebisa nje ukuthi 
uma uyifuna ngempela, phuthuma. Baningi esengibezwile 
bekhuluma ngayo.” 

“Sengifikile.” Asho uSithole aluvale ucingo, aphuthume eMlazi. 

Wathi efika uSithole, waqonda ehhovisi lomphathi. Wangena 
maqede wazichaza: 

“NginguSithole wase-Adams obekade efonile ekuseni 
mayelana nendlu eseMafezini.” 

“Awu sibonene mnumzane Sithole! Mina nginguZikode 
isibongo.” Baxhawulane. 

“Nami ngiyathokoza ukukwazi. Angingabe ngisakuchithela 
isikhathi, angikuxhumanise nomdayisi wendlu kulesiya sigceme.” 


Nempela baphume belandelana sebeya ehhovisi lomdayisi. 
Baxhumana-ke. Basuka sebephikelele kuyona indlu. USithole 
wafike wayibona, wagculiswa yiyona. Baphindela ehhovisi futhi 
ukuyobhalisa imininingwane yokudayiselana indlu. Kwathi 
bangaqeda, bavalelisana, bahlukana. 

Ekubuyeni kwakhe eMlazi uSithole, wangena ehhovisi lakhe, 
wahlala phansi. Wabiza uDumazile. Wafika. 

“Manje Dumazile, ngenxa yokubona ukudlonga kwethuku 
ekhanda kuMaNzimande, ngibone kufanele ukuba ngikushayise 
ngomoya.” Aqale axakeke nje uDumazile. Aqhube futhi uSithole: 

“Ngidlule kuNaidoo eSiphingo ngakukhulumela naye ukuba 
uyosebenza kuyena. Angithi uyambona lona esi-oda kuyena 
izimpahla zasesitolo?” 

“Yebo ngiyambona!” 

“Ehhe ngisho yena-ke. Akazange angihluphe, uvele wathi fika 
kusasa uqale umsebenzi.” Lwamuthi heqe uvalo uDumazile uma 

ecabanga ukuthi usezoya kosebenza eNdiyeni. Wathatha wathi: 

“Indawo yokuhlala ikhona?” 

“Ungakhathazeki ngendawo yokuhlala. Ngizokwenza 
konke okusemandleni ami ukuba uthole indawo ekahle futhi 
ekhululekile.” USithole wakhombisa uDumazile iphephandaba 
elinohla lwezindlu ezidayisayo. 

“Uyayibona lena esesigcemeni sakwa-Z eMafezini?” Esho 
ekhomba ngomunwe ephepheni. UDumazile avume. 

“Iyona-ke engiyithengile. Yinhle kabi! Inamakamelo 
amathathu okulala, yikhishi, yindawo yokudlela, yindawo 
yokuhlala, yizindlu zangasese ezimbili kanye negalaji. 
Uzozihlalela ngokunethezeka kuyona.” 

“Uma esengikhipha futhi kuyona umkakho 
ngiyokwenzenjani?” 


“Uyobe etshelwe ngubani ukuthi sengithenge umuzi eMlazi? 
Lokhu yisifuba sami nawe. Ungake ulokothe utshele noyedwa 
umuntu. Uyezwa?” 

“Yebo ngiyezwa!” UDumazile waba nokukhononda 
ngenhliziyo. Wayekhonondiswa ukuthi indoda ikwazi ukwenza 
into enkulu kangaka kodwa ingamtsheli umkayo! Wasukuma, 
waphuma ehhovisi eseyoqhubeka nomsebenzi.

 Kwathi bangavala esitolo ntambama, uDumazile waya 
endlini yakhe. USithole yena waya ekhaya kwakhe. Wayifica 
imanzi yakhe izihlalele nje. Umnumzane wekhaya wayitifiza 
ngokubabaza umashayandawonye. 

“Eyi MaNzimande, safa!” esho ezamula futhi ezelula. Kwabe 
uzithintele. 

“Nifanele phela wukufa! Angithi niqedwa yile ngculaza 
eniyithola ngokuhamba nibhabhabala nje! Awu, amadoda 
angamanuku! Afana nse nempukane yona efike ihlale emboleni 
bese isuka lapho iyohlala phezu kokudla kwekhethelo!” 

“Kahle MaNzimande bo! Inkemane seyaphenduka ingculaza 
lapha kuwena?” 

“Awuzange wena usho ukuthi uphethwe yindlala, uvele 
wababaza ukufa nje. Ngokwazi kwami yingculaza-ke ebulalayo.” 
Inkulumo kaMaNzimande yathanda ukumcasula uSithole. 
UMaNzimande wabe esephakela umyeni wakhe ukudla. 
USithole wakuthatha, wathi choko choko, engula amaqatha 
wodwa, wayesekubeka phansi, wakumboza. Kwenzeka konke 
lokhu nje kanti uMaNzimande uyabuka. 

“Yise kaMpisendlini, angithi kade kusho wena khona 
manjena ukuthi ulambile, manyala mani lawa owenza ekudleni? 
Ngiyabuza, manyala mani? Bewungasho ngani uma kanti ukudla 
bewungasakufuni? Kuzofanela manje uziphakele wena ukudla 
ebhodweni. Angikwazi ukudlala wena mina! Angikwazi nje!” 
Yasho imanzi yakwabo yakuthi hlwi ukudla yaphuma nakho, 


yakuqulela esitsheni senja phandle. USithole waphuma ekhishini 
eseya kolala, nomkakhe wabuye walandela. 

Baphuza ukufika ubuthongo kuSithole ethatha ebeka: 

“Uma kungasekho ukuthula phakathi komuzi wami, kufanele 
ngishaye isixaxa. Ngizomshiya nawo lo muzi. Akangazi kahle 
mina, nginguJobe ongenankinga nje. Ngifuna ukubona ukuthi 
uyosala ephendulana nobani uma mina ngingasekho lapha. 
Angiyona into yokuganga. Ngidlale umfazi! Ngeke! Ngithi 
ngeke!” Kwathi ngesikade ubuthongo bathi lelele, zaya 
kakhulu.

 Ukusa kwabonwa nguyena uSithole, wathatha imoto 
wakhala wemuka. Wafika esitolo kuseyisekuseni kakhulu, 
kungakabi yisikhathi sokuvula. Waqonda endlini kaDumazile, 
wangqongqoza. UDumazile wavula. USithole wangena, wahlala 
phezu kombhede. 

“Hawu,kwanuka ugwayi sewuyabhema yini?” 

“Usho ngani?” 

“Ngizwa kunuka ugwayi sengathi kade usanda kubhenywa.” 

“Nx, ayi suka. Yiphoyisa uMkhize lona obekade efikile 
lapha ezocela ngimenanele ngezinti zikamentshisi. Ugwayi 
wakhe uwokhele ngaso leso sikhathi.” USithole wakhombisa 
ukungaphatheki kahle ukubona ukuthi ekuseni kangaka 
uMthovovo usephuma endlini kaDumazile. 

“Washesha kangaka ukufika namhlanjena?” 

“Ngizophuza itiye.” Ahleke uDumazile. Bakhumbula ukuthi 

konje bebengakabingelelani, babingelelana. 

“Akakwenzelanga yini umama kaMpisendlini?” 

“Eyi, musa ukuyiphatha indaba yalowo msangano wena. 
Njengoba ungibona ngalesi sikhathi nje, ngizokutshela ukuthi 
qoqa konke okungokwakho; ntambama uzothutha uyohlala 
eMafezini.” Kwathanda ukumethusa lokho uDumazile. 


Wayengenalo ulwazi lokuthi impilo yakwenye indawo 
izokumphatha kanjani. Nokho akenqabanga. 

Yashaya intambama engaliyo, wathutha uDumazile. Izimpahla 
zakhe zathuthwa nguyena uSithole ngeveni yakhe. Kwathi uma 
iphoyisa uMkhize libuza ukuthi uDumazile uthutha nje ulibhekisa 
kuliphi ilizwe, kwaphendula uSithole kuqala: 

“Ngimphindisela kubo lapho ngamthatha khona.” Laxakeka nje 
iphoyisa ukuthi uDumazile uhambelani esitolo lokhu bebehlezi 
kahle njena. 

Kwathi ukuba bafike eMafezini, behlisa izimpahla emotweni, 
bazifaka endlini. UDumazile wandlala kahle umbhede. 
Esikhundleni sokuba uSithole aphindele emuva, ngoba phela 
wayesewuqedile umsebenzi ayewuzele, wathatha imoto wayifaka 
egalaji, wavala. UDumazile waxakeka nje ukuthi uSithole 
akasahambi ngani ngoba phela kuhlwa ngobumnyama. USithole 
waphuma egalaji maqede wangena endlini. UDumazile wayehlezi 
phezu kombhede, naye uSithole wahlala eduzane kwakhe. Kwabe 
sekuqala ingxoxo eyasusa esikhulu isixakaxaka lesi. USithole 
wasuke wakhulumela eduzane kakhulu kobuso bukaDumazile 
okwadala ukuba agxume izithonto ayokuma eduze kwesicabha. 

“Ngizomemeza!” UDumazile esho ngoba ebona uSithole 
ekhuluma ngendlela ayengayejwayele neze. 

“Umemezeni?” 

“Hhayi bo! Kodwa bazothini nje abantu?” 

“Bazothini kwani? Abantu balapha abazi lutho ukuthi mina 
nawe siyizini. Bazocabanga ukuthi wena uyinkosikazi yami. 
Akekho umuntu owazi uMaNzimande lapha.” 

“Ngeke bo baba kaMpisendlini! Ngeke kulunge!” Asho 
uDumazile aze anikine ikhanda ekhombisa ukuthi akafuni 
ngempela nje. USithole wehlisa umoya. Wabona ukuthi kufanele 
aqwale umqansa. Wathembisa uDumazile umhlaba nezulu. 


Akukho ayengakusho ukuthi kuyokuba ngokwakhe uma 
sebethandene. Ngisho indlu lena wamthembisa yona. Kwathi 
ngesikade babuye bazixoxela nezinye izindaba eziphathelene 
nomsebenzi. Ngesikhathi sokulala, uDumazile walala ekamelweni 
lakhe, kanti uSithole walala kwelinye. 

UMaNzimande akazange abuthi quthu ubuthongo e-Adams. 
USithole wayeqala ngqa ukungalali ekhaya engabikanga. Kwathi 
kwesikabhadakazi, wavuka uMaNzimande, wahlala ngezinqe 
phezu kombhede, wacabanga: 

“Kungenzeka nje ukuthi uyise kaMpisendlini uphukelwe 
yimoto? Mhlawumbe useqonyiwe nje, kwazi bani? Uma kuze 
kusa engaqhamuki, kuzofanela ngivuke ngiyombheka esitolo. 
Ehhe, ngizokwenza njalo.” Bathi lelele ubuthongo, wazumeka. 

Nakho-ke esefikelwa yiphupho elethusayo. Uphupha ebona 
uvava lwenkunzi olumnyama bhuqe luza kuyena luthibile. Wathi 
zinyawo zami ngibelethe. Wabaleka waze wayoqhamukela 
emfuleni owawungenisa; kwehla izigodo kanye namabibi. 
Amanzi kwakungekhona ukungcola kuyizibhidi. Kwathi kusenjalo 
kwaqhamuka isihlenga sewusa umfula. Kusona kwakukhona 
uSithole kanye nesipatsha sentokazi engathandanga ukubheka 
ngakuyena uMaNzimande. Wakhala kakhulu uMaNzimande 
efuna ukuya kumyeni wakhe, kodwa isihlenga samshiya. 
Wazama ukugijima osebeni lomfula, kodwa kwaba nhlanga 
zimuka nomoya. Intokazi lena yaphakamisa isandla imthathazela. 
Isihlenga samuka njalo saze sayosithela emagagasini. 

UMaNzimande waphaphama esejuluke esemanzi te. Wavuka 
maqede waqonda ekhishini ukuyofudumeza amanzi. Kwathi 
angaba ntukuntuku, wafaka uvoyizana, waphuza maqede 
waphumela phandle, wagabha. Wabe esebuyela endlini 
ukuyogeza. Kwathi angaqeda, wagqoka, waphuma esephikelele 
esitolo. 

Iphoyisa lalilokhu lizulazula esitolo ngenkathi kufika 


uMaNzimande. Yayibonakala nje imanzi kaSithole ukuthi 
ukuthukuthela kanye nokucikeka ikubambile. Iphoyisa labe 
selizincokolela nje: 

“Kwafika wena namhlanjena, ubasi usezohlala ekhaya yini?” 

“Ukushiso yini lokho?” 

“Ngisho ngoba phela nguwena ohlala ekhaya bese ubasi eza 

lapha.” 

“Uphi uSithole?” Iphoyisa liqale manje ukwethuka uma lizwa 
lowo mbuzo. 

“Akakafiki. Wambuza kimina, kanti awumshiyanga yini 
ekhaya?” 

“Akalalanga ekhaya.” Izinyembezi zigcwale amehlo 
kuMaNzimande. 

“O, sengiyakhumbula. Uthe uhambisa uDumazile kubo 
eMzimkhulu izolo.” 

Wathuka kwaphela nasozwaneni uMaNzimande. 
Wathula ebambelele esihlathini. Kwathi ngesikade wabheka 
ngasephoyiseni, wathi: 

“Uyise kaMpisendlini ubengangitsheli ngani uma ezokuba 
nendlela? Kungathiwani ukuba baqomene ngempela bakithi? 
Sengathi bekungcono khona uDumazile ehlezi lapha ngoba 
indoda yami beyingikhohlisa-ke ifike seyisule umlomo. Awu 
ngiyazisa ngalo nonkiloshi waseMzimkhulu!” Limoyizele iphoyisa. 

Kwathi kungasazi muntu, nabantu abazothenga sebeqala 
ukugcwala egcekeni esitolo, yaqhamuka iveni seyiwuhazane! 
Yangena nezintuli kwavalwa amehlo! Wayibamba yaze yavuma 
ngekhanda uSithole. Wehla, wavula esitolo, bangena abasebenzi. 
UMaNzimande wama phuhle eduze kwemoto yakwakhe 
phandle. Kwathi ngesikade, uSithole waphuma esitolo. Wayifica 
imanzi yakhe seyibila, ithuthumela! 


“Yini MaNzimande, kwenzenjani?” Avele aphihlike akhale 
uMaNzimande. Ngokubona ihlazo nokuphoxeka uSithole, 
wamthatha umkakhe ngemoto waye wamuthi qithi ekhaya. 
Wabe esethatha ethi: 

“Ngithe ngiseMkhobeni izolo kusihlwa, imoto yakhunyukelwa 
ngushafu, yagijima phansi nge-enkapleti. Cishe yangibulala. 
Ngenhlanhla enkulu ngikwazile ukuyibamba, yama. 
Ngihlale lapho-ke kwaze kwasa ngikhanda.” Kwavele kwala 
kuMaNzimande ukuba aqhubeke nokulalela leyo mbude. 

“Bewuyaphi eMkhobeni yise kaMpisendlini?” 

“EMkhobeni phela kusendleleni ebheke eMzimkhulu. 
Bengihambisa uDumazile kubo njengokwesicelo sakho. 
Ngiyathemba usakhumbula ukuthi wathi angimphindisele lapho 
ngamthatha khona. Ingozi-ke ingehlele ngisohambweni olunjalo.” 

“Pho bewukhanda kanjani ukilini kanjena?” Aphinde 
asikhihle futhi isililo uMaNzimande. USithole wezwa ecikeka nje 
ukutetenyelwa ngumuntu omdala kangaka, futhi olokhu embuza 
ipasi nesipesheli. Wadumisa imoto, watshela umkakhe ukuthi 
sebeyobonana ntambama, wakhala wemuka. 

UMaNzimande wasala nentshidi wasala nesidanga sevondwe. 
Wazibuza, ezifuna ngaphakathi: 

“Nkosi yami, lesi sichitho esingaka sivela kuphi phakathi 
komuzi wami? USithole ubengenje! Selokhu ngakhuluma noLizy 
angibange ngisakuthola ukuthula phakathi komuzi wami. Ukuba 
uLizy akangifikelanga nezindaba, ngabe ngisahlezi kahle nomyeni 
wami. Mh..., ngaze ngazibhidlizela umendo wami! Kuzofanela 
ngifunde manje ukuba ngingaqophisani noyise kaMpisendlini. 
Kuzothi uma ebuya ntambama, angifice sengiwumama omuhle 
wekhaya onesizotha. Ngeke ngisamqulisa amacala umyeni 
wami. Ngizomphekela ukudla okuhle akuthandayo, ngimenzele 
netiye, aphuze. Ehhe, kusukela namhlanjena ngizomphatha kahle 
umyeni wami. 


USithole wafika esitolo abantu sebazi ukuthi ubekade 
engalalanga ekhaya ngayizolo. UMaNzimande wayeseyichele 
yonke indawo indaba. Isimo sasingasesihle neze esitolo. 
Abasebenzi base behlukene phakathi. Nabantu nje abangabathengi 
base bekhombisa uqhekeko. Abanye babemdabukela 
uMaNzimande, kanti abanye babesimze bathi: 

“Uyalunga futhi uyaqhuqheka! Sengathi uDumazile 
angayithatha unomphela le ndoda yakhe. Ehhe, khona ezoyeka 
ukuba wumedemu lokhu.” 

Kwasetshenzwa-ke ngaleyo ndlela kwaze kwavalwa ntambama. 
Kwathi angathi kixi izihluthulelo esitolo ntambama uSithole, 
wangena emotweni yakhe, yaduma, zaya esephikelele khona 
eMafezini eMlazi. 

Ngemuva kwezinsuku ezimbili, uSithole wafikelwa ngomunye 
umcabango: 

“Ngeke ngishiye umfazi nomuzi wami. Lo muzi ngawakha 
kanzima kabi. Kuzofanela aphume aphele aphindele kubo. Ukuthi 
akusekho muntu kubo, akudokwe ligayelwe mina lelo.” USithole 
wayifaka-ke incwadi yesehlukaniso phakathi kwakhe nomkakhe. 
Wazibeka izizathu ezimenza angakwazi ukumbekezelela umkakhe. 
Inkantolo yambiza noMaNzimande ukuba azoziphendulela. 
Ngemuva kokulalelisisa macala onke, inkantolo yabeluleka 
ukuba bangahlukanisi, kodwa babekezelelane emshadweni 
wabo. Basukuma, bavalelisa, baphuma. USithole akalubhadanga 
unyawo emzini wakhe e-Adams, kodwa washaya imoto waqonda 
eMafezini eMlazi. 


ISAHLUKO SESITHUPHA 

“Ukuze ngizuze uMaNzimande eseyintombi, kwadingeka 
ukuba ngihambe ngijubalale. Kwakuwuhlanya lwentombi 
uMaNzimande. Wayeseshikilise eziningi izesheli. 
Ngaqhamuka mina wakoMatshana sengivela kophekwa lena 
kwaMhlabuyalingana, ngathatha kanye. Pho sengingahlulwa 
wuDumazile? Awu ngeke!”Wafunga wagomela uMondise. 

KwakunguMgqibelo kusihlwa ngenkathi uSithole eqhamuka 
nohalakasha logedla luzoqinisa umuzi, luzobethela phela. 
Alugcinanga lapho, lwaqinisa naye umninimuzi ngezindlela 
ezahlukene. Nakuba uSithole wayengasakujwayele ukugquma 
nokugabha, kodwa wazithola njalo ngantambama esegquma 
ngohlobo oluthile lwentelezi, kuthi angaqeda ageze wonke 
umzimba. Wayevuka ekuseni aphalaze ngobulawu obumhlophe. 
Wawusebenzisa kahle umuthi laze laphela golokoqo isonto 
njengokwesinqumo senyanga. Konke lokhu ukwenza nje 
akasalubhadi unyawo kwakhe e-Adams. 

Ngelinye ilanga uDumazile, esemsebenzini kwaNaidoo, 
wafikelwa ngumcabango: 

“Yebo khona uSithole mdala kunami, kodwa uyangithanda 
bantu. Wangiphathisa okweqanda emsebenzini esitolo 
sakwakhe. Wangithengela izimpahla zikanokusho. Wangifunela 
umsebenzi kuNaidoo ngemuva kokunganambithisisani nomkakhe 
uMaNzimande. Manje uzimisele ukuba ngibe wundlunkulu 
wakwakhe. Abazali bami futhi bangadla kahle ngami. Abanye 


abantu bathi umuntu omdala unempatho. Selokhu kwathi nhlo 
uSithole ukhuluma ulimi olulodwa; ulimi lokuthi ufuna ngibe 
ngumkakhe azoziqhenya ngaye. Selokhu ngingenile kule ndlu 
usengikhombisile ukuthi angangiphatha kanjani uma ngivuma. 
Nabantu bayasho ukuthi ngayeka izehla, imana uqobo lwayo.” 
UDumazile wathatha isinqumo asibona ukuthi simfanele. 

USithole wafika uDumazile esefikile evela emsebenzini. Wathi 
engena yena wayebingelelwa ngenkomishi yekhofi. Kwalandela 
esivuthayo isitshulu lesi. Kwenzeka konke lokhu nje abamile, 
kodwa bayaxoxa. 

“Akakuthethisi umkakho njengoba ungasavamile ukuya e-
Adams?” 

“Athethise bani, mina? Uyangazi naye ehlezi nje!” Ahleke 
kancane uDumazile. 

“Ngisazomvova! Yena, ngisazomvova! Ngiyezwa futhi 
ngabasiki bebunda ukuthi usethambe useyimfocomfoco.” 

“Hawu! Wathi uzwa ngosibhincamakhasana, kanti wena 
awusayi yini kwakho ukuyodla ilantshi emini?” 

“Angilubeki! Hleze angidlise lo mfazi.” 

“Yena kanti akafiki yini esitolo ukukulethela inkumbulo?” 

“Wazi kahle ukuthi kungenzekani uma engase afike esitolo. 
Wazi kahle. Ngamvala kulokho.” UDumazile wabe esexoxaxoxa 
ngezinto nje eziphathelene nomsebenzi wakwaNaidoo. Wagcina 
ngokuthi : 

“Mayelana nesicelo sakho semihla ngemihla….” Athi 
ukuthula kancane uDumazile. USithole ahlahle amehlo elindele. 
UDumazile waqhuba wathi: 

“Hhayi bengidlala!” Ayifunde ivaliwe uSithole. 

“Ngijatshuliswa yikho nje ukuthi unesikhathi sokudlala nami.” 

“Hhayi bo wena njalo!” UDumazile esho ngezwi elithambile 


namehlo alele. Athi ukukhophoza kancane. USithole asondelele 
ngakuyena, ambambe isandla sangakwesokunxele, sithambe. 
Wasondeza ubuso bakhe kobukaDumazile, baba bunye. Izindebe 
zemilomo zaqala ukududulana. 

UDumazile wanikezwa amandla negunya lokuba anakekele 
umuzi ngokugcwele. Waqasha umuntu wokusebenza. 
Wayezoholelwa nguSithole ukuba alungise igceke. Nempela kwaba 
njalo. Kwakungekhona ubuhle balo lobuya kwakuyisimanga! 
Kwakutshalwe ungwengwe olwalulokhu lugundwa kahle 
ngemishini yesilungu. Ekupheleni kwalo kwakubiywe ngocingo 
oluzungeze umuzi wonke, luthothene ngendlela yokuthi ngisho 
nenyoni mbala kwakungelula ukuba ichushe. Uma umuntu efuna 
ukungena esangweni, wayethinta inkinojana maqede kuzwakale 
izwi liqhamuka ngaphakathi endlini libuza ukuthi ngubani lowo. 
Kwenye inkathi inkulumo yayixoxwa ize iphelele khona lapho 
abantu bengasabonananga mahlanze. 

Indlu yase igcwaliswe ngezimpahla zikanokusho. 
Amawodilophu kanye nemibhede kwakungokohlobo olubizayo 
futhi oluphambili. Yilelo nalelo kamelo lalinombhede kanye 
nowodilophu walo. Endaweni yokuhlala kwakubekwe osofa 
abathofozela kamnandi. Eduzane kwabo kwakubekwe 
ucingo kanye nomabonwakude omibalabala. Phansi endlini 
kwakundlalwe ubuthofothofo bukakhaphethi. Phezu 
kwamakhabethe kwakuhlotshiswe ngezimbali eziyizithombo 
zokutshalwa. Uma umuntu engena wayezibonela nje naye ukuthi 
ikhona impilo kulo muzi.

 Zahamba izikhathi uDumazile waqala ukuzisola. Kwathi uma 
sekuqala inyanga yesithathu, wacela emsebenzini ukuyozanelisa 
kudokotela. Udokotela wafike wamhlola, wayesemtshela ukuthi 
ngempela sekunjalo. Wake wathula uDumazile ecabanga: 

“Hhayi bo Nkosi yami! Ngoba ngangihlela nje! Pho 
ngingakhulelwa kanjani?” Udokotela wabuza uDumazile uhlobo 
lokuhlela ayelusebenzisa. UDumazile wachaza ukuthi wayehlela 


ngendlela yokusebenzisa amaphilisi. Udokotela wachaza ingozi 
umuntu engamvelela uma eke nje wakhohlwa ukuwasebenzisa 
amaphilisi. UDumazile wakhumbula masinyane ukuthi kwake 
kwamehlela lokho. Wake wathula esacabanga: 

“Kuzothiwani nje? Ngize ngithole ingane yesibili ngingashadile? 
Abazali bami bazothi ngiyabacabangela kodwa? Mh, ngaze 
ngaziyala ngokudlala ngomlilo!” UDumazile wake wacabanga 
ukusihushula isisu, kodwa wabuye wazikhuza. Wasuke 
wakhumbula isigigaba samantombazane amathathu ayefunda 
nawo ashona elandelana kade ekhiphe izisu. UDumazile wabe 
esecela iseluleko kudokotela. Udokotela wamtshela ukuba 
asheshe aqale ukuhamba umtholampilo. Wamnikeza amaphilisi. 
Wakhokha, waphuma maqede wangena indlela ebheke ekhaya. 
Kwathi ukuba afike, wangena endlini, wazilahla phezu kombhede. 

USithole wamfica uDumazile ewubhaca embhedeni. 
Wasola ukuthi kukhona okushaya amanzi. Wasondela kuyena, 
wamnyakazisa. 

“Swithadi, kwenzenjani mntakwethu?” Avuke ngomude 
umzimba lo uDumazile, ahlale phezu kombhede abambelele 
ezihlathini. 

“Eyi, angazi ukuthi ngizoyiqala ngiyithini le ndaba.” Athi 
ukuthula kancane uDumazile, abheke phansi, izinyembezi zivele 
zithi qatha qatha. 

“Kanti khuluma nje ukhululeke mntakwethu. Ngitshele lavi.” 

“Kade ngiye kudokotela, wafike wathi ngikhulelwe, izinyanga 
zintathu.”Wabonakala ethuka uSithole, kodwa waziqinisa 

njengendoda. 

“Uze waya kudokotela njena bewusoleni?” 

“Kanti ngiyaqala yini ukukhulelwa? Ngibe sengicela 
emsebenzini ukuba bangivumele ngiyobonana nodokotela. Ufike 
wabona-ke yena ukuthi sekuyabheda. Eyi, Nkosi yami, kazi 


ngangenzani?” Esho enikina ikhanda ekhombisa ukuzisola. 

“Ungakhathazeki, ngizowuthwala wonke lowo mthwalo. 
Yizinto ezincane lezo mntakwethu.”

 Nakuba wayephatheke kabi uDumazile, kodwa kwathi 
cosololo uma ezwa lawo mazwi ayinduduzo. 

“Uzoya nini ekhaya ukuyoziveza kubazali bami?” 
Athi ukuthula kancane uSithole esacabanga. Lo mbuzo 
wamqhamukela kabi engawulindele. Wathatha wathi: 

“Kunganjani uma ngiya ekupheleni kwenyanga ezayo?” 
Anqekuzise ikhanda uDumazile ekhombisa ukuthi uyavumelana 
nalokhu okushiwo nguSithole. 

“UMama wayevame ukuthi ufuna inkomo yakhe kube yimali. 
Kusho ukuthi uma ungase uphathe izinkulungwane ezimbili 
zamarandi, zingakwazi ukumenelisa. Ubaba-ke wayengakaze nje 
ayixoxe leyo.” 

“UMama wakho angimkweleti lutho. Inkomo eyinhlawulo 
kwakufanele ayithole kuMoloi. Mina umuntu engimkweletayo 
ngubaba wakho.” 

“Uthisha uMoloi akayikhokhanga nje!” esho uDumazile 
ebuyisa izinhlonze. 

“Akudokwe ligayelwe mina lelo. Le nkomo ayivele ikhishwe 
nje. Kunemidanti nemibandela ukuphuma kwayo. Futhi 
kuyihlazo nje ukukhokhela into ongayazi.” 

Kwathanda ukumphatha kabi uDumazile ukuzwa ukuthi kanti 
unina ngeke athole lutho kuSithole. 

“Khona yikuphi okungcono ukuba ngiyokhokha isephulo 
kubaba wakho nokuba ngikubuyisele esikoleni uma sewutetile?” 
Waqale wathula uDumazile esacabanga ukuthi yikuphi 
okungcono uma eqhathanisa. Kwathi ekugcineni wathi: 

“Kungcono ukuba ungibuyisele esikoleni.”Wamamatheka 


kancane uSithole. UDumazile waphaka ukudla, wanikeza 
uSithole. Wadla, balala. 

Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi uDumazile waphoqeka 
ukuba awuyeke umsebenzi ngenxa yokugula. Wayesehlala 
ngokungaphatheki neze kahle. Izinyawo zazivuvukala 
kabi. Wayesehlala ephethwe yisiyezi, abuyise. Nokho-ke 
akubanga yinkinga kakhulu ukuhlala kwakhe ekhaya. USithole 
wamphatha ngezandla ezifudumele, emphethe njengeqanda. 
Wayemphathela yonke into ayithandiswayo. 

UDumazile wayevame ukugoduka ngemuva kwezinyanga 
ezintathu. Kwaya ngokuya wagoduka ngemuva kwezinyanga 
eziyisithupha. Wagcina esegoduka kanye ngonyaka; agoduke 
ngesikhathi sikaKhisimuzi. Lokho kwakungasho ukuthi 
wayeseqala ukubhunguka, kodwa wayezama ukuqongelela imali 
ukuze ingaxhaphazeki ngokwehla enyuka ngezimoto. Imali yona 
wayeyiposa zinyanga zonke. Wayephathisa umshayeli webhasi 
eThekwini ukuze ayinikeze unina ekhaya. Kuthe ukuba ayeke 
ukusebenza ngenxa yokugula, lo mthwalo wokuposa wahlala 
phezu kwamahlombe kaSithole. Wayekhipha kweyakhe imali. 

Zahamba izikhathi wasikwa uDumazile. Kwenzeka konke 
lokhu nje kuphakathi kwamabili ebusuku. USithole wathatha 
imoto wamphuthumisa esibhedlela eMshiyeni. Akuthathanga 
sikhathi eside bafika. Wehla emotweni uDumazile, wangeniswa 
egunjini labantu abanjalo. Wathi efika nje kwabe kwenzeka 
lokho. Abahlengikazi bamphuthuma, bawenza kahle wonke 
umsebenzi wabo. Kwathi ukuba baqede, bamsonga kahle 
umntwana, bambeka eduze kukanina. 

“Kodwa ngumuntu muni?” kubuza uDumazile ekhulumela 
phansi kubonakala nje ukuthi utubekile. 

“Ngumkhapheyana.” Amoyizele uDumazile sekumfoma 
nekhala. 

“Sizothi ngubani igama lakhe?” kubuza umhlengikazi ephethe 


ibhuku nepeni. Aqale athule uDumazile esacabanga: 

“Konje khona ngizoze ngimqambe igama nje lo mntwana, 
ngiyothi kubazali bami ngimthole kuphi? Mh…!”Wazwakala ethi: 

“Asithi nguMtholephi Kheswa.” Nempela umhlengikazi 
wabhala phansi, wadlulela kwabanye. 

UDumazile akahlalanga isikhathi eside esibhedlela. Kwathi 
ntambama uSithole wafika esebalandile benosana lwabo. 
Wajabula kabi uSithole ukubona ukuthi uDumazile uthole 
isigemfunga sensizwa engaka! 

“Abahlengikazi babuzile ukuthi igama lomntwana ngubani? 
Ngivele mina ngangazi nje ukuthi ngizomqamba ngithi ubani. 
Ngibe sengithi nje uMtholephi.” USithole wamqamba naye 
elakhe. Wakhipha amanabukeni kanye nezingubo zomntwana. 
UDumazile wamgqokisa umntwana, wamnikeza uSithole ukuba 
amgone. Ngemuva kokubhalisa imininingwane ethile, baphuma 
sebeyongena emotweni phandle. 

Bathi bangangena nje emotweni, uDumazile wawuhlaba 
inhlali owakhe. Uthule nje akathule kodwa uyathatha uyabeka: 

“USithole wathi angikhethe phakathi kokuba akhokhele 
abazali bami nokuba angiphindisele esikoleni. Njengoba 
ngakhetha ukuba angibuyisele esikoleni nje, kusho ukuthi 
abazali bami abatholi lutho ngami? Uthisha uMoloi akazange 
amkhokhele uLerato. Manje uSithole akafuni ukukhokhela 
uMtholephi? Kanti mina kuzothiwa ngiyintombazane eziphethe 
kanjani? Awu ngeke, ngizolakha isu lokuba abazali bami 
badle ngami. Ngeke nje ngikhuleliswe ngumuntu adlule lapho 
angabakhokheli abazali bami. Ngeke nje!” USithole waxakeka 
nje ukuthi uDumazile ucabangani. Kwathi noma uSithole ethi 
uyabuza ukuthi kwenzenjani, uDumazile anikine ikhanda 
ekhombisa ukuthi akukho lutho olonakele. Bahamba njalo baze 
bafika eMafezini eMlazi. Behla emotweni, bangena endlini. 

Unkatho lwamudla uSithole ukuba kube nguyena olungisa 


ukudla. Yazama indoda ukufudumeza isikhokho sangayizolo. 
Waphaka, badla. Kwathi bangaqeda, uSithole waqoqa izitsha 
wazihlanza. Kwenzeka konke lokhu nje uDumazile uhlezi phansi 
ugone usana lwakhe. Kwathi angaqeda uSithole, bazixoxela 
izindaba ezingatheni nje kwaze kwashaya isikhathi sokuya kolala. 
Bengakazumeki, uDumazile waluqala-ke udaba lwakhe: 

“Manje baba kaMtho bengicela ungihambise ekhaya kusasa. 
Uma ngicabanga ngabazali bami, ngivele ngishaywe wuvalo 
kubande kwamancane. Ngiyasola ukuthi ikhona into eyenzekile 
ekhaya.” 

“Into efana nani?” 

“Awazi wena, abakithi abadala banolaka kabi! Mhlawumbe 

sebelwisa abazali bami nje ngenxa yesenzo sami.” 

“Isenzo sakho sani?” 

“Sokuthola umntwana ongahlawulwanga. Abalele 

bangathukuthela bangiphuce lo mntwana uma kuthuleka 
njengoba kuthulekile nje.” 

“Abathukuthelanga ngani ngomntwana wakho wokuqala 
ongakhokhelwanga?” 

“Ubaba washweleza. Wabathembisa ukuthi ngeke 
kusaphinda. Njengoba sekuphindile manje, ubaba uzongidikila, 
athi abaphansi abenze into abayithandayo ngami nomntwana 
wami.” Athule kancane uSithole esacabanga: 

“Eyi madoda! Yinto ezothiwani-ke lena? Kusho ukuthi 
kufanele ngiphathe imali yenhlawulo. Okwakobani nje ukuziyisa 
ejele ubhekile? Mh, sengizophoqeka phela ukuba ngikhokhe 
isephulo sikayise. Eyi, madoda!” USithole wavuma ukuthi 
uzomhambisa uDumazile kubo, kodwa hhayi ngokushesha 
njengoba uDumazile ayecelile. Wathi bayohamba ngoMgqibelo 
ngemuva kokuba esevalile esitolo ntambama. 

Washaya-ke uMgqibelo ongaliyo. USithole wavala esitolo 


maqede waphuthuma eMafezini ukuyolanda uDumazile nosana 
lwabo. Wabafica sebemi ngomumo. Bangena emotweni, 
yasuka seyiphikelele eMzimkhulu. Babehamba bezixoxela nje. 
UDumazile wayelele phezu komqondo othile. 

“Kufanele baba kaMtho uthembise abazali bami okuthile.” 

“Okufana nani nje?” 

“Mhlawumbe singathi nje into enjengokungicela kumbe 
ukungilobola, noma-ke ukukhokha inhlawulo ngomntwana lo,” 
esho ekhomba usana lwabo. 

“Ungakhathazeki kulokho mntakwethu, ngihlomile ngalapho. 
Bengingathini phela ukuqhamuka ngivathazela nje kubaba 
wakho, nokwenza ayengikhonze kangaka!” Kuthi cosololo 
kuDumazile. Yahamba njalo imoto yaze yayofika kuhwalala 
kwaKheswa eMzimkhulu. 

“Yise kaDumazile, ngekabani le moto ema phandle?”Wathi 
lacu uKheswa, walunguza ewindini. Wathula isikhashana 
esabukisisa. Asukume noMaNdovela alunguze. 

“Hawu, sengathi yimoto kaSithole nje lena?” kusho 
uMaNdovela sakubuza. Kuthi kusenjalo kuphume uDumazile 
emotweni egone umntwana, alandele noSithole sebeqonde 
emnyango. UMaNdovela benomyeni wakhe bahlala phansi. 

“Nqo nqo nqo!” UDumazile engqongqoza esicabheni. 

“Ngena!” sekusho uMaNdovela. Kuvuleke isicabha, bangene 
maqede bahlukane ngezinini, bahlale phansi. Kwabingelela 
uSithole. Bavuma. Baphilelana. 

“Dumazile mntanami, sewahamba ijuba likaNowa! Khona 
bewusakhumbula nje ukuthi washiya umntwana lapha ekhaya?” 
“Yebo! Bengisakhumbula mama. Angithi bengiyiposa nje 

imali! Beyingafiki yini?” 
“Beyifika ukufika, kodwa umntwana uyamdinga unina wakhe. 


Awu, sewungaze ufike umntwana eseyintombi!” Ahlekele phansi 
uDumazile. 

“UMaNzimande nimshiyile yena?” Aqale abakaze uSithole, 
bese ethi: 

“Yebo!” Athande ukwexwaya uMaNdovela. Wayecabanga 
ukuthi ingane lena ngekaMaNzimande. 

“Pho umntwana lo?” esho ekhomba usana. 

“Umntwana ngowendodakazi yenu.”

 Umnumzane uKheswa amise ikhanda sengathi akayizwisisi 
kahle le nto engena ngezindlebe zakhe. 

“Ngithe angize ngizozilahla kinina ngokuba ngizoziveza.” 
Anikine ikhanda uKheswa. Asukume kancane abheke 
ngasemsamo. Athi qala qala, angayiboni le nto ayicingayo. 
Waphuma esedlwathizela eseya kwenye indlu. UMaNdovela 
wayifunda ivaliwe, walandela. Wamfica umyeni wakhe edonsa 
iklwa ngaphansi kombhede. 

“Wenzani yise kaDumazile? Wenzani?” 

“Ngizobonda wena ngomkhonto uma ungabhekile!” 

“Uzoze ungibonde ngomkhonto nje ngenzeni yise 
kaDumazile? Hhi, ngenzeni?”“Awuboni ukuthi uSithole 
uzongedelela lapha emzini wami? Ukhulelisa ingane yami bese 
ezopepenyeka nayo lapha! Akwenziwa lokho kokaNdodenye 
umuzi! Ukuthi besikhonzene naye akusho lokho ukuthi 
usengamane enze noma yikanjani emzini wami. Akhulelise 
ingane yami? Isigcino phela uzodlulela kuwena!” 

“Yise kaDumazile, ubabezala wayeseluleka ngokuphakamisa 
isikhali phakathi komuzi. Wayethi lokho kuletha umkhokha 
omubi ekhaya. Kubi impela lokhu okwenziwe nguSithole, kodwa 
kufanele kuhlalwe phansi kuxoxwe.” 

Umnumzane uKheswa wazikhumbula izeluleko zikayise 


esaphila, wathamba. Babonisana ngokuthi uSithole ahlawule. 
Baphuma endlini igwebu lemfezi selehlile, baqonda ekhishini 
lapho kwakuhlezi khona uSithole benoDumazile. 

“Awu goba msenge zidle izimbuzi! Yimina lona osevele 
alibuke nje iphithi liziletha esagileni? Hho, yekanini imihlola! Lafa 
elihle kakhulu; lafa silibhekile!” 

“Ayidle izibekele Nozulu!” Sekushweleza uSithole. 

“Idle izibekele ini, inja?” Aphinde ashweleze futhi uSithole. 

“Isenzo sakho simbi kabi wena! Ungcole kabi! Awuhlukene 
nokuthi ugange nengane yakho! Angikaze mina ngiyibone into 
enjena!” 

“Nozulu ngiyashweleza ezinyanyeni zonke zakwaKheswa. 
Ngizimisele ukukhipha konke enginakho ngishweleze ngakho 
kwabalele.”

 Kuthi cosololo kumnumzane uKheswa. Wabheka 
ngakumkakhe, wathatha wathi: 

“MaNdovela, udinga ukuhlawuliswa lo muntu. Udinga 
inhlawulo. Akuyona eyami le ngane adlale ngayo, ngekababa.” 

“Yiqiniso yise kaDumazile. Kufanele umntwana ahlawulwe 
nje.” Umnumzane uKheswa wabheka ngakuyena uSithole, 
wathatha wathi: 

“Ngizofuna izinkulungwane ezinti zamalandi.” Esho emisa 
iminwe emithathu. USithole adonse isikhwanyana sakhe 
ekhukhwini elisenqulwini, akhiphe amaphuphu ezikhova wodwa, 
athi: 

“Ngicela into yokubeka.” 

“Thatha ithileyi MaNdovela.” Nempela asukume alithathe, 
alibeke phansi phambi kukaSithole. Aqale-ke ukuyibhacaza imali 
uSithole. Kwathi ingaphelela isibalo leso, uKheswa wayithatha 
ngethileyi wayibeka emsamo, wabuya wahlala phansi. 


“MaNdovela, angazi noma iyabongwa yini into enjena?” esho 
ebheke phansi ebambelele ngezandla ebunzini. UMaNdovela 
wathatha wathi: 

“Siyabonga-ke bandla!” esho ebheke kuSithole. 

Wabonakala uSithole esencibilika, kwazise phela amaphaphu 

ayesephezulu. UDumazile waxoxa nonina. 

“Uphi uLerato ma?” 

“Awu uLilatho uselele. Sewuyombona ekuseni.” Kwale 
kuDumazile, afune ukuyombona ngaso leso sikhathi umntwana 
wakhe. Wathatha usana lwakhe walugonisa uyise walo, baphuma 
benonina sebeya endlini lapho kulele khona uLerato. 

“Hawu, usekhule kangaka umntanami bantu!” 

“We mame…! Uklekhule kangaka umntanakho, angithi 
ubungasabuyi ukuzombona ekhula!” Ahleke uDumazile uma 
ezwa unina ekhuluma kanjena. Wanyakazisa indodakazi yakhe, 
yaphaphama. 

“Muntuza, uyambona uma?” Acikice amehlo uLerato bese 
elala futhi. Kubonakale nje ukuthi umntwana uphazanyiswe 
esesebuthongweni bakhe obumnandi kabi. Bamyeka, 
bammbathisa ingubo. Baphuma behamba bezixoxela nje. 

“Kodwa mama, ubaba ubengeke esalinda kuze kuse bese 
kuyima ekhokhisa uSithole le mali?” 

“Wukuthi uyihlo ubedinwe kabi! Umqondo wakhe uye 
uphambane uma kukhona okumcasulile. Ngimkhuze esethi 

uthatha umkhonto ukuyobhokoda uSithole.” 

“Hhayi bo ma! Kanti bese kunjalo?” 

“Nyaniso! Awumazi wena uyihlo ukuthi unjani uma 

esethukuthele! Isenzo sakho kodwa mntanami sibe sibi kabi! 
Indoda endala kangaka pho?” 

UDumazile waqala esinye isihloko sendaba. 


“Mama, angazi ukuthi ngizokwenzenjani ukuze ngithole 
umzanyana. Bengingathokoza uma ngingase ngithole umuntu 
othembekile.” 

“Awu Dumazile, anisafuni ukuziphathela izingane 
zenu? Nizalelani pho?” Ahleke kancane uDumazile kodwa 
angamphenduli. 

“Asazi-ke ngoba phela noLilatho uyafunda esikoleni. Ukuba 
ubengafundi, bengingathi thatha yena ayokulekelela.” 

“Uyazi mama, yisu lelo. Ngizothatha yena ayofunda eMlazi. 
Kuyothi-ke ntambama angisize uma esebuyile esikoleni.” 

“Angazi-ke phela mntanami, kuzofanela ukhulume 
noyisemkhulu.” 

“Usho ukuthi ubaba angase ale naye ma?” 

“Angazi mntanami.” Babe sebengena ekhishini lapho 
kwakuhlezi khona oSithole benoKheswa. 

UMaNdovela walubeka-ke udaba kumyeni wakhe. UKheswa 
waqale wanqaba ukudedela uLerato, kodwa kwathi uma 
sekuxoxiswana kahle, wagcina evumile. Ngemuva kwezingxoxo 
bahlukana, yilowo nalowo eseya egunjini alungiselwe lona. 

Ngakusasa ekuseni uMaJwara wabona imoto kaSithole 
imi ebaleni kwaKheswa, waphikelela khona. Wadlula 
kwaMaMdinsilwa wafika wamtshela ukuthi make bathi gqi 
kwaKheswa ukuyobheka ukuthi kwenzenjani. Nempela 
uMaMdinsilwa wasukumela phezulu. Bathi bengena nje ebaleni, 
baphambana nabo emnyango. 

“Hawu, senixoshwa yithina yini Dumo?” kusho uMaJwara 
esethelwa ngamahloni. Kuphendule uMaNdovela kuqala: 

“Cha bandla Jwara, bewuvele umthwalo ususobhokweni. 
Sebeleti kabi emsebenzini wabo.” 

“UMaNzimande yena akezanga?” kubuza uMaJwara ngoba 


ecabanga ukuthi uDumazile uphathele uMaNzimande ingane. 
Kuthi xhifi kuDumazile, anyukubale abuyise nezinhlonze. 
UMaNdovela ayilande-ke indaba. Kwathi engakaqedi, kwezwakala 
uDumazile esethi: 

“Asihambe yise kaMtho.” UMaMdinsilwa abuke uMaJwara 
kodwa angasho lutho. UDumazile wangena emotweni egone 
usana lwakhe, uLerato benoSithole balandela. Bavalelisana-ke 
ebaleni. Imoto yaduma, yasuka. 

OMaJwara benoMaMdinsilwa babamba abebeze ngayo. 
Babehamba bezixoxela endleleni. 

“We ntombi kaJwara! Kodwa yini lena evelele uMaNzimande? 
UDumazile useyithathe ngempela indoda yakhe?” 

“Indaba yabantu besilisa! Ahlupha kabi amadoda ngokungafuni 
ukuguga. Mdala kabi phela uSithole ukuba angenza lo mkhuba.” 

“Nezingane zamantombazane zinjalo kodwa, zihamba zizineka 
nje koyise ngoba zifuna imali.” 

“UDumazile akasabuyi nje ekhaya kanti usengumfazi kaSithole? 
Yehheni bo we bantu! Shono nje kanti uMaNdovela wayebalisa 
kangaka ngokungabuyi kwakhe!” 

“Kusho ukuthi oSithole laba bebengakezwa ngalesi sifo. 
Kusobala bebengakezwa.” 

“Usho lesi samagama amathathu?” 

“Sona kanye.” 

“Akekho umuntu ongakezwa ngalesi sifo. Noyedwa! Nalabo 
esibaphathayo kungukuthanda kwabo.” 

“Musa ukukhuluma kanjalo wena bo! Uzozizondanisa nabantu 
qiniso! Abantu basosizini kabi ngokuhanjelwa yizihlobo zabo.” 

“Uthi angithini phela ngoba uhulumeni usememezele waze 
washa izwi ezama njalo ukuxwayisa abantu ngobungozi balesi 
sifo. Umuntu esingakamphathi lesi sifo uyabuphika ubukhona 


baso. Asisho lutho-ke, kodwa isalakutshelwa sibona ngomopho.” 

“Ngiyakuvumela khona, akekho umuntu ongakezwa futhi 
nongazi ngalesi sifo.” 

“Bheka nje uhulumeni usekhiphe namaplastiki ukuba abantu 
bawagqoke uma beya ocansini, kodwa abantu abanobudedengu 

njengoSithole abawasebenzisi.” 

“Usho amaplastiki lawa okuthiwa amakhondolo?” 

“Usho wona kanye. Amakhondomu.” 

“Ngoba esebenza ngempela wona amakhondolo lawo?” 

“Kuthiwa ayasiza wona uma esetshenziswe kahle nangendlela 

yakhona.” 

“Okusho ukuthi ikhona ingozi uma engasetshenziswanga 
kahle?” 

“Yonke into inobungozi uma ingasetshenziswanga kahle 
nangendlela yakhona.” 

“Abantu abanenkani njengoSithole bazovelelwa wumshophi; 

umshophi wokuhaqwa yigciwane lengculaza.” 

“USithole udlala kabi; udlala ngomlilo, uzokumhangula” 

“Uyozibona yena-ke ukuqeda.” 

“Kwakungcono kuqala ngezikhathi zethu. Izifo 
ezinjengogcunsula namaqondo zazelapheka. Hhayi ubhubhane 
lolu olushisa ubuhanguhangu okomlilo wequbula! Awu, 
seziphelile izingane zethu!” 

“Kudela umfazi ongazalanga, qiniso! Indaba yokubuka 
izingane zakho zibuthuka phambi kwakho! Izingane zethu 
azibazi ubumnandi bokuba musha. Nansi imamba ivundle kabili 
endleleni. Weqa, ngqofo!” 

“Ukuba izingane zethu ziyakhuzwa zilalele, ngabe azisayi 
ocansini. Abantu abaningi esibangcwaba mihla namalanga 
bahamba ngendlela yocansi; ucansi olungaphephile.” 


“Kepha usho ukuthi bangayi ocansini baze babe yimixhiliba 
yezalukazi nemidodovu yamaxhegu?” 

“Cha phela, kuze kufike isikhathi lapho izithandani zingena 
ezingeni lokwakha umuzi. Nalapho futhi, kufanele izithandani 
zihambe ziyohlolwa igazi kuqala anduba ziye ocansini.” 

“Sengathi nguwena wedwa onalowo mqondo. Abantu 
abaningi abayihhoyi leyo.” 

“Sisazoqhubeka nokubangcwaba-ke njengoba sibangcwaba 
nsuku zonke nje.” 

Bahamba njalo bezixoxela baze bahlukana enhlukanandlela 
yilowo nayilowo esebambe ebheke kwakhe. 


ISAHLUKO SESIKHOMBISA 

Ngemuva kokubuya kwakhe eMzimkhulu uDumazile, wavuka 
ngakusasa ekuseni waphikelela esikoleni esiseduzane nomuzi 
wakhe. Wathi efika nje wayezikhalela kuthishanhloko ukuba 
ancikise uLerato kwezinye izingane. Ngemuva kokuncenga 
isikhathi eside uDumazile, nothishanhloko elandula, wagcina 
evumile ukwamukela umntwana. Wakhokha imali yesikole, 
wamshiya-ke umntwana. 

UDumazile akabange esabuyela emsebenzini wakhe 
wakwaNaidoo. Wahlala ekhaya unyaka wonke esakhulisa 
umntwana wakhe. Nokho-ke wayengenayo inkinga yemali 
ngoba uSithole wayemondla, emthengela yonke into ayidingayo. 
Wamqashela ngisho nomzanyana ukuze angakhathazeki. ULerato 
wakhokhelwa nguyena esikoleni, futhi emondla njengengane 
yakhe. 

Ngonyaka olandelayo uDumazile wabuyela naye esikoleni. 
Waba nenhlanhla enkulu yokuba uSithole abe ngumngani 
kathishanhloko wesinye sezikole khona elokishini. Kwahlelwake 
ukuba uDumazile ayokwenza ibanga leshumi. Leso senzo 
sacishe sasusa omkhulu umsindo esikoleni. Inqubo nenkambiso 
yesikole yayithi umfundi ovela kwesinye isikole akavumelekile 
ukuba ayoqala ibanga leshumi kulesi sikole. Othisha bakhononda 
ngokuthi uDumazile kwakufanele ayoqala phansi ebangeni 
lesishiyagalolunye uma enokwamukeleka. Abafundi bona 
bacishe bagxoba itoyitoyi ngalesi senzo sikathishanhloko. 
Babekhala ngokuthi nabo banazo izihlobo kanye nabangani 
babo abangemukelwanga ebangeni leshumi ngenxa yokuqina 


kwemithetho kulesi sikole. Babuza-ke ukuthi pho ngonjani lo 
mfundi yena owamukelwayo? 

Nokho-ke uthishanhloko wazama ukuwubhula lowo mlilo, 
wathembisa ukuthi iphutha elifana naleli ngeke lisaphinda 
lenzeke ngomuso. UDumazile yena wagcina engenile ebangeni 
leshumi. 

Baqala-ke ukufundisa othisha. UDumazile wazibonela 
zibekwa nje ukuthi akudlalwa lapha, kuyasetshenzwa. Naye 
wakhuphula amasokisi wabhukula impela. Waqhuba kahle 
kwaze kwafika isikhathi sokuvivinywa ekupheleni konyaka. 
Nokho kwaba lula-ke ukuphendula imibuzo ngoba umsebenzi 
babewulungiselele ngempela. UDumazile waba ngomunye 
wabafundi owaphumelelayo. 

Kwakuvele kuyisifiso sakhe uDumazile ukuba abe 
ngumhlengikazi ngenkathi esakhula. Kwase kuyithuba-ke leli 
lokuba afezeke amaphupho. Wafaka isicelo sakhe kwesinye 
sezibhedlela ezinkulu eziseThekwini. Akuthathanga sikhathi 
eside, yabuya impendulo ethi makafike ngokushesha. Nempela 
kwaba njalo. 

Ngenkathi efika esibhedlela uDumazile, wayephethe incwadi 
leyo ayeyitholile. Wangena ehhovisi lomphathi, babingelelana. 
Udaba lwabe selusingathwa ngabasizi bomphathi ngoba lwase 
luphethwe yibona. Bamnikeza amafomu ukuba awagcwalise. 
Nempela wenza njalo. Kwathi angaqeda, wawabuyisela kubona 
futhi. Bamtshela ukuba alindele impendulo ehlezi ekhaya, 
bazomthinta kungekudala. Wasukuma, wabonga, waphuma. 

Ngemuva kwamasonto amathathu elindile ekhaya uDumazile, 
kwafika incwadi embizayo ukuba aphuthume afike esibhedlela 
ayoqala ukufundela ubuhlengikazi. Wajabula kabi ukuthola leyo 
ncwadi. Wayikhombisa uSithole, naye futhi wajabula. Kwabe 
sekwenziwa amalungiselelo khona manjalo. Ngakusasa ekuseni 
uSithole wavuka maqede wahambisa uDumazile esibhedlela. 
Ekufikeni kwabo, behlisa izimpahla emotweni maqede bazibeka 


lapho ayezohlala khona uDumazile. USithole wabuyela emuva 
esitolo. 

Abahlengikazi abasathwasayo bahlanganela ehholo 
ukuyotshelwa ngenqubo nenkambiso yasesibhedlela. Kwathi 
ukuba umphathi aqede ukubayala, bahlakazeka sebeya 
emakilasini abo. Bafika bafundiswa ukuthi iziguli ziphathwa 
kanjani. Kuningi nokunye abakufundayo okumayelana 
nokuhlalisana emsebenzini. Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi badedelwa 
baya emawodini ukuyokwenza lokho ababekade bekufundiswa 
emakilasini. Bawuqhuba kahle lo msebenzi baze bawujwayela. 
Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi babebuye badedelwe bodwa bahlenge 
iziguli, abahlengikazi bezihlalele emahhovisi bephumule. 

Ngelinye ilanga insizwa yakwaZuma yambuka 
uDumazile maqede yamukha. Kwacaca ukuthi uma ingase 
ithole lo sukasambe wentokazi, konke ngabe sekulungile 
futhi sekuphelele. Yahluleka wukubekezela, yazibika 
ukuhlupheka kwayo. Nokho intokazi kaNozulu yalandula 
impela. Kwakungekho nje emqondweni kaDumazile ukuthi 
bangahlukaniswa yini noMatshana. Insizwa ayiphelanga ithemba. 

Zahamba izikhathi iminyaka idedelana, sasondela isikhathi 
sokuvivinywa kokugcina. Kwakungathi yiphupho lelo 
kuDumazile. Wayezibuza kodwa ahluleke wukuziphendula 
ukuthi nguye ngempela yini lowo owayesezobizwa ngoSista. 
Wayethi uma ebuka ubuphansi bomuzi wakubo, afikelwe 
yizinyembezi. Wazimisela ukuba angabalahli abazali bakhe uma 
eseqedile ukufunda. Zaqala-ke izivivinyo. Nakuba amaphepha 
ayelukhuni impela, kodwa uDumazile wayenethemba lokuthi 
uzophumelela. Nangempela imiphumela yafika injengoba 
ayethembile. Kwenzeka konke lokho nje, noLerato akazibekile 
phansi; uphumelela kahle kakhulu ezifundweni zakhe. 
Wayengomunye wabafundi owaklonyeliswa ngesitifiketi 
sokuzinikela emsebenzini wakhe. UMtholephi wayezama naye 
ebangeni lakhe nakuba wayengafani noLerato. 


Ngenkathi uDumazile ebuyela esikoleni, washiya ehlelile 
ukuthi ngubani umuntu ozokuba yiso lakhe ekhaya; umuntu 
ozonakekela ukuphila kwabantwana kanye nesithandwa 
sakhe. Wacabangisisa uhlobo lomuntu olufanele lo msebenzi. 
Akadidekelanga ngasekufuneni umuntu osemncane. Wayemazi 
kahle uSithole ukuthi akacushwa ngaseziketini. Wabona kufanele 
ukuba afune umama osekhulakhulile; umuntu azokhululeka 
ukumshiya noSithole kungonakali lutho. Nempela wamthola 
umama osemdala nje. Wawenza ngokwethembeka umsebenzi 
wakhe wokuwasha, ukupheka kanye nokunakekela ikhaya. 
Ekuphothuleni izifundo zakhe uDumazile, wawufica umuzi 
wakhe usekuleso simo ayewushiye ukuso. 

Ngelinye ilanga uDumazile wazixoxela nje ngempilo 
ayeyibona esafundela ubuhlengikazi esibhedlela. 

“Uyazi yise kaMtho, izinga lempilo yabantu besifazane 
seliguqukile.” Athi ukuthula kancane uDumazile. 

“Liguqulwa yini?” kubuza uSithole ngoba engaqondi kahle 
ukuthi uDumazile uqondeni. 

“Wawungabona wena ngenkathi ngifika esibhedlela! Izimoto 
zazipakwa zigcwale iyadi ungafunga ukuthi ngezodokotela kanti 
phinde.” 

“Kwakungezobani kanti?” 

“Ingxenye enkulu yalezo zimoto kwakungeyabafundi 
ababefana nami nje.” 

“Beyithathe kuphi imali yokuthenga lezo zimoto zibiza 
kangaka?” Ahleke uDumazile, bese ethi: 

“Bezithengelwe ngamasoka abo. Umuntu uma ekuthanda 
ngempela, kungeve ngoba ekukhohlisa nje, udela konke 
anakho. Nami ngacabanga nje ukuthi ukuba nganginomuntu 
owayengithanda ngempela nangokweqiniso, ngabe ngathi 
ngiphuma esikoleni sasesibhedlela, ngabe sengishayela imoto.” 


Amhlaba lawo mazwi uSithole. Nokho indoda yaziqinisa. 
Wabe esezibuzisa imibuzo engatheni nje. 

“Uyakwazi yini ukushayela?” 

“Ukushayela imoto wubala. Umuntu ukufunda ngokuphazima 
kweso lokho.” USithole wacabanga, wabona kufanele ukuba 
azame imizamo yokuvala lesi sikhala esingaba yimbangela 
yokupheshukelwa yingilosi yakhe. 

Ngelinye ilanga uSithole wasuka ekhaya waqonda egalaji 
ukuyokhetha uhlobo oluthile lwemoto. Nempela wayibona, 
wayithanda. Yayibiza yona, kodwa kwakungelutho lokho, inqobo 
nje uma ejabulise isithandwa sakhe. Wake wacabanga ukuthi 
ayikhokhe yonke imali, kodwa wabuye waguqula umqondo. 
Wabona ukuthi impahla seyithanda ukukhopheka esitolo, 
ngaleyo ndlela wahlela ukuthatha ingxenye enkulu yemali 
agcwalise ngayo impahla esitolo. Wathatha ingxenye yesine 
yemali yakhe wakhokhela imoto. Wabhalisa imininingwane 
yokuthi uzokhokha kanjani ngenyanga. Wabambisa nangesitolo 
sakhe ukuthi uma kwenzeka ehluleka ukukhokha, kuyodliwa 
sona. Nokho-ke uMondise omkhulu wayenzela ukugcwalisa 
amaphepha nje. Wayengaboni ukuthi kungadalwa yini ukuba 
ahluleke ukukhokha okwakungenza kudliwe isitolo sakhe. 

Langa limbe uDumazile ezihlalele endlini, wezwa ihudi 
yemoto ithi papabhu ebaleni. Wathi lacu, walunguza. Wakhangwa 
wunyonyovu lwemoto selugcwele igceke. USithole waphuma 
phakathi, wama eceleni kwayo. UDumazile wasondela kuyena. 

“Mntakwethu, yisipho sakho lesi. Nanku nomakhalekhukhwini 
futhi.” UDumazile wajabula ngendlela yokuthi wahluleka 
ukuzibamba. Wazithola esegomothela uSithole emanga. “What a 
surprise!” 

“Manjena kufanele siye endaweni evulekile ukuze 
ngikukhombise kahle ukuthi ishayelwa kanjani. Kulula nje ngoba 
yona iyazishintsha; wena owakho umsebenzi wukuqondisa 


amasondo nje.” UDumazile kwakuthi akahlanye ngenxa 
yenjabulo. Kwathi emini yantambama, bashona khona 
enkundleni kanobhutshuzwayo ukuyofundisana. Akuthathanga 
sikhathi eside, uDumazile wazizwa esengumpetha. Yathi isibuyela 
ekhaya imoto yabe seyishayelwa nguDumazile. 

Kwadlula izinsukwana nje kwafika incwadi ivela esibhedlela. 
Leyo ncwadi yayisiyimpendulo yesicelo ayesenzile sokufuna 
umsebenzi. Babemazisa-ke ukuthi makafike ukuzoqala 
umsebenzi. Wabe esenza amalungiselelo khona manjalo. 
Ngakusasa ekuseni uDumazile washesha ukuvuka. Kwathi 
ukuba aqede ukuhlamba umzimba, waphuza itiye. Kwathi 
angaqeda, wagqoka, waphuma endlini wangena emotweni, zaya 
esephikelele esibhedlela. Wathi efika, wagcwalisa imininingwane 
ephathelene nokuqala umsebenzi. Bamnikeza indawo lapho 
ayezosebenzela khona. 

Ingakapheli inyanga uDumazile eqalile ukusebenza, 
shayisiyane yena emgwaqweni. Wangena ngemuva emotweni 
yomlungu yohlobo oluphambili. Nayo futhi leyo moto yashayisa 
engaphambi kwayo. Zalimala zaphela izimoto. Kwenzeka 
le nhlekelele nje yingoba uDumazile wayenganakile ukuthi 
kufanele ame ezibanini zomgwaqo. Wayekhuluma ocingweni 
olungumakhalekhukhwini. Amaphoyisa afika ngokuphazima 
kweso, abhalisa yonke imininingwane. Izimoto zona zasuka 
sezidonswa. 

UDumazile wafika ekhaya wabikela uSithole ngokushayisa 
kwakhe. Wathi uma elibuka leli cala uSithole, wabona ukuthi 
uDumazile ngeke adabule, lizomchitha. Wazimisela ukuba 
lithwalwe nguyena. Wenza imizamo yokuba lolu daba luphele 
ngaphandle kwenkantolo. Ngakusasa ekuseni wavuka waqonda 
emaphoyiseni ukuyothola imininingwane yabaninizimoto ezabe 
zilimalile. Nempela wafika wayithola. Wabashayela izingcingo 
ukuba bafike emaphoyiseni. Ngenhlanhla enkulu wabathola, 
bafika. Bakha isivumelwano phambi komthetho sokuthi yena 
wakoMatshana uyazibophezela ukuthi uyozithwala zonke 


izindleko ezidalwe wukushayela budedengu kukaDumazile. 
Bavumelana-ke ukuthi icala lizophela ngaphandle kokuya 
enkantolo. 

USithole waqala-ke ukukhokha amanconzunconzu. Imoto 
yomlungu yabiza imali eshisiwe ukuyilungisa. Imali yakhe 
ebhange yayiya ngokuya ihwabheka. Nokho ithemba lakhe lonke 
lase lisesitolo. Sasiyenza sona imali, kuyihhinikazi uqobo lwalo. 
Ngosuku lwempesheni nje wayelala ebomvu, kwazise phela 
kwakuholelwa esitolo sakhe. 

Ngelinye ilanga uDumazile wafikelwa wumcabango wokuthi
