angahlomula kanjani emalini kaSithole engena lapha esitolo. 

“Lesi sitolo siyayenza phela imali; siyenza ngempela. Ngisuka 
kude kabi naso. Ngempela bekufanele uSithole abonge kumina 
njengoba enzile nje. Lesi sitolo sesikhule sadlondlobala kangaka 
nje kungenxa yami. Ngangiyiwozawoza kazibuthe ezinsizweni. 
Zazifika zidedelana zizozithengisa ugwayi nokunye, kanti 
zaziqonde ukuzozibika kimina. Impahla esitolo yayihamba 
ubuthaphuthaphu, uSithole alale ebomvu. Futhi mina 
nganginekhono elihle lokuxoxisana nabathengi. Ngamakhela 
phela uSithole umsebenzi wakhe. Kuzofanela ngihlele nephoyisa 
uMkhize ukuze angaphazamisi uma sengenza izinto zami. 
Imali engiyoyithola ngaleli cebo lami ngiyothengela ubaba 
umhlahlavana wemoto, esalayo ngivule ngayo isaluni. INkosi 
isiyongixolela bandla, imali ngiyayidinga. Okumnandi-ke wukuthi 
uSithole ngeke yena ashone kumbe alahlekelwe yilutho ngoba 
umshuwalense uyokhokha.” 

Langa limbe kwenzeka ukuba impesheni iqondane 
noLwesihlanu lokuphela kwenyanga. USithole wayexakeke 
ngendlela yokuthi wayengakwazi ukunyakaza esitolo. 
Nangakusasa ngoMgqibelo kwakuseyiso sona leso; abantu 
kunyamfuka bezothenga, abanye bezokhokha izikweletu zabo. 
Wayengakhohliwe uSithole ukuthi kwakufanele aye kokhokhela 
isitifiketi somshuwalense wesitolo ebhange. Wayenesibopho 


sokuwukhokhela lo mshuwalense njalo ekupheleni kwenyanga 
kumbe ngaphambi kokuba iphele. Waziduduza-ke ngokuthi 
useyoze aye ebhange ngoLwesibili zizine enyangeni elandelayo 
njengoba kuyobe kuyiholide ngoMsombuluko. 

Entathakusa yangoLwesibili, uSithole wathola ucingo 
esalele. Lwaluvela kumuntu mumbe ongazishongo igama, luthi 
akaphuthume esitolo kukhona umonakalo owenzekile. Nempela 
wavuka, wagqoka, wadumisa imoto, yasuka seyiphikelele khona. 
Wathi eqhamuka, wakhangwa yizicimamlilo seziqedela ukucisha 
lokho okwakusalokolokoza. Isitolo sona sase sishe sangqongqa, 
sekusele nje amagebedu ezindonga. USithole wasangana 
ukusangana. 

Ngemuva kokubhalisa isitatimende sobunikazi sitolo uSithole, 
amaphoyisa aqala ukwenza uphenyo. Aqala ngonogada 
owayeqaphe isitolo ebusuku. Waziphendulela-ke oweNkosi: 

“Kufike abantu abalinganiselwa eshumini ebusuku bayizolo 
bathi angilale ngesisu phansi emhlabathini. Ngigologolozile, 
baqhumisa isibhamu. Ngalala-ke mina. Babulala isicabha. 
Ngathi ngizama ukumemeza, bangishaya ngesidunu sesibhamu. 
Ngathula. Isicabha saklayeka, savuleka. Bangena. Batapa, batapa 
batapa impahla. Ngithe ngibona kwaqhamuka umhuqa weloli, 
kwalayishwa kulo impahla. Ekuqedeni kwabo, laduma, lasuka 
lamela buqamamana. Behla, babuya sebehamba ngezinyawo 
bephethe isipakupaku sikaphethilomu. Bawuthela endaweni 
yezingubo, balayitha, kwalanguka amalangabi. Basuka babaleka 
bangena elolini, bakhala bemuka. Ngavuka phansi ngacela 
usizo ukuba kuthintwe uSithole. Kwathintwa amaphoyisa kanye 
nezicimamlilo. Yilokho-ke engikwaziyo okwenzekile.” 

Kubonakale nje ukuthi umngqayi usethukile. Baningi 
abantu abaphenywa emphakathini. UMaNzimande yena 
waba ngumsolwa wokuqala. Wathathwa waya kophenywa 
emaphoyiseni. Abutholakalanga ubufakazi obumhlanganisa 
nalesi sigameko. Nokho imbokodebomvu yayilokhu iqhubekile 


nokuthungatha umkhondo. 

USithole waphikelela ebhange ukuyokhokhela isitifiketi 
somshuwalense wesitolo. Walubika-ke udaba lokusha kwaso. 
Kuthe uma echaza ukuthi kwenzeke nini kanjani, bamtshela ukuthi 
inkampani yabo ngeke ikwazi ukumkhokhela ngoba isitolo sakhe 
besingasavikelekile. Imali leyo eyisivumelwano sokuvikela isitolo 
uma siba nenkinga, ikhokhwa ebhange ekupheleni kwenyanga 
kumbe ngaphambi kokuba iphele, hhayi manje njengoba uSithole 
efika nayo ngalesi sikhathi. Balulandula usizo uSithole angase 
aluthole kubona. Wakhala ezithulisa okaMatshana. 

Kwaduma ikhanda kuSithole engazi ukuthi kufanele athatheni 
ahlanganise nani ukuze aphile. Insengwakazi yayisishelwe 
wubisi. Wagcina ebone kufanele ukuba agqobhe isigqala ukuze 
impilo iqhubeke. Wavuka ekuseni waphikelela emapulazini 
ukuyofuna izinto zokudayisa. Wabuya notamatisi, amaklabishi, 
amazambane kanye nesipinashi wadayisela abezitolo. Wabuye 
walanda izinkuni ehlathini wazidayisela labo abazidingayo. 
Kwagcina sekuyimpilo yakhe ukusebenzisa iveni ukuthuthela 
abantu abakhayo usimende, isihlabathi, izitini kanye nokunye nje 
okusindayo. Wayeyithola imadlana yokuphila. 

Iveni likaSithole lase lisebenza umsebenzi ongaphezulu 
kwamandla alo. Laqala ukuzwela. Muveni nje injini yalo yase 
iphelile. Kwakuthi uma lihamba emgwaqweni kuthaphuke 
isikhatha sentuthu ngemuva. Wayesehlala ephethe igalani 
lamafutha. Kwenzeka konke lokhu nje injini isiqalile 
ukuhlanganisa amanzi namafutha. Amagiya nawo ayengasathandi 
ukungena ngenkululeko. Uma kwenzekile ngenhlanhla langena, 
kwakudingeka alibambe, kungenjalo lizoqhasha. Nodifu 
wawusunomsindo uma ihamba. Nesimo sokubukeka komzimba 
sasingasaginyisi mathe, kuwumdlekedleke nje. Iphoyisa 
lomgwaqo laliyibona iseza, liphakamise isandla, liyikhombe 
eceleni, kwenzeke-ke lokho. Lagcina likhishiwe emgwaqweni, 
lazalela izinkukhu ebaleni. 


Zahamba izikhathi saguquka isimo sezinto. USithole 
wayengasenamali. Kwase kuyisinxibi, impabanga uqobo 
lwayo. Umsebenzi ayesewenza kwakuba wukuvuka ekuseni 
adidizele ebaleni kuze kubuye uDumazile emsebenzini 
ntambama. Isithunzi sakhe sobunjinga, ukwethembeka kanye 
nokuhlonipheka saya ngokuya sishabalala. Wagcina naye 
esezibona eyinto engenamkhuba walutho. Waqala ukuba 
azinikele ophuzweni oludakayo. Pho utshwala buyakwazi 
ukuzakhela ikhehlana labo! NoSithole wawungafunga ukuthi 
ngelidala ixhegu leli. Into ayeseyikhuthalele kwakuba yikho 
ukuvuka ekuseni ahequnge imizi edayisa uphuzo olunamandla. 
Nalapho njalo kwakungasho ukuthi wayefika athenge, kodwa 
wayelinda abathengayo bese ecela kubona. Kwesinye isikhathi 
wayeba nosizo khona ejoyintini, bese bemuthi phohlo injongo. 

Kwakuye kuthi uma esebuyela kwakhe uSithole, abe 
noDumazile shaqa. Wayeseqale umkhuba omusha wokumchapha 
ngenhlamba, kwesinye isikhathi ambeke nesandla. Onesi 
ababhenywa-ke bengensangu. UDumazile wathula ecabanga: 

“Kodwa ngiyofa nini nje ngilokhu ngibhoklozwa yilesi 
sikhondlakhondla sikamabhongendlini? Le nto iyazingcolisa 
injalo nje uma ilele! Ngubani umuntu ozomela ukunazingana 
nokuntokanjana nendoda endala kangaka ibe ingaguli? 
Ngiyayehla mina le bhasi.” UDumazile waqala ukulala 
ekamelweni lakhe nezingane zakhe. USithole washiywa yedwa 
ekamelweni elikhulu. Wayixoxa le ndaba kubangani bakhe 
emsebenzini uDumazile. Bamtshela ekhaleni ukuba ahlukane 
nendoda kaMaNzimande. UDumazile wagcina naye esembona 
uSithole ukuthi uyindoda kaMaNzimande. 

Kwenzeka konke lokhu nje umfo kaMsholozi akamnike thuba, 
kodwa umfuna endlini. Kwala noma uDumazile echaza ukuthi 
usengunina wezingane ezimbili, umfo kaNxamalala wayesevaleke 
izindlebe, engasezwa nakuzwa. 

“Ngijatshuliswa wukuthi wethembekile. Wazikhulelwa, 


wazibeletha, wazikhulisa, zaphila. Maningi amantombazane 
lapha phandle angenazo izingane, kodwa lokho okungasho 
ukuthi ayizintombi nto. Kwenzeka ntoni ebuntombini bazo? 
Ziningi izisu ezihushulwayo, izingane zifakwe ezitamkokweni. 
Mina ngiyagculiswa yisimo sonke osungichazele sona. Ngizimisele 
ukukuthatha nakho konke onakho. Futhi izingane zakho 
kuyokuba ngezami nami.” Kwaduma ikhanda kuDumazile, 
wasangana ukusangana lokhu. 

UMtalaselwa Zuma wayengomunye wabashayeli bamaambulense 
akhona lapha esibhedlela. Waqala ukweshela 
uDumazile ngenkathi esafika ukuzofundela ubuhlengikazi 
kuso lesi sibhedlela. Nokho uDumazile wayelokhu emphike 
njalo umfo kaMsholozi. OkaNxamalala wayelokhu ephikelele, 
eyilandele intokazi lena. Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi inhlansi 
yothando yaya ngokuya ilokoza enhliziyweni kaDumazile, 
yadlonga yadlondlobala. UDumazile wabona sekufanele ukuba 
amazise uMtalaselwa ukuthi usemehlulile. 

UDumazile waqala ukuhlukumeza uSithole ngezindlela 
ezahlukene. Wayevele azihambele nje ekhaya angabiki kumuntu 
ukuthi uyaphi futhi uyobuya nini. Wayezibuyela ngesikhathi 
esithandwa nguyena. USithole wahluleka ukubekezelela leyo nto. 
Ngelinye ilanga wagcina ebuzile: 

“Kanti wena uphuma ngasikhathi sini emsebenzini?” 

“Ubuzelani?” esho uDumazile esebiphe esengubani! 
Izinhlonze seziyimivingqi esiphongweni. 

“Ngisho ngoba angisaqondi nqindi nasibhakela manje. 
Namhlanjena usheshile ukubuya. Izolo uphuzile ukufika, wafika 
sengilele, wabuye wahamba ngingakavuki. Kuthangi awubuyanga 
kwanhlobo. Ngabe sengishaya ucingo ngibuza esibhedlela ukuthi 
bakubambise i-ova yini, kodwa baphika. Sekuyangicacela-ke 
manje ukuthi kukhona lapho wena wawukade uye khona.” 

“Ungabozixaka uzixukuze ngami. Mina ngiyisosha 


elizikhuzayo. Angithi uyabona lapha emunweni wami ukuthi 
angifake lucingo lwamuntu? Khohlwa-ke wukunakana nentombi 
kaNozulu nesikhathi efika ngaso.” 

Wajuluka bume uSithole uma ecabanga ukuthi yini lena 
emvelelayo. Wehlisa umoya. Wacabanga: 

“Kusho ukuthi uDumazile ufuna ukuba sishade naye ukuze 
ngikwazi ukuba nezwi kuyena. Nakhu ekhala ngobungekho 
bendandatho emunweni. Ehhe kusho lokho. Uyawufuna 
umshado.” Washo kwezwakala: 

“Kuzofanela siye kini siyohlela usuku lomshado.” 

“Ini? Ushade nobani? Angithi wena uyindoda 

kaMaNzimande?” Aqale athule uSithole. Wabe esezwakala ethi: 

“Ngizozama ukumdivoza uMaNzimande.” 

“Uyakwazi ukudivosa ukuthi kubiza malini? Ngiyabuza, 
uyakwazi? Wawuhlaleleni ungamdivosi uMaNzimande? Sekuthi 
ngoba sewunguLazaru sewubona kufanele ukuba udivose? 
Phinde, phindela kuyena!” 

“Ukhuluma kanjani uma ukhuluma kanjena mntakwethu?” 
kubalisa uSithole ezama ukuzehlisa ngoba eyibona seyiqonge 
kakhulu intokazi lena. 

“Angiseyena umntakwenu mina. Sengizitholele i-boyfriendethi 
mina!” Asho aze ambambathe isifuba emabeleni. 

Wacishe waquleka uSithole ngenkathi ezwa lawo mazwi. 
Wacabanga ngezimali zakhe azidulela kuDumazile ezama 
ukumenza abe ngcono. Kuleyo mizuzwana nje kwazwakala 
ukungqongqoza ngesankahlu esicabheni. UDumazile wathi lacu, 
wavula. Kwangena ezembokodwebomvu zihlome zithe shi. 
Azibange zisachitha sikhathi: 

“Singamthola uSithole?” UDumazile waphenduka wabheka 
ngakuSithole ukukhombisa ukuthi nangu. Yayingasekho-ke enye 
indlela kuMatshana ngaphandle kokuzisho. 


“Yimina uSithole.” 

“Uyayikhumbula imoto yomlungu eyashayiswa yimoto 
yakho?” Athi dlengelele uSithole, kodwa asheshe akhumbule 
ukuthi konje imoto eyayikade iyisipho sikaDumazile yayisabiza 

yena emabhukwini, futhi necala layo lalibhaliswe ngaye. 

“Yebo ngiyakhumbula!” 

“Isivumelwano sakho nomninimoto sathi wena uyozithwala 
zonke izindleko ezadalekayo lapho. Umlungu usefake icala 
lokuthi wena wasephula leso sivumelwano. Ngakho-ke umthetho 
wenkantolo uthi asikufake ozankosi, sihambe nawe khona 
manje ukuze uchazele imantshi, yona ichazele umlungu ukuthi 
awusigcinanga ngani isivumelwano leso.” 

“Manje makhos..” 

“Hheyi, uyolanda phambili!” Bamdumela, bamfaka ozankosi, 
baphuma naye. Bamphushela phakathi evenini eyayimi phandle, 
bavala. Yaduma, yakhala yemuka. 

Kwasala kwafika abasebhange bezokudla imoto eyayiyisipho 
sikaDumazile. Bafika nojibha bayihudula. 

Ukuboshwa kukaSithole ngemuva kokwaliwa kwakhe 
wuDumazile, kwanikeza uMtalaselwa ithuba lokuba 
angene ngonoqhakala emzini kaDumazile. USithole phela 
wayesewubhalise ngaye umuzi, itayitela selibiza yena uDumazile. 
UMtalaselwa wayesecabange waqeda ukuthi usefuna ukwakha 
umuzi. Babonisana-ke nesixebe sakhe ngokungena kulesi sigaba. 
Bagcina bevumelene ngokuthi yilowo nayilowo makaye kubo 
ukuyobika lolu daba. Nempela kwaba njalo. 

Ngenkathi uMtalaselwa efika ekhaya, abazali bakhe 
babezihlalele nje botha imbuthuma. Bajabula kabi ukubona 
indodana yabo. UMtalaselwa wabe eseyixoxa-ke indaba. 

“Kunentombazane yakwaKheswa esengiyibonile engifuna 
ukwakha nayo umuzi; ingusista esibhedlela. Bengicabanga 


ukuthumela abakhongi mbayimbayi.” Athi ukuthula kancane 
esafuna ukubona ukuthi abazali bakhe bayizwa kanjani le ndaba. 
Bake bathi ukuthula nabo besacabanga. Kwabe sekuthatha unina 
wathi: 

“Ngeyakuphi leyo ntombi?” 

“NgeyaseMzimkhulu.” 

“Uthi kodwa intombi yakoMzimkhulu iyokwazi ukuqwala 

le mimango engaka nenyanda yezinkuni ekhanda mntanami?” 
Ahleke kancane uMtalaselwa, bese ethi: 

“Iyokwazi.” Unina bese ebheka ngakumyeni wakhe, athi: 

“Yise kaMtalaselwa, sekungawe baba. Kusho ukuthi izinkomo 
kufanele ziphume zonke esibayeni.” 

“Uthi akuyona intombi yenkosi nje leyo pho?” 

“Usho ngani yise kaMtalaselwa?” 

“Ngisho phela uma sesizophuma sonke isibaya. Kubiza 
kabi ukulobola intombi yenkosi. Awadlali amashumi amathi 
ezinkomo,” esho emisa iminwe emibili. Kwabe sekuphendula 
yena uMtalaselwa. 

“Cha baba, akuyona intombi yenkosi. Abazali bayo ngabantu 
nje phaqa. Futhi ningesabi, nezinkomo zayo azisaphelele.” 

Athi dlengelele unina, bese ethi: 

“Usho ukuthini uma uthi izinkomo zayo azisaphelele?” 

“Ngisho ukuthi isinemilanjwana.” Kwake kwathuleka endlini 
kungekho ofuna ukukhuluma. Kwathi ekugcineni kwezwakala 
unina ethi: 

“Mntanami, iphulaphiko pho? Bese kuphele izintombi yini 
kodwa? Mh, uyazi ukuthi kwakuba yintombi yamakhehla leyo 
emandulo?” Athelwe ngamahloni uMtalaselwa, abheke phansi 
ecabanga ukuthi kuyihlazo kangakanani endaweni yakubo 
ukuganwa yigqinkehli. Unina wabe esethatha ethi: 


“Uthi uyawazi kahle amaqhashamlenze ukuthi ahlupha kanjani 
mntanami?” Aphakamise amehlo kancane uMtalaselwa, bese ethi: 

“Ahlupha ngani?” 

“Awahlukani noyise babantwana bawo. Mntanami ngifuna 
ungizwe kahle, mina angisho ukuthi yehlukana nale ntombazane 
yakwaKheswa uma wena uyithanda. Engikushoyo ngithi kufanele 
ulindele-ke phela ukuba nozakwenu.” Athule uMtalaselwa 
ecabanga indlela unina alisebenzise ngayo leli gama. Wabe 
esethatha ethi: 

“Angisezwa-ke manje mama. Kanti akubona abantu besifazane 
ababizana ngozakwabo uma begane indoda eyodwa?” 

“Ehhene mntanami, uqinisile. Uma phela nani bantu besilisa 
senihlangene kumuntu oyedwa wesifazane ngizothini?” Athule 
ebheke phansi uMtalaselwa. Unina waphendukela kumyeni 
wakhe, wathi: 

“Yise kaMtalaselwa, wathula nje?” 

“Nami bengisacabanga ngentokazi kaManzini lena 
enomntwana wakhe. Iyahlonipha kabi leya ngane yomuntu!” 

“Inyanda eyithwalayo yezinkuni angeke wena wakwazi 
ukuyisukumisa phansi. Yisikhukhula sikamhlola lesi, umfazi 
uqobo lwakhe.” Uyise wabe esephendukela ngakuyena 
uMtalaselwa, wathi: 

“Mfana wami, uyekeleni ukuganisa le ngane yakwaZungu?” 
Kwaphendula umkakhe kuqala: 

“Angithi phela ubona ukuthi ayifundile yona. Kanti imfundo 
ayisho lutho nje. Nakhu thina asifundile, kodwa siyakhile imizi.” 
Athi ukuthula kancane esagwinya amathe. Wathatha wathi: 

“Ngabe kungcono ukuba umntanami uvele wathatha yona 
intokazi kaZungu, hhayi umhlola lona. Amaqhasha ahlupha kabi, 
ahluphisa okwamadikazi.” 


UMtalaselwa wayengasaphenduli lutho, esethule du. Abazali 
bakhe baqhubeka nokuzixoxela bodwa. 

“MaShandu, uMtalaselwa useyindoda manjena, usekhule 
ngokwanele. Kukuyena ukuzikhethela umfazi wakhe. Thina 
asinawo amandla okumkhethela umfazi.” 

Kwathi cosololo kuMtalaselwa uma ezwa lawo mazwi evela 
kuyise. 

“Yise kaMtalaselwa, ukhuluma kanjani uma ukhuluma 
kanjena? Usho ukuthi asinakukhuluma lutho ngisho noma 
umntwana eseqhamuka neHhanana?” 

“Angisho phela ukuthi singamvumela uma eletha 
abakoMyekwana phakathi komuzi kababa, kodwa bengiphawula 
nje.” 

“Siyoyicela ivuthiwe!” UMtalaselwa wabe esecacisa ukuthi 
ubefisa ukuba abakhongi bathunyelwe nini ukuyokokhela 
umlilo. Wahlela ukuba abakhongi abathathe khona elokishini 
lakwaMakhutha lapho ayeqashe khona ikamelo. Unina walungisa 
okuya ngasethunjini, badla. Kwathi bangaqeda, uMtalaselwa 
wavalelisa, waphuma eseyogibela amathekisi aphindela emuva. 

UDumazile wafika kubo kukhona unina kuphela. Uyise 
wayesalukile eyozifunela izichibi ematshwaleni. Walubeka-ke 
udaba lwakhe kunina: 

“Mama, sengithole umuntu ozimisele ngomshado ngami.” 

“Owakwabani lowo muntu?” 

“OwakwaZuma mama kwaJilafohlo, ngaphansi kwentaba 

iNgilanyoni kwelaseMid-Illovo.” 

“Sewuke waya yini kuleyo ndawo wayazi kangaka?” 

“Cha mama. Usho ngani?” 

“Bengibuza nje mntanami. Jila fohlo! Kazi kwakuluhlobo 

luni lwendawo lolo? Kodwa mntanami uthi uyokwazi ukuhlala 


kuleyo ndawo? Ngizwa igama layo nje sengathi ngamahhelekehle 
amaqele.” 

“Ngeke mina ngihlale lapho. Nginomuzi wami eMafezini 
eMlazi.” 

“Phela mntanami kuyokuya ngokuthi umkhwenyana uthini. 
Uma ekukhomba lena emakhaya, kufanele uye khona.” Anikine 
ikhanda uDumazile. 

“Uthe uyofika nini umfokazi ndini lowo?” 

“Ubezimisele ukufika ekupheleni kwenyanga yona lena 
esiyiphetheyo.” 

“Ngiyezwa mntanami, kodwa ayikho into engingayinquma 
ngingedwa. Ngizolinda yena uyihlo ukuze sibonisane naye.”

 Akuthathanga sikhathi eside waqhamuka uyise. Ngenhlanhla 
wafika ekahle nje engemnandi kangako. UMaNdovela wabe 
eselubeka-ke udaba lwendodakazi yabo: 

“Yise kaDumazile, indodakazi yakho seyifuna ukusilethela 
izinkomo.” 

“Ini?” esho sengathi akezwanga kahle. UMaNdovela 
waphendukela ngakuDumazile, wathi: 

“Mtshele uyihlo.” UDumazile waba namahloni, waphendula 
ngokuthi: 

“Mtshele wena ma!”Wayilanda-ke indaba uMaNdovela. Wake 
wathula uKheswa esacabanga. Ekugcineni wazwakala esethi: 

“UDumazile uqiniseke kangakanani ukuthi leli huzu lakhe 
lithembekile?” UMaNdovela waphendukela ngakuyena 
uDumazile, wathi: 

“Ziphendulele Dumazile.” Ahleke kancane uDumazile bese 
ekhophoza. 

“Kuzofanela sibonisane kahle ngezibizo kanye nelobolo 
MaNdovela. Mina ngendodakazi yami ngifuna ihhashi nesihlalo 


salo kanye nemvubu. Ngifuna futhi bangithengele imbilijisi kanye 
namagomazi. Izinkomo ngiyofuna zibe yisikhombisa zoboya, 
bese beleka ngeshumi lezimbuzi kanye nesikhwehlela. Emveni 
kwalokho-ke sengingamshadisa umkhwenyana.” 

“Yise kaDumazile, mina bengibona ngenye indlela. Kunganjani 
sivele sibize isizumbulu semali esihlanganisa lonke ilobolo?” 

“Ukushiso yini lokho MaNdovela?” 

“Ukucucuza ilobolo kuchitha isikhathi futhi kubambezela 
umkhwenyana elokhu eqoqa lokhu nalokhuya. Okunye-ke futhi 
kugcina sekuvele namahlazo nje.” 

“Amahlazo anjani MaNdovela?” 

“Amahlazo phela yise kaDumazile anjengokuthi nje 
umkhwenyana aveze ukuthi ngeke ayikhokhe inkomo kamama 
ngoba kuwukuthi nokuthi nokuthi. Uyayibona nje leyo nto yise 
kaDumazile.” 

“Kuyezwakala khona uma sewubeka. Bewufuna sibize malinike 
ngokwakho?” 

“Mina bengibona ukuthi akufanele ukuba simbize kakhulu 
umkhwenyana ngoba indodakazi yethu ayisaphelele. Futhi 
eqinisweni umuntu akathengwa yise kaDumazile, kusuke 
kwakhiwa ubuhlobo nje. Asikho-ke isidingo sokuba umuntu 
umumbe eqolo. Uma uhlupheka, hlala nje nokuhlupheka kwakho. 
Ungacabangi ukuthi ukugana kwendodakazi yakho sekusho 
ukubamba umjaho wamahhashi kuwena.” 

“Angazi noma uwuzwe kahle yini umbuzo wami? Ngithe 

bewufuna simbize malini umkhwenyana?” 

“Angazi phela yise kaDumazile, nquma wena njengendoda.” 

“Ngakube simbize kakhulu uma sithi akakhokhe 
izinkulungwane ezinti?” esho emisa impama yonke. Athi ukuthula 
kancane uMaNdovela, bese ethi: 


“Sengathi ilungile yise kaDumazile. Inkosi, ilungile. Kanti 
yena usengamane afune ukuphiwa umfazi nje?” UMaNdovela 
waphendukela ngakuDumazile, wathatha wathi: 

“Utshele umfokazi lowo ukuthi imali iyaphathwa lapha, 
akudlalwa. Uma engenayo, angezi kwakuza nje.” Bahleke 
bobabili. UDumazile wasukuma, wavalelisa,waphuma 
esephikelele eMlazi.

 Ngakusasa uDumazile wahlangana noMtalaselwa esibhedlela 
ngesikhathi senhlabakhefu. Bathathana besalula izinyawo nje. 
Babehamba bezixoxela baze bafika endaweni yokuphumula 
ngaphansi kwemithi. 

“Uhambe kanjani ekhaya mntakwethu?” kubuza uMtalaselwa. 

“Ngihambe kahle sweetheart, wena?” 

“Nami ngihambe kahle. Ngibatshelile ukuthi ngizothumela 
abakhongi ekupheleni kwenyanga. Hhayi ayibanga khona 
inkinga.” Bazihlalela kamnandi ngaphansi kwemithi kwaze 
kwashaya isikhathi sokubuyela emsebenzini. Balulangazelela-ke 
lolo suku lokuphela kwenyanga. 

Zahamba izinsuku lwafika usuku olwabe lulindelwe. 
Abakhongi batheleka ngesikhathi senhlazane emagcekeni 
akwaKheswa eMzimkhulu. Bakhuleka, bawathamunda ngemibala 
yawo amabheka. Kwaphuma ingane endlini yabatshela ukuba 
bangene. Nempela benza njalo. Baphinda futhi bawathamunda 
amabheka sebengaphakathi. UKheswa wathumela ukuba 
kubizwe amantombazane onke ukuze abakhongi bakhombe 
okuyiyona abazoyilobola. Nempela afika amantombazane, 
ahlala phansi ngasesinini sawomame. Abakhongi bamkhomba-ke 
umakoti wabo ngendlela yakhona. Amantombazane asukuma, 
aphuma futhi. Umfowabo kaKheswa wabatshela-ke abakhongi 
ukuthi isibizo selobolo siyimalini. Bajabula banconcoza 
abakhongi ukuthola umtitilizo kamazitapele onjena. Bayikhiphake 
imali beyibhacaza esicephini. Kwathi bangaqeda abakhongi, 


abakwaKheswa bayiqoqa yonke imali bayikhweza. Kwakikiza 
omame kwakuhle kwanjeyaya. 

Abakhongi babona kufanele ukuba balisebenzise leli thuba 
ukuba baxoxisane nabalingani babo ngosuku lomshado. 
Bavumelana ngokuthi kufanele kudlule amasonto amabili bese 
behlangana kumfundisi ababhale. Bathi umshado omkhulu 
uyobuye ulandele. Babonga. Kwakhishwa okuya ngasethunjini, 
bathi choko choko nje basheshe bayeka. Basukuma, bavalelisa, 
baphuma. 

UDumazile wajabula kabi ukubona abazali bakhe bethokozile. 
Kwakukade kuyiphupho lakhe lelo ukuba abazali bakhe bathole 
okuthile futhi badle ngaye. Wababonga kakhulu ngokuba 
bengazange bamumbe eqolo umkhwenyana wakhe. Nabo futhi 
abazali bakhe uDumazile bajabula kakhulu ukubona indodakazi 
yabo igcina seyimtholile umkhwenyana wangempela. 

Ngenkathi abakhongi befika kwaMakhutha, babikela 
uMtalaselwa ukuthi bahambe kanjani. Abayivalanga imilomo 
ngombuso ababenawo kanye nempatho nje jikelele. Naye 
uMtalaselwa wajabula kakhulu ukuzwa izindaba ezimnandi 
ngekhwe lakhe. Kwabe sekukhishwa-ke ukudla neziphuzo 
ezinhlobonhlobo. Bazicima, bazicima abakhongi kwaze kwaba 
yiyo leyo nkathi. Omakhelwane nabo bafika bezozibethela. 
Akuthathanga sikhathi eside kwabe sekuzalela ihlokohloko 
endlini. Babusa kamnandi abantu beNkosi baze bahlukaniswa 
wukuhlwa. UMtalaselwa wabe esehlela ukuthi uzobathumelela 
kanjani abazali bakhe ngohlelo lomshado. 

Zahamba izinsuku wamenyezelwa umshado esontweni. 
Imindeni nxazombili yayilokhu imincile icabanga ukuthi 
kungavela sichiphatheki simbe siwumise umshado. Nokhoke 
lwaze lwafika usuku olwabe lulindelwe. Kwahlanganelwa 
esontweni limbe eThekwini. Umfundisi walibopha ifindo 
lomshado ngaphandle kokuphazamiseka. Kwathi angaqeda, 
abantu baphuma bakhukhusa sebephikelele kwaJilafohlo lapho 


babelindelwe khona ngamehlo abomvu. Bafika benza umkhuleko 
omfushane, babe sebethola okuya ngasethunjini. Kwabe 
sekulandela iziphuzo ezinhlobonhlobo. Kwathi bangaqeda, 
bahlakazeka abantu. 

UMtalaselwa benomkakhe bahlala isonto elilodwa 
ekhaya. Babekade becele izinsukwana zokuba bangabi bikho 
emsebenzini. Kwathi ukuba ziphele lezo zinsuku, babuyela 
emuva. Bavumelana ngokuthi bazohlala bobabili eMafezini 
eMlazi. Labe selivaleka-ke ikamelo likaMtalaselwa elokishini 
kwaMakhutha. 


ISAHLUKO SESISHIYAGALOMBILI 

USithole wahlala ejele izinyanga eziyisithupha edonsa 
kanzima. Kwakungathi uyaphupha ngosuku lokugcina ngenkathi 
iphoyisa limtshela ukuthi isigwebo sakhe sesiphelile. Wake 
wathula ecabanga ngobunzima ayesebuthwalile: elala edle 
ukudla okungagculisi, alale ngompisimpisana omantwentwesana 
nje, ehlukunyezwa ngezinye iziboshwa. Kwathi khona 
esekhumula izikhindi zasejele, esegqoka izingubo zakhe, wabona 
ngempela ukuthi useyagoduka. 

USithole wathathwa yiveni yamaphoyisa yaze yayombeka 
eSiphingo. Waqale wangakholwa kahle ukuthi ngakube nguyena 
ngempela yini lona oselapha. Kwakungathi usangene ngenkathi 
ebona abantu ayekade abagcina. Wabaxoxela ngosizi lwakhe 
lwasejele kanye nokungabi namali. Abanye babemdabukela 
bamuphe imali, kodwa abanye babebika usizi lwabo nabo. Wake 
wathula esacabanga: 

“Ngakube yimina lona osemukela imali njengesinxibi, 
impabanga uqobo lwayo? Mina lo engangibhenka izishaqane 
zezizumbulu zezimali? Yekanini kuhlupheka! Yimina lona 
osesongwe ngumhlaba kanjena? Khona ngisenayo indawo 
yokuhlala kulo mhlaba ohlabayo? Uma ngisuka lapha eSiphingo 
ngizolibhekisa kuphi? Ngiye eMlazi kuDumazile? Uma ngiya 
lapho, ngisemukelekile njena? Mh, mhlawumbe ngizofike 
ngihlangabezane nenkinga nje madoda? Kodwa wangitshela 
uDumazile ukuthi akasangifuni. Kusobala-ke ukuthi ukhona 


umuntu asethandana naye. Ukuya kwami lapho kungase 
kungidalele izinkinga. Kusho ukuthi kufanele ngivele ngiye e-
Adams kumkami uMaNzimande. Ehhene. Isithandwa sami sona 
asingalanga, kodwa yimina nje engadlala ubuhuzu. Ngiyazi 
ukuthi umntakwethu usangithanda futhi usangilindile. Mh, kepha 
uma sengifika ekhaya uMaNzimande esehlezi nelinye ihwanqa 
ngiyokwenzanjani madoda? Hhayi suka, ayikho leyo nto.” 

USithole wabe esegibela ithekisi elihambela khona e-Adams. 
Wathi efika kwakhe uSithole, kwabe kukhala ibhungane. 
UMaNzimande wayesemsebenzini emajalidini eManzimtoti. 
UMpisendlini wayesesikoleni. Wahlala phansi phezu kwetshe 
ngasekhishini. Omakhelwane bambona umnumzane 
wekhaya esehlezi njengesivakashi emzini wakhe. Abanye 
babefisa ukumsiza, kodwa babuye basabe uMaNzimande. 
Wayesenenhliziyo encane kabi muva nje. Bambuka-ke bandla 
umnumzane esedabukisa ebaleni. Walinda, walinda kwaze 
kwabuya umntwana wakhe esikoleni. 

Ngenkathi uMpisendlini eqhamuka ekhaya, wakhangwa 
yimpondlela yendoda ithe chwa phezu kwetshe ebaleni. Weza 
ngomude umzimba lo engazi ukuthi ngubani lo muntu. Kwathi 
uma esondela eduze, wabona ukuthi kanti nguyise. Washaya 
sengathi akaboni, waqonda endlini, wavula maqede wangena. 
USithole naye walandela. 

“Sawubona mfana wami! Usaphila kodwa?” USithole 
esinesineka. 

“Yebo!” 

“Uphi unyoko?” 

“Usemsebenzini.” Athi dlengelele uSithole ecabanga 
ukuthi ukuhamba kwakhe ekhaya kwadaleka isimo esaphoqa 
uMaNzimande ukuba aye kofuna umsebenzi. 

“Usebenza kuphi?” 


“Angazi.” Umfana lona wayengathandisisi kahle 
ukukhulumisana noyise ngenxa yezinkulumo ezase zigxishiwe 
emqondweni wakhe ngoyise. Imbewu yenzondo namagqubu 
yase itshalwe yamila kumntwana. Kwakuthi uma ebuka uyise, 
abone uhlobo oluthile nje lwesilwane esinonya. 

“Mfana wami, akukho kodwa okuya ngasethunjini? Ngafa 
yindlala!” UMpisendlini wasukuma, waphaka uphuthu, wenza 
umntanya maqede wanikeza uyise ukuba adle. Wakubuka lokhu 
kudla uSithole, wanikina ikhanda. Wazwakala ethi: 

“Yikhona kudla eninakho lokhu?” ebuza ngoba engazi ukuthi 
uphuthu olumhlophe wu lolu uzoluqala ngakuphi. 

“Yebo!” esho umfana eziphakela olwakhe uzolo. Wenza 
umbhubhudlo, wahlala phansi, wadla.USithole yena wakha kabili 
kathathu ophuthwini lwavele lwahlakazeka nomlomo wonke. 
Kwathi noma ethi uyanambinambitha, luvele luhlabe ezinsinini. 
Wagcina esephuza umntanya wodwa. Wabona ingcono 
kabi impilo yasejele kunalesi simo esimbingelelayo kwakhe. 
UMpisendlini yena washaya esentwala, waphuma eyodlala 
nezinye izingane phandle. 

Kwathi ilanga seliyozilahla kunina, yaqhamuka intokazi 
kaNzimande ilibeka lapho ilibeke khona. Kwakubonakala nje 
bo ukuthi ukhathele umuntu lona. Wayephethe inkowane 
ayeyiqhibule ngenkathi ephuma ejalidini eManzimtoti. 
Kwambona kuqala okungumfana wakhe, kweqa amagqanqu 
kujahe ukuyomphathisa. Kwathi kufika nje kwakudumela 
umthwalo, kwabe sekukhipha izindaba. 

“UBaba usefikile ekhaya.” 

“Uyihlo?” 

“Yebo mama!”Yagqunqa yaba mnyama ngesikhathi intokazi 
kaNzimande. Izindebe zomlomo zafuna ukukhuluma, kodwa 
kwangakhulumeka. Kwaphela ukukhathala, yakhabuzela 
isiphikelele khona kwayo. Yathi ingena nje emnyango imanzi 


kaSithole, yakhihla isililo owawungafunga ukuthi kushoniwe. 
Wathwala izandla ekhanda, waphumela phandle ehayiza. 
Wawungathi uphethwe wufufunyane. Omakhelwane bagcwala 
ngokushesha. 

“Yini makhelwane, kwenzenjani MaNzimande?” 
Babesazophendulwa ngubani phela ngoba uMaNzimande 
wayezibhonqa, ekhicileka ekhala. USithole yena 
wayesekhungathekile nje engazi noma mhlawumbe yitulo yini 
leli lokuba kuzovinjezelwa yena. Omakhelwane bagcina bebonile 
ukuthi ayingangabo le ndaba, kodwa ngeyomndeni. Babe 
sebemonyuka. 

Kwaya ngokuya lehla igwebu lemfezi kuMaNzimande. 
USithole wabona kufanele ukuba alisebenzise leli thuba. 

“MaNzimande, nami sengibuyile nkosikazi. Ngiyaxolisa 
kukho konke engikwenzile okuhlukumeze umphefumulo wakho. 
Ngiyazi ukuthi bekunzima kangakanani kuwena ukusala nomuzi. 
Ngiyakuthembisa ukuthi ngeke ngisakushiya wedwa nkosikazi.” 
UMaNzimande wayethule ethatha ebeka: 

“Kodwa uyaphi lo sathane onezimpondo? Kade yabhunguka 
le nto! Engani bekwaziwa ukuthi ngeke esabuyela emzini 
wakhe, usehambe unomphela uSithole! Bese ngihlezi kahle 
kabi engekho! Okwakobani-ke manje ukuzoshayelwa yile nto 
umthetho? Nx, hhayi suka! Mhlawumbe le nto ibuya negciwane 
lengculaza nje lapho ivela khona! Awu ngeke!”Wasukuma 
uMaNzimande wapheka inkowane. Kwathi ingavuthwa, waphaka 
uphuthu, inkowane wayithela ngaphezulu njengesishebo. 
Wanikeza umyeni wakhe ukudla. USithole wathi choko choko, 
engula yona inkowane, washiyela umfana wakhe. UMaNzimande 
naye waziphakela. Kwathi ukuba baqede ukudla, balungiselela 
ukuya kolala. 

UMaNzimande wayengaqoqile ekamelweni lakhe, kubufihlilili 
nje. Kwakukhona izinqamu zikagwayi nesimehlane sikagavini 


phezu kwetafula kanye nezimbadada ngaphansi kombhede. 
Wayibuka le nto uSithole, kodwa wafela phakathi okwebutho 
likaZulu. UMaNzimande naye wabona ukuthi uSithole uyabona, 
kodwa wangagqiza qakala nje. Wagaba ngokuthi uma eke 
wambuza nje, kuyobe uyinyathele emsileni. Bangena engutsheni. 
Bacisha, balala. 

Ngakusasa uSithole wavuka waqonda eSiphingo ukuyofuna 
umsebenzi. Wafuna wafuna kodwa do ukuwuthola. Wayebasathe 
uyafika ndawana thile bamlandulele. Kwezinye izindawo wayefica 
kubhalwe ngamagama amakhulu: AWUKHO UMSEBENZI. 
Kwakuvele kumqede amandla lokho. Kwaze kwathi ntambama, 
naye esethi uyalahlela nje, wadlula emahhovisi aphathelene 
nokuthuthwa kwenkunkuma elokishini eMlazi. Bambuza ukuthi 
unazo yini izincwadi ezinkulu zokushayela imoto. Kwabe basho 
entshweni, wabakhombisa khona manjalo. Bamtshela-ke ukuthi 
akofika ngakusasa azoqala umsebenzi. Wabonga, wavalelisa, 
wahamba eseyogibela. 

USithole wafika e-Adams esefikile uMaNzimande. 
Wayezenamele nje kade ethole umsebenzi. 

“Sewubuyile MaNzimande? Awu washesha namhlanjena!” 
UMaNzimande wanganaka nje, waziqhubekela nalokho 
ayekwenza. 

“Eyi nami ngiwutholile umsebenzi wokushayela.” Athi qwebu 
amehlo uMaNzimande, wafisa manje ukuzwisisa kahle. 

“Uzoshayela ntoni?” 

“Ngizoshayela amaloli athutha inkucunkucu elokishini.” Kuthi 
cosololo ukuzwa ukuthi uSithole akasezukuba ngumthwalo 
nezindleko kuyena. Wayeka yonke into ayeyenza, walungisa 
ukudla. Ngakusasa ekuseni uSithole wavukela khona emsebenzini. 
Wawuqala-ke umsebenzi wokuthutha inkucunkucu. Babezungeza 
yonke indawo elokishini laseMlazi. 

Ngelinye ilanga uSithole esenhlabakhefini, wathatha 


iloli waqonda ngqo emzini kaDumazile. Wafika wama 
emgwaqweni ngasenhla komuzi, washaya ihudi. Kwavela 
umsebenzi emnyango. USithole wakhiphela ingalo ngaphandle, 
wamqhweba. Weza esekhabuzela. Babingelelana, baphilelana. 

“Ngingamthola uDumazile?” 

“Yebo. Ngizothi ucelwa ngubani?” 

“Mtshele ukuthi ubizwa nguyise kaMtholephi.” Umsebenzi 

wabuyela endlini. Wamfica uDumazile eselungiselela ukuya 
emsebenzini. Wayesebenza ebusuku kulelo sonto. 

“Kunobaba othi angikubize sisi.” 

“Ubaba?” 

“Yebo Sisi! Uthe unguyise kaMtholephi.” 

“Kodwa uyaphi nje bakithi? Nx, hhayi suka!”Washo 
uDumazile kwabonakala ukuthi ucikekile. Waphuma endlini 
uDumazile waqonda elolini phandle. 

“Sawubona!” kubingelela uDumazile izinhlonze seziyimivingqi 
esiphongweni. 

“Yebo sawubona! Hawu waqhamuka wedwa, uphi umfana?” 

“Uyadlala ngalena kwendlu.” 

“Nami bengithi angizonilunguza nje ninomfana. Manje 
ngangayibona iveni yami ebaleni, ikuphi?” 

“Umkhwenyana wami wathumela kwabasezikilebheni ukuba 
bazoyidonsa.”Wathi dlengelele uSithole ukuzwa uDumazile 
ekhuluma kanje. 

“Kanti wawuqinisile ngempela ukuthi sewunendoda?”

 UDumazile aqale angaphenduli. Acikeke uSithole. 

“Kodwa yayimxake ngani nje imoto yami izimele ebaleni?” 

“Wathi ibanga udoti ebaleni.” Kwathi xhifi futhi kuSithole. 


“Kanti ngokabani lo muzi? Niyazi ukuthi mina ngingavele 
ngiwudayise niphakathi?” 

“Cha phela yise kaMtholephi ngeke kwenzeke lokho. Umuzi 
lona ungowami. Akuyona neze into esingayibanga leyo.” 

“Owakho wawuthathaphi?” 

“Ngawuthengelwa nguwena.” 

“Sengathi ngenza iphutha. Ngifuna ubuyele kimina umuzi 
wami lo. Ehhe ngiyawufuna bo! Okwesibili ngifuna utshele le 
ndoda yakho ukuthi ngiyayifuna imali yemoto yami enayidonsela 
esikilebhuyadi. Ngiyazi ukuthi yakhokhelwa imoto yami lapho. 
Okwesithathu ngifuna ingane yami ibuyele kimina ngizondlele 
yona.”Wathi engakaligwinyi nje, thushu i-ambulense. UDumazile 
waswela umgodi wokucasha. Watatazela ngendlela yokuthi 
wagcina engasazi okufanele akwenze. Kwake kwathi akayovulela 
umyeni wakhe isango, kodwa enye inhliziyo yabona ngenye 
indlela. UMtalaselwa wazivulela isango, wangenisa i-ambulense 
ngaphakathi. Kwathi angangena uMtalaselwa, wacela ukuba 
enzelwe itiye. Nempela umsebenzi wabeka amanzi ngeketelo. 

“Ngubani lona okhuluma nomkami phandle?” 

“Uthe unguyise kaMtholephi.” 

Kwathi xhifi kuMtalaselwa, wayesethi: 

“Hamb’umbize!” Umsebenzi wathi ethi uyombiza, 
wahlangana naye uDumazile evele esebuya. Bangena endlini 
sebelandelana nomsebenzi. UMtalaselwa wahluleka ukulinda aze 
ahlale phansi uDumazile. 

“Ngubani le ndoda obumi nayo?” Aqale athule uDumazile 
engazi ukuthi uzoyibeka kanjani inkulumo. Kwathi ekugcineni 
wabona ungekho umasiza. 

“Nguyise kaMtholephi.”Wagqunqa waba mnyama ngesikhathi 
uMtalaselwa. 


“Nisathandana naye?” esho emjamele ngezimbokodwe 
zamehlo. 

“Cha ube…” Izinyembezi zivele zigcwale amehlo, abibitheke, 
akhicileke. 

“Nx, demede!Uhamba ukwenza kukulungela!”Wathi lacu, 
wamuthi wu wu ngempama; wayesemuthi xhafa ngenqindi, 
wathi khilikithi phansi! Wathatha ukhiye wemoto, waphuma. 
Kwasuka amaphepha engasaliphuzanga itiye uMtalaselwa. 
UDumazile wasala ezithulisa. Wavuka phansi maqede 
wazithuntutha, waqonda ekamelweni ukuyozibuka esibukweni. 

“Hawu! Le ndoda ingilimaze kanjena? Awubheke manje ihlo 
liyavuvukala! Angikwazi ukuya emsebenzini nginjena! Awuthi 
ngishayele umphathi ucingo.” Nebala wabika amanangananga 
nje. UDumazile wahlala ekhaya kwaze kwabuya umyeni wakhe 
ntambama. 

Yatheleka-ke insizwa kaMsholozi ingasadle nkobe zamuntu. 
Yayingathukuthele yayibila. Yangena endlini maqede yadlula 
yayoqhinqa ekamelweni. UDumazile wazibonela ukuthi 
kufanele ehlele ngezansi. Wacabanga kaningi ukuba amlandele 
umyeni wakhe. Enye inhliziyo kodwa yayibona ngenye indlela. 
Ekugcineni wazithola ephoqekile ukuba amlandele umyeni 
wakhe. Wadudula isicabha, wangena engasangqongqozanga. 
Wahlala eqhulwini lombhede. 

“Manje uhambe emini ngisathi ngiyakuchazela ukuthi uyise 
kaMtholephi ubeyaphi.” Njengoba uMtalaselwa wayebheke 
phansi nje, wamuthi klulu ngeso lengulube umkakhe, wabuye 
wabheka phansi futhi. UDumazile wathi: 

“Ubethi uzodonsa iveni lakhe ngeloli. Manje ngenkathi ufika 
wena, mina bengisathi ngiyamchazela indawo lapho iveni lakhe 
lahudulelwa khona.” 

“Yilokho nje kuphela?” 


“Okunye-ke ubethi ufuna ukubona ingane, kodwa mina 
nginqabile.” 

Anikine ikhanda uMtalaselwa. Intukuthelo iye ngokuya 
ivubeleka ngaphakathi. Aqale ukukhumbula amazwi kanina 
mzukwane eyobika ukuthi usefuna ukuthatha. Wabe esethatha 
ethi: 

“Le ngane kufanele ihambe iyohlala nogogo wayo 
eMzimkhulu ukuze uSithole lowo akwazi ukuyoyibonela khona. 
Mina anginaye umfazi ozolokhu eqhabisana nabashayeli bamaloli 
kadoti emzini wami.” UDumazile akabange esayithi vu indaba 
yendlu. Wayebona ukuthi izosusa omunye umsindo futhi. 

UDumazile wakhombisa ukuzehlisa kumyeni wakhe. 
Ukuthukuthela kuMtalaselwa kwaya ngokuya kudamba. 
Ekugcineni wakwazi ukuxoxela umkakhe ukuthi kwakukade 
kukhona umuntu owayeshaye ucingo ebiza i-ambulense ukuba 
izothatha umuntu ogulayo kwesinye sezigceme elokishini. 
Isibhedlela sathumela yena-ke ukuba ayolanda leso siguli. 
Ngeshwa elikhulu wasifica leso siguli sesiphangalele. Akabangeke 
esasithatha. Ngenxa yokuthi kwakungasekude nakwakhe 
lapho, wathi akadlule ekhaya athole inkomishana yetiye. Nakhuke 
esezithela phezu komhuqa weloli likadoti. 

Kwedlula izinyangana isimo sezinto saguquka enhlalweni 
kaMtalaselwa. Waphoqeka ukuba athuthe eThekwini ayohlala 
eMgungundlovu lapho ayesesebenza khona. Wayesekhushulelwe 
esikhundleni sokuphatha ophikweni lwezokuthuthwa kweziguli 
ngama-ambulense KwaZulu Natali emaphakathi. Lolu guquko 
lwenzeka nje umkakhe usezithwele. 

Kuyibangana khona ukusuka eThekwini kuya eMgungundlovu. 
Akuyona nje into elula ukusebenza khona ube uhlala eThekwini. 
Yingakho-ke nje uMtalaselwa azithola ephoqekile ukuba ahlale 
ngakhona emsebenzini. Wathatha indlu elokishini laseMbali. 
Umndeni wakhe wayesewuvakashela kanye ngesonto. Wayevama 


ukufika ngezimpelasonto. Nakho lokho kubuya kwakuthanda 
ukumgqilaza kakhulu. Yayinkulu kabi imali ayeyikhokha yokugibela 
amathekisi ukuya nokubuya. Wayethi uma eyibala leyo mali 
ekupheleni kwenyanga, athole ukuthi uyalahlekelwa impela. 
Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi wazithola ephoqekile ukuba avakashe 
kanye ngemuva kwamasonto amabili. Kwakuthi ekupheleni 
kwenyanga bavakashele abazali bakhe ekhaya kwaJilafohlo. 
Kwesinye isikhathi uMtalaselwa wayesukela ngakhona 
eMgungundlovu baficane naye umkakhe ekhaya. 

Akuphelanga sikhathi eside wakhululeka uDumazile. Wathola 
isigemfunga sensizwa. Wasiqamba igama wathi nguSanele. 
Kwakuvele kuyinhloso yakhe leyo yokuthi amasu amathathu 
anele kuyena. Wayekholelwa kakhulu wukuthi umuntu 
wesifazane ohululayo nje ugcina esephethwe ngumdlavuza 
wesibeletho. Wabona kubalulekile-ke ukuba ahlele umndeni. 
Baxoxisana nodokotela, bakumisa ukuthola kwakhe abantwana. 

Abafowabo bakaMtalaselwa base bephume eyabo imizi. 
Abazali bakhe bona babehlala namadodakazi abo ayengakendi. 
UMtalaselwa wayefikela kwabo uma evakashile. Wasibuka 
lesi simo senhlalo, naye wafisa ukuphuma owakhe umuzi. 
Wayesevama ukuhlangabezana nezinkinga zokuqula amacala 
phakathi kodadewabo kanye nomkakhe. Kwakuye kuthi 
uma unina ethi uyalamula, kuthiwe uyenzelela. Naye unina 
wayesekhathele wukuqophisana ngamazwi nomalokazana 
wakwakhe. Wayesefisa kabi impela ukuba uMaKheswa 
aphume owakhe umuzi. UMtalaselwa walubeka udaba kuyise, 
babonisana. Bagcina bevumelene ngendawo lapho indlu 
izomiswa khona. UMtalaselwa wabe eseqonda kumkakhe 
eyomazisa ngokumiswa kwendlu. Wayezimisele ukwakha indlu 
yesakhiwo. UDumazile akathandanga ukuphawula ngoba ebona 
ukuthi isikhathi asikakamvumeli. Umyeni wakhe wamshiya 
yedwa endlini esaya kozixoxela nabazali bakhe ekhishini. 

Kwathi ebusuku besendlini yabo yokulala, kodwa 


bengakazumeki, wayiqala-ke indaba uDumazile. 
“Yise kaSanele, mina angiboni ukuthi kuzongilungela ukwakha 

umuzi wami kini.” Athi dlengelele uMtalaselwa. 

“Ngilalele,” sekusho umyeni wakhe exakekile nje. 

“Selokhu ngashada kulo muzi ngiyabona nje ukuthi 
angithandwa muntu. Ngisho noyedwa qhwaba! Yonke into 
engiyenzayo iyafenyiswa nje. Kodwa uma kwenzekile kwaba 
khona okuhlana okwenziwe yilezi zinkonsolo zakwenu, kuduma 
izwe lonke. Okwami okuhle engikwenzile akunakwa nakunakwa. 
Kunyathelwa ngezinyawo kuthulwe du.” Anikine ikhanda 
uMtalaselwa ekhombisa ukuthi akahambisani nenkulumo 
yomkakhe. Wathatha wathi: 

“Awuzokwakha umuzi wakho kithi, kodwa uzokwakha 
umuzi wakho kwakho. Ubaba usenginikeze yona yonke le 
ndawo engezansi komuzi womfowethu. Akekho umuntu ozobe 
ekushayela umthetho kwakho.” 

“Ehhene kufanele phela unikine ikhanda uphikisane nami 
engashada nawe. Angithi oshomu bakho labo?” 

“Obani bona labo?” 

“Ubuza ngoba ungazi yise kaSanele? Musa ukungenza isilima 
mina, musa nje. Kusho ukuthi awunandaba nami, ehhene kusho 
lokho phela. Ukhona umuntu ongayiboni into esobala kanjena? 
Kodwa bonke abantu bayasho. Inkosi, basho into efanayo.” 

“Bathini abantu?” 

“Bathi abantu kuyobe ngiyakwazi ukuchatha ukhuphe uma 
nje ngike ngakwazi ukuhlala nomama wakho. Bathi ngisho 
ozakwethu laba baze baphuma eyabo imizi nje kwakuyingenxa 
yakhe lo mama wakho behlangene nale mijendevu yakini. Futhi 
sekuyafakazeleka lokho.” 

Athi ukuthula kancane esagwinya amathe. Wabe esethatha 
ethi: 


“Uyakhumbula ukuthi ngenkathi sishada umama wakho 
akakikizanga yena? OMaNgedlane benoMaNdleleni bona 
babekikiza, besuluza baze babhedle benziwa yinjabulo. UMama 
wakho yena wawungathi ubona imoto ethwele isidumbu. 
Ucabanga ukuthi kwakudalwa yini konke lokho? Odadewenu 
kuthiwa babepikla bethi ngeke ngiwakhe lo muzi. Umesisi Vilakazi 
uthi izinkulumo ezazikhulunywa ngami ngalelo langa zazisabisa! 
Uthi kwasuka elikhulu igidigidi leli ngenkathi udadewenu ethi 
wena ushade neqhashamlenze, umsalazabiwa uqobo lwawo.” 

“Yibaphi labo dadewethu ababesho lokho?” 

“Kanti bangaki? Awusabazi manjena? NguBavelile-ke owasho 
lokho. Bathi uBadingile yena wayengibiza ngembexembexe 
yedisholo ledikazi. Umama wakho wayehleka, kunguKhisimuzi 
nje kuyena. Angiyiboni-ke inhlalo enhle engingaba nayo kule 
ndawo yakini. Akukho neze ukuthula lapha. Abantu bakule ndawo 
banesipepe kakhulu.” 

“Seningamathe nolimi nabantu bakwaVilakazi? Ngiyabuza, 
hhe?” 

“Ukube angizange ngizihlanganise futhi ngixoxisane noMesisi 
Vilakazi, ngabe sengadla ushevu lapha kini. Angifunwa muntu 
mina lapha, nawe uyakwazi lokho, ungufakazi. Nakuba ngisaphila 
ngiphilela yena uMesisi Vilakazi. Nami angisakudli nje ukudla 
engingakwazi ukuthi kuphekeke kanjani. Hha mame!” Asho aze 
aklolode. 

“Laba bantu bakwaVilakazi osubadonse bangena bagamanxa 
phakathi komuzi kababa, uyobakhipha kanjani?” 

“Aningenelani nje nabangani nabantu bakwaVilakazi belunge 
kangaka? Kusho khona impela ukuthi nibanga yona le ngqondo 
ebolile yakini. Balunge kabi abantu bakwaVilakazi!” 

“Abantu bakwaVilakazi badla umngcele wensimu yakithi. Sathi 
uma sithi siyakhuluma nabo, bahamba kuqala ukuyosimangalela 
enkosini. Ngenxa yokuthi bahlobene nayo, labe selisilahla icala. 


Icala lathethwa ngobuhlobo. Ngikhuluma nje umndeni wonke 
wakithi awuhambelani nabo, kodwa wena ulala khona, uvuke 
khona.” 

“Mina angiboni nje kungumqondo ophusile ukuba abantu 
bethi bakhelene kangaka kodwa bangangenelani. Mina 
ngizozingenela nje kwaVilakazi.” 

Yasho imanzi yakhe kwabonakala nje ukuthi izongena ngodli 
dlakalasi kwaVilakazi. UMtalaselwa wagcina ebonile ukuthi 
uDumazile akadlali ngempela uma ethi akafuni ukwakha umuzi 
wabo kwaJilafohlo. Wabe esezitshela ukuthi yena uzokwehlela 
ngezansi ukuze kube khona ukuthula phakathi komuzi. 

“Manje bewucabanga ukuba senzenjani?” UMtalaselwa esho 
ngokuthamba. 

“Mina bengithi akufanele sijahe umdaka linganile. Sinawo 
umuzi wethu elokishini. Pho sijaheni ngokwakha? Uma sifuna 
ukwakha indlu yethu ekhaya, kufanele siqongelele kahle imali. 
Kuyothi uma seyanele, bese mina ngigoduka ngiyokhuluma 
nobaba ukuba asinikeze indawo yokwakha. Mkhulu kabi 
umhlaba kababa eMzimkhulu.” 

“Mina ngakhe ngakini? Ngibe wusibali-makoti?” 

“Kungcono kabi ngakithi. Abantu bangakithi baphucuzekile, 
abafani neze nalaba bangakini.” Kumkhonondise lokho 
uMtalaselwa. 

“Okunye-ke ebengingathandi ukukutshela khona sengizosale 
sengikutshela nje.”

 Athi ukuthula kancane ecabanga ukuthi uzoyisho kanjani le 
nto. Bese ethi: 

“Ngesonto eledlule ngahamba ngaya kumuntu obonayo. 
Ngangifuna ake angihlolele nje ukuthi umshado wethu umi 
kanjani. Hhayi wabhula waqeqebula, washiya angalaziyo. 
Wabona ngisho nezinto ebengingazinakile.” Athi ukuthula 


kancane ngoba umyeni wakhe wayekhombisa ukungakuthakaseli 
lokhu kuya kobhula komkakhe. 

“Wawuhamba nobani ukuya lapho?” 

“Ngangihamba nobani? Ngangizohamba nobani ngokwakho? 
Ngangihamba ngedwa!” esho kubonakala nje ukuthi igazi 
seliyafudumala. 

“Babona ntoni-ke omangothobana?” 

“Angithi uke ubone ukuthi ingane ikhala uqanduqandu 

ebusuku?” 

“E!” 

“Bathi kunezilwane eziyengamayo ingane yami. Ngithe uma 

ngibuza ukuthi zivela kuphi, hhayi angithandi ukusho.”

 Athi ukuthula kancane sengathi akathandi ngempela. 

“Bathi zivela kuphi?” esho ngokungancengi. 

“Ungeke ukholwe. Bathi zivela kumuntu osondelene kabi 

nawe. Mina kodwa ngivele ngabona ukuthi kunjengoba kushiwo. 
Wumayihlonze phela lowo.” 

“Ake ukhulume into ecacile. Bathi ngubani umuntu othumela 
imikhovu enganeni?” 

“Bathi… eyi…!” Athi ukuthula kancane. UMtalaselwa 
amjamele ngezimbokodwe zamehlo. UDumazile aqhube athi: 

“Bathi umama wakho. Bathi wayefunga egomela 
ngisakhulelwe ethi ngeke ngiyigone. Ngenxa yokuthi wahluleka 
ukuyibulala isengumbungu, usefuna ukuyiphoqoza ngezilwane 
zakhe manje.” 

“Umama usenezilwane muva nje?” 

“Ehhene! Uyamphikela yini?” 

“Cha angisho ukuthi ngiyamphikela, kodwa wukuthi 

ngiyamangala.” 


“Umangaliswa yini?” 

“Ngimangaliswa yikho nje ukuzwa ukuthi umama 
useyathakatha. Kusukela ngisewusana umama wayewa evuka, 

ekhombisa uthando olumangalisayo kimina. Wangikhulisa ngaze 
ngaba yindoda. Angiboni-ke ukuthi angangibulala kanjani manje.” 
“Akabulali wena phela, ubulala mina nengane yami. Futhi 

ngeke wena akubulale njengoba usho nawe ukuthi wakukhulisa.” 

“Ngakube uyaqinisa ngempela ukuthi umama uyathakatha?” 

“Ngamanye amazwi wena awukholwa? Usho ukuthi abantu 

ababonayo ababoni, bayabheda nje?” 
“Angisho ukuthi ababoni, kodwa ngikholelwa wukuthi babona 

lokhu abangakuboni.” 

“Angisezwa-ke manje ukuthi uthini.” 

“Ngithi umuntu okuthiwa uyabona usuke ekhuluma into 
acabanga ukuthi uyayibona. Okuyikhona akubonayo ngempela 
akukhona lokho akushoyo.” 

“Kodwa lona engangiye kuyena usebenzisa abalozi. Bonke 
abantu bayasho ukuthi abalozi abashayi phansi. Ungidonse 
ngendlebe-ke wathi uma ngisayithanda le ngane yami, kufanele 
ngishaye isixaxa kule ndawo. Ngisayithanda-ke bandla le ngane 
yami. Kufanele ngishaye isixaxa ngempela kule ndawo. Kuhle 
ngiyishiye nabanikazi bayo; ngiyishiye kusekuhle nje. Wena uma 
ufuna ukusala, angikwenqabeli uzosala. Kodwa mina nengane 
yami, cha bandla siyahamba.” UMtalaselwa wabona ukuthi kubi, 
imanzi yakhe ifuna ukuhamba ngempela manje. Wehlisa umoya, 
wavuma engavumi. Baze balala phakathi kobusuku.

 UMtalaselwa wavuka ekuseni waya endlini enkulu 
yakwabo. Wabafica abazali bakhe sebevukile nabo, sebezihlalele 
nje. Wabe eseyilanda-ke indaba: 

“Njengoba baba bewunginike yonke leya ndawo ukuba 
ngakhe kuyona, sengathi akusezokuba njalo. UMaKheswa ubona 


ngenye indlela.” 
“Ngamanye amagama ndodana usho ukuthi awusezukwakha 

kule ndawo engikunikeze yona?” 

“Yebo baba!” 

“Ewu, asazi-ke ndodana ngoba nonyoko ubekhala ngokuthi 

usekhathele wukujonqwa ngumkakho sengathi babanga indoda. 
Manje niyokwenzenjani uma nifika lapha?” 

“Usho ukwenza njani okunjani baba?” 

“Ngisho ndodana ukuthi niyoquba kuphi uma nivakashile 
ninomakoti njengoba izindlu zonke kungezami nonyoko nje?” 

“Sengathi baba ngeke kusaba khona ukuvakasha.” Kubethuse 
lokho. 

“Hamba juba bayokuqhutha phambili! Ngithi hamba juba!” 
kusho unina ngomoya obuhlungu. 

“E, ndodana nguye umakoti obona kanjalo?” 

“Wukuthi baba ngiyabona khona ukuthi uMaKheswa ngeke 
ahlale lapha. Yingakho nje ngibona kungcono sakhe buqamama.” 

“Kuyezwakala khona ndodana. Ngeke ngisakushayela 
umthetho, sewuyindoda manje. Uzobona-ke nawe njengendoda.” 

“Awu mntanami, sewuyahamba? Usuhamba unomphela 
lapha ekhaya?” kusho unina ehlengezela izinyembezi. Nokho 
uMtalaselwa wazama ukumduduza unina. Wasukuma, 
wavalelisa, waphuma endlini enkulu, waphindela endlini lapho 
kuhlezi khona umkakhe. Baqoqa-ke izimpahla zabo. UDumazile 
wajabula kabi ukubona ukuthi intando yakhe seyiyenzeka. 
Kwathi bangaqeda, bagibela sebephikelele eMlazi. 


ISAHLUKO SESISHIYAGALOLUNYE 

Ngelinye ilanga kwakunengqungquthela kakhukhulelangoqo 
womhlangano wabahlengikazi eCity Hall eThekwini. Lo 
mhlangano wawukade ugqugquzelwe ngungqongqoshe wezempilo 
kwaZulu-Natal. Inhloso yomhlangano kwakuwukuzocobelelana 
futhi kuxwayiswane ngegciwane lesandulela ngculaza. 

Umhlangano waqala ngehora leshumi ekuseni. Wavulwa 
ngumfundisi ngomthandazo onzulu. Wanxusa uMdali ukuba 
abe nobubele kithina ngoba sonke sonile phambi kobuso bakhe. 
Wacela ukuba kutholakale imishanguzo ezoshanguza lolu 
bhubhane oluqotha imbokodo nesisekelo. Kwathi angaqeda 
umuntu weNkosi, kwangenwa odabeni losuku. Ekupheleni 
komhlangano, kwanikezwa umuntu womshuwalense ithuba 
lokuba achazele abahlengikazi ngosizo inkampani yabo elunikeza 
abantu asebehaqwe yileli gciwane. 

“Mphathi wohlelo, bafowethu kanye nani bodadewethu 
ngiyanibingelela. Mina nginguZitike Jeffrey Moloi . Ngiqhamuka 
eGauteng eSoweto. Ngenxa yomsebenzi engiwenzayo, sengihlala 
lapha eThekwini eDurban North. Lapha ngimele inkampani 
yakwa-New Life. Le nkampani seyinesikhathi eside yasungulwa. 
Ihhovisi lethu elikhulu liseKapa. Sinawo futhi amanye amahhovisi 
eGoli, Bloemfontein kanye nazo zonke nje izindawo. Ihhovisi 
lethu lapha eThekwini litholakala ekhoneni likaSmith Street kanye 
noField Street.”Wabe esechaza injongo kanye nosizo lwabo 


kubantu asebehlaselwe yileli gciwane emphakathini. Kwathi 
angaqeda, kwabuzwa imibuzo. Wayiphendula. 

Kwenzeka konke lokhu nje uDumazile akekho lapho, kodwa 
usesemajukujukwini emicabango: 

“Mh, kanti kuyiqiniso ngempela ukuthi yizintaba kuphela 
ezingahlangani? Ngizokumbizela amaphoyisa ngempela phela 
mina. INkosi, ngizombopha ngempela! Anginakudlala yena, 
ungathi angenza nje!” Kwathi ukuba uphele umhlangano, 
kwahlakazekwa. 

UDumazile waqonda ngqo kulo mfokazi owayehlezi nomunye 
umhlengikazi emotweni yakhe kanokusho. Umhlengikazi 
wayethathekile yincazelo, esezofuna usizo lokuxhaswa. 

“Sawubona!” kubingelela uDumazile izinhlonze seziyimivingqi 
esiphongweni. 

“Yebo sawubona!” Sekuvuma le nsizwa ngokusola okuthile. 

“Angazi noma usangibona yini?” Iqale ithule le nsizwa 
isambukisisa, ikhumule izibuko emehlweni, bese ithi: 

“Konje ngizothi ngangikubona kuphi?” Avele acikeke 
uDumazile. Wacabanga ukuthi insizwa lena imenza 
isiphukuphuku. 

“Wawungibona eZenzele High School eMbumbulu ngenkathi 
wena usafundisa khona. Awusamkhumbuli uDumazile Kheswa?” 
UDumazile uchaza nje, uMoloi kudala ekhumbulile. Waswela 
umgodi wokucasha. UMoloi, ngokubona ukuthi uzohlazeka kulo 
mhlengikazi ozocela ukusizwa, wabe esemcela ukuba babuye 
babonane naye ngesinye isikhathi, waphuma emotweni. Kwabe 
sekungena uDumazile. 

“Kodwa thisha, nguwena ngempela lona?” 

“Yimina Dumazile. Ngiyalazi icala lami. Ngiyisiboshwa 
ngizihambela nje. Ngicabanga ukuthi sizodinga isikhathi esanele 
ukuba sixoxe ngakho konke okwenzeka, bese sibona-ke ukuthi 


singawalungisa kanjani lawo maphutha adalekayo. Njengamanje 
ngisaphuthuma komunye umhlangano engiwuhlele nabahlengikazi 
basekuHlengeni. Kunganjani ukuba unginikeze inombolo yakho 
yocingo ukuze ngikuthinte ngemfonomfono?” 

“Anginikani inamba yocingo lwakwami. Ngikhuluma nje 
ayibhaliwe emabhukwini ngoba ngingafuni ukushayelwa yinoma 
ngubani nje!” 

“Nami angiqondile ukuthi ngizokushayela noma yikanjani nje. 
Ngenzela ukuba ngikwazi ukulungisa amademesha adalekayo.” 

Aqale athule uDumazile esacabanga ukuthi kufanele 
yini ukuba amnikeze inombolo yocingo lwakwakhe. Hhayi, 
akamnike. UMoloi wakhipha ipeni lakhe lohlobo oluphambili 
kanye nedayari, wabe esethi: 

“Awungiphindele inamba.” Ayiphinde futhi uDumazile. 
Abhale. Bavalelisane, bahlukane.

 Kwathi ebusuku eselele uDumazile, kwangena ucingo. 
Wagxuma izithonto uLerato, walugxavula. 

“Hello! KukwaZuma lapha ekhaya, singakusiza?” 

“Hallo! Angazi noma ngingamthola yini uSista Zuma?” 

“Yebo ungamthola! Bamba-ke ngisayomvusa.” Asho elubeka 
eceleni. 

“Mama, olwakho!” esho ememeza. 

Wathi gubhu uDumazile. Washwayizela ebhushuzela 
waqonda kulona ucingo maqede walucaphuna. 

“Hello! NguMesisi Zuma lona okhulumayo.” 

“Hallo! Angazi noma nguDumazile yini lowo?” 

“Yebo nguyena!” 

“NguMoloi okhulumayo lapha eDurban North. Ninjani 
ngalapho nina?” 


“Siyaphila.” Athule. Kuqhubeke yena-ke uMoloi. 

“Ngamafuphi nje ngicela sizinqume amakhanda sizishiye 
ngoba ngeke sikwazi ukuziqeda zonke lapha ocingweni. Ushayisa 

ngasikhathi sini kusasa?” 

“Ngi-off-duty kusasa. Kwenzenjani?” 

“Bengithi ngizokuhlangabeza ntambama uma sewushayisile 

emsebenzini. Kusho ukuthi ngingakubona nini, kanjani?” 

“Eyi, angazi.” Athi ukuthula uDumazile esacabanga: 

“Uma ngiletha lo muntu lapha, uzongidalela amazinyo 
abushelelezi emndenini wami. Mh, kepha uma ngingambambeli 
eduze, ngiyophinde ngimthole kuphi ukuze ngimchuthe? 
Yihhinikazi phela leli, lidinga ukugqonjwa lize libe yisigqala.” 
Wabe esethatha ethi: 

“Mangithi nje kukuwena. Mina ngikhululekile ngalapha.” 

“Ngizozama ukufika ngehora lesishiyagalolunye ekuseni. Konje 

inamba yendlu ithini?” 

Amtshele. 

“Ngiyabonga. Sesiyobonana kusasa ekuseni. Ulale kahle.” 
Balubeke phansi bobabili ucingo. UDumazile waphindela 
embhedeni, walala. 

Lathi ligamanxa ihora lesishiyagalombili ekuseni, uhuntshu 
lwemoto lwabe selumile esangweni. UDumazile akangabazanga 
ngenkathi ezwa imoto ima phandle ukuthi sekunguyena uyise 
womntwana wakhe. Walunguza ngewindi, wathola ukuthi 
nguyena ngempela uMoloi. Waphuma maqede wavula isango, 
yangena imoto. Kwathi ingaqeda ukuma ebaleni, uMoloi 
waphuma phakathi, bangena endlini sebelandelana noDumazile. 
ULerato benoMtholephi base behambile ukuya esikoleni. 
Umsebenzi wasekhishini wayehlanza izitsha. USanele yena 
wayesalele. Wayengakakhuli ngaleyo ndlela yokuba wayesengaya 
esikoleni. 


“Uyazi, ngizwa ngifikelwa yizinyembezi. Inhliziyo yami iconsa 
igazi.” 
“Yini sekwenzenjani manje?” 
“Uma ngikubona, umqondo wami uvele ubuyise yonke le nto 
owayenza kimina.” 
“Kahle ngamatshe phela, ngingezansi.” 

“Uyazi qiniso, kuthi angivele ngikubizele amaphoyisa 
azokuthatha khona manjena nje. Into owangenza yona! 
Wangihlekisa nezwe muntu wabantu!” 

“Empeleni kuhle ngikhulume iqiniso njengomuntu ofayo. 
Ngaphathwa ngamahloni ngenkathi ungibikela ukuthi 
sewukhulelwe. Ngabe sengiya esihlotsheni sami eNtuzuma. 
Ngahlala lapho izinyanga ezimbili. Ngathi ngithi ngiyabuyela 
esikoleni, ngathola ukuthi kanti ibhantshi seligcwele umoya. 
Uthishomkhulu wayeseluthathe udaba walubikela izikhulu 
zoMnyango wemfundo. Ngaleyo ndlela-ke kwaba wukumiswa 
kwami emsebenzini. Kwathiwa ngeke ngiqashwe ndawo 
emsebenzini kahulumeni kuze kuphele iminyaka emihlanu. 
Ngabe sengibona ukuthi akekho umasiza, ngakhuphuka ngaya 
ekhaya eGoli. Ngathi ngiyazama okungamatohwana, kwavele 
kwanhlanga zimuka nomoya. Ngahlala unyaka golokoqo 
ngingasebenzi. Kwaze kwathi phakathi nonyaka wesibili, kwaba 
yima ngithola umsebenzi kule nkampani engiyisebenzelayo 
njengamanje.” 

“Kodwa uthi wawuke ucabange ngomthwalo owangithwesa 
wona?” 
“Ja ngangicabanga khona maar I could not make ends meet 
toe. Eintlik I was really desperate.” 
“Ubunzima owangishiya nabo ngiyabesaba muntu wabantu!” 

“Kahle phela, kuyazwela nakumina manje. Ngiyazi khona 
ukuthi ngenza iphutha impela. Ngizimisele ukulungisa konke 
okonakalayo.” 


Kuthi cosololo kuDumazile ukuzwa lawo mazwi. 

“Nendodakazi yakho sekuyigqumgedlela lentombi. Awu, 
umntanami akalwazi uthando lukayise. Uyise wambalekela 
engakafiki kulo mhlaba.” 

“Kodwa bewuye uphendule uthini nje uma umntwana 
ekubuza ukuthi mina ngikuphi?” 

“Eyi, ububa nzima lowo mbuzo. Amanga engangiwaqamba 
aguquka akha inzondo nesithombe esibi enganeni. Umntwana 
wayesekuthatha njengesigebengu somuntu esingafuni ukondla.” 

“Ngizozama ukuwuguqula lowo mqondo nomfanekiso 
umntwana anawo ngami.” 

“Nomama usayilindile inkomo leyo. Ubehleze ebalisa kabi 
ngayo, ethi usengaze afe impela engayitholanga. Ubaba naye 
uyasifuna isephulo.” 

“Ngizokulungisa konke lokho. Ngingathokoza ukuba ngiqale 
ngithengele indodakazi yami izimpahla zokwembatha, bese 
ngiyifakela nemfalakahlana ebhange. Ngemuva kwalokho 
sesingahlela ukuba ngiyokhokhela abazali bakho.”Wajabula 
uDumazile ukuzwa lawo mazwi. Wabona kufanele ukuba 
ambambele eduze uMoloi. Babe sebakha olunye usuku 
abayohlangana ngalo sekukhona nendodakazi yabo. 
Babezohlanganela esitolo simbe sezingubo eThekwini. 
Bavalelisana-ke, uMoloi waphuma eseya kongena emotweni 
yakhe phandle. Wayidumisa, yasuka. 

Lwafika-ke usuku olungaliyo. UDumazile wayeziphihle zonke. 
ULerato yena wawungathi yisihlahla sikaKhisimuzi, engasagqokile 
eseconsa! Kwakungasentombi kwakuwusukasambe woqobo. 
Bathi befika esitolo sezingubo, uMoloi wayesefikile elindele 

bona. Babingelelana, baphilelana. 

“Nihambe kanjani kodwa ngala matekisi andizayo?” 

“Sihambe kahle. Sesawajwayela nalezi zigubhu zawo eziduma 


kuvaleke izindlebe.” Athi ukuthula kancane, bese ethatha ethi: 

“Iyona-ke indodakazi yakho lena,” esho ekhomba uLerato 
owayemoyizela kancane. 

“Awu sawubona-ke ndodakazi!” esho uMoloi elula 
isandla exhawula. Avume uLerato. UDumazile wabheka 

ngasendodakazini yakhe, wathi: 

“Nguyena-ke ubaba wakho lona.” 

Wahlengezela izinyembezi uLerato. Wayengazi ukuthi 
kufanele akhale noma ajabule yini ukubona uyise. Wayesehlanze 
ngedela ukuthi yena wayeyoke abonane noyise omzalayo. 

“Ngiyathokoza nami ukukwazi baba.” Bajabulelana kwaba 
kuhle kwaba njeyayana. Babe sebengena ngaphakathi esitolo. 
Wabathengela-ke izingubo uMoloi. Nakuba kwakuqondwe 
ukuba kuthengelwe uLerato, kodwa noDumazile wahlomula. 
Kwathi bangaqeda ukuthenga, baya lapho kudliwa khona. Badla 
bashaya esentwala. UMoloi wagqabula isheke, wakhokha. 
Baphuma, bangena emotweni phandle. Yaduma, yasuka 
seyiphikelele khona eMafezini eMlazi. 

Ngenkathi befika eMlazi, uMoloi wayethi uzobathi qithi 
bese ephindela emuva. Kwakungekho emqondweni wakhe 
ukuba avuse izindaba ezindala zokuthandana kwabo. Ukushona 
komkakhe okwakusanda kwenzeka kwamfundisa ukuba athathe 
isinqumo sokuba aphile impilo entsha; impilo yokuzithiba 
nokuzinqabela ezintweni. Ngokucelwa-ke wuDumazile ukuba 
bangene endlini, wahlonipha wangena. Baxoxa-ke isikhathi eside 
waze wahlwelwa. 

Izindaba kazilali endleleni ngoba zesaba amazolo. 
Akuthathanga sikhathi eside zafika izindaba kuMtalaselwa 
eMgungundlovu. Izingcingo zazingena zingenile emsebenzini 
zimbikela ukuthi akaqaphele, kukhona okudla amantshontsho 
emsamo. Wacishe waphambana ikhanda uMtalaselwa ngenkathi 
ezwa lokho. Nakuba kwakungeyena umuntu owayejwayele 


ukuthandaza, kodwa wazithola esevala isicabha sehhovisi lakhe, 
wakhuleka. 

Kwabe sekuphazamisa ucingo olwangenayo. Wathi uma 
elubamba, wathola ukuthi lwalumazisa ngayo indaba yomkakhe. 
Wathula ecabanga, wabona khona ukuthi ayinuki ingosiwanga. 
Wabe esehlela neziphathimandla ukuba izinsuku zokuphumula 
kwakhe zingabe zisaba ngempelasonto, kodwa zibe phakathi 
nesonto. Wayengathandi ukugcina ngokuzwa ngosizwile, kodwa 
wayefuna ukumbamba oqotsheni umkakhe. UMtalaselwa 
akazange amazise uDumazile ngalolu hlelo olusha. 

Waqala-ke ukuvakashela kwakhe uMtalaselwa. Ngosuku 
lokuqala wafika sekuhwalele. Umkakhe wayengekho ekhaya. 
Wabe esebuza kuLerato: 

“Uphi umama wakho?” 

“Usemsebenzini. Usebenza ebusuku kuleli sonto.” Ezwe lokho 

uMtalaselwa ahlale ocingweni, balubambe ngale. 

“Kusesibhedlela lapho?” UMtalaselwa ebuza ecikekile. 

“Yebo yikhona.” 

“Ukhona uSista Zuma lapho?” 

“Yebo ukhona! Kodwa usewodini labantu abagula kakhulu. 
Ubomfonela ngehora leshumi nambili, uzokube esetiyeni ngaleso 
sikhathi. Ngizothi ubecelwa ngubani?” Kwathi khalakahla ucingo 
eselubeka phansi uMtalaselwa. Kwathi ukuba athole ukuthi 
uDumazile ukhona ngempela emsebenzini, kwathi gidi.

 Ngakusasa ekuseni uDumazile wamfica umyeni wakhe 
eselungiselela ukuphindela emuva eMgungundlovu. 

“Hawu, kwenzenjani wabuya phakathi nesonto?” 

“Ngakhohlwa yizincwadi zokushayela ebhantshini ngesonto 
eledlulile. Manje akusebenzeki kahle uma zingekho. Amaphoyisa 
ayavutha bhe emgwaqweni. Uma ekuthola ushayela imoto 


izincwadi zingekho, awakhulumi lutho kodwa akufaka phakathi. 
Bengilande zona-ke.” 

“Hhayi, ngiyezwa.” UDumazile angasoli lutho. Waphuma 
uMtalaselwa eseyogibela amatekisi. 

UDumazile wayeselungiselela ukuya emsebenzini ntambama 
ngenkathi okungumfana wakhe kumthela ngezinyembezi: 

“Mama, mama! Owami ubaba uyofika nini lapha ekhaya?” 
kubuza uMtholephi ngokukhathazeka okukhulu. 

“Usho ngani mfana wami?” 

“Ngisho ngoba ubaba kaSisi Lerato uyafika yena. Nami 
phela ngiyafuna ukuba ubaba wami afike. Futhi uSisi Lerato 
uyangitsakela ngokuthi ubaba wakhe umphathela amakhekhe, 
uswidi, imali, ushizi, upholoni kanye nedonono. Uye angincishe 
uswidi, athi angiye kubaba wami. Ngiyamfuna-ke nami owami 
ubaba azongilethela uswidi nemali.” 

Aqale athule unina esacabanga: 

“Yaqala-ke inkathazo. Okwakobani nje ukufikelwa nguSithole 
lapha? Ngeke, awu ngeke! Kuzofanela ngihambise yena 
umntanami aye kuyise e-Adams. Ehhe kuzokuba lula futhi kube 
yisu elingcono ngaleyo ndlela. Kungaba khona inkinga phela uma 
ngingase ngilethe uSithole lapha. Uma bengase baficane noMoloi, 
njengoba bengazani nje, cishe kungachitheka izishebo, kufe gula 
linamasi. Ngibe yini-ke mina lapho? Mh, kuzofanele kuhambe 
yena ngempela uMtholephi aye kuyise.”Wabe esethatha ethi: 

“Cha kulungile mfana wami, ngizoyilungisa indaba yakho.” 

Wajabula bandla umfanyana ukuzwa unina ekhuluma kanjalo. 

 Uthe esuka wabe eseya koxoxa noLerato ekamelweni. 

“Umama uvumile ukuthi nowami ubaba uzofika lapha ekhaya 
angilethele uswidi namakhekhe. Ngizokuncisha mfana.” Asho aze 
agodle ingalo kwasakuyithukusa ngemuva sengathi usewuphethe 
ngempela uswidi. 


“We, ubaba wakho uzoyithathaphi imali yokuthenga uswidi 
namakhekhe mame?” 

“Ubaba uyathesha, unenyuku mfana; futhi uzothenga imoto 
ebelethe isondo ngikutshele mina.” Asho kuze kube sengathi 
uphukula umlomo uMtholephi. 

“Ayikho into ongangitshela yona ngobaba wakho. Ubekade 
ehlala lapha ekhaya enguqhwayilahle, ehlupha umama 
ngokumcela imali. Futhi ubaba wakho ubehlupha kabi 
ngokusincintela ukudla. Thina mfana singakhuluma ngezinto 
zoMoloi, izinsizwa ezishaya ngensimbi emanzi.” 

“We bhatata! Okokuqala nje ubaba wakho ushaya ngeginsi! 
Ungcono kabi ubaba wami kunobaba wakho. Owami ubaba 
wathenga lo muzi wakithi. Uphi-ke umuzi owathengwa ngubaba 
wakho?” 

“Unamanga! Wazi kanjani ukuthi lo muzi wathengwa ngubaba 
wakho?” 

“Kwasho umama mfana, wathi lo muzi wathengwa ngubaba 
wami.” 

“Hhayi suka unamanga! Akawudayisanga ngani pho ngenkathi 
esehamba lapha uma kanti wawuthengwe nguyena? Unamanga 
nje wena!” 

“Uthini ngeginsi likababa wakho, waziba nje?” 

“Akulona iginsi, akulona nje! Ubaba wayithenga le moto 
ngikutshele!” Asho uLerato kubonakale nje ukuthi usethanda 
ukufudumala. 

“Wayehleli kuphi sonke lesi sikhathi engabonakali lapha? 

Wayeboshiwe! We gelele, uBaba wakho yibhantinti!” 

Asho aze ahleke uMtholephi. Acasuke uLerato. 

“Ngizomtshela umama!” Asho avule isicabha ngesankahlu 
uLerato, aphume eseya ekhishini lapho kwakuhlezi khona 
uDumazile. 


“UMtholephi uthi ubaba yibhantinti! Uthi futhi uhamba 
ngemoto yokwebiwa.” 

“Ukuthathaphi lokho uMtholephi?” 

“Angazi.” Asho kuze kube sengathi ufuna ukukhala. 

“Hamba umbize!” esho ngendlakadla. Aphume esejabulile 
uLerato eyobiza uMtholephi. Wangena ekamelweni maqede 
wamtshela ukuthi unina uyambiza. Wathi lacu, baphuma 
belandelana sebeyongena ekhishini. 

“Utheni kuLerato wena?” esho ngokufutheka. 

“Angishongo lutho mina,” sekuphika uMtholephi. 
Agxambukele uLerato: 

“Unamanga! Angithi wena uthe ubaba wayeboshiwe? 
Waphinda futhi wathi uhamba ngeginsi! Uyakuphika lokho?” 
Agwajaze uMtholephi, bese ethatha ethi: 

“Nguyena uSisi Lerato ongiqale kuqala. Uthe ubaba 
wayenguqhwayilahle. Wathi futhi waze waxoshwa nje lapha 
ekhaya yingoba kwakuyisihula sesihubengu.” Aphakamise izandla 
sengathi uyazithintitha uLerato, athi: 

“Hawu, hawu, hawu, unamanga! Angizange mina ngiyisho 
leyo nto! Ungiqambela amanga aluhlaza nje!” 

UDumazile wabona ukuthi seyiqalile-ke inkinga phakathi 
kwezingane zakhe, yileyo nayileyo izama ukuvikela uyise wayo. 
Wabona kungcono ukuba asheshe ayingene indaba ngoba 
uLerato wayesefuna ukusebenzisa izikhwepha. 

“Niyithathaphi yonke le nto eniyishoyo? Ngiyabuza, 
niyithathaphi?” Bagwajaze. Wabayala bobabili ukuba bayeke 
ukukhuluma izindaba zabantu abadala; izindaba ezingaphezu 
kwabo. UDumazile waphatheka kabi impela ukubona ukuthi 
yonke le nto isuswa wukuthi uMtholephi ufuna uyise afike 
naye lapha ekhaya. Wazama ukuxoxisana nendodana yakhe. 
Wayivumela nayo ukuba ivakashele uyise uma ithanda. Wajabula 


uMtholephi ukunikwa lelo lungelo. Okwakuyisifiso sakhe 
esikhulu kodwa kwakuwukubona unina etetemuka noyise khona 
lapha ekhaya ngoba noyise kaLerato wayenalo lelo lungelo. 

UMtholephi waqala-ke ukuvakashela uyise e-Adams 
ngezimpelasonto. Wakujabulela lokho uSithole, kodwa imanzi 
yakhe yavele yashaya amakhala zisuka nje. UMaNzimande 
wayeba namazwi ajoqayo enganeni; akhulume sengathi uhlezi 
nozakwabo. Zamphatha kabi lezo zinkulumo uSithole ngoba 
wayewezwa amazwi ayiziswana ebhekiswe endodaneni yakhe, 
kodwa ahluleke ukumkhuza umkakhe. Kwathi ekugcineni, 
uSithole wabonisana nendodana yakhe ngokuba ingabe 
isamvakashela lapha ekhaya, kodwa imvakashele emsebenzini. 
NoMtholephi wabona kuyisu elingcono lelo. Ngenhlanhla 
enkulu uSithole wayesethenge imoto nakuba yayingeyintsha. 
Kwakuyisekenyana elisabukeka impela. Kwakuye kuthi uma 
uMtholephi kade evakashele uyise emsebenzini, ambuyise 
ngayo imoto ukuza ekhaya. UDumazile wakuthakasela lokhu 
ukuba oyise bezingane zakhe babe nezimoto bobabili. Lokho 
kwanciphisa ukubukelana phansi kwezingane zakhe. Ngenkathi 
uMoloi kusenguyena yedwa onemoto, uLerato wayehlupha kabi 
ngokuqhoshela uMtholephi. 

Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi uSithole wajwayela naye lapha 
emzini kaDumazile ukuzobheka indodana yakhe. Wayevama 
ukuyiphathela uswidi, amakhekhe, izithelo ezinhlobonhlobo, 
ushizi, nopholoni njengokwesicelo sendodana yakhe. Kwakuye 
kuthi uma efikile uSithole, aphathwe kahle naye. Babemenzela 
itiye, kwesinye isikhathi bamphakele nokudla. USithole 
wayengaphumi endlini engazange akhiphe imadlana kuDumazile 
yokumqinisa iphakethe. Muveni nje wayesekukhuthalele kabi 
ukuhambisa uDumazile emsebenzini uma engena ebusuku. 
UDumazile wayengenankinga nje yokuthi abantu bazothini uma 
eshintshanisa izimoto zoyise babantwana bakhe. Wayezimisele 
futhi ukubatshela ukuthi uSithole unguyise wengane yakhe naye. 

Ngelinye ilanga uSithole wafika njengemihla ezobheka umfana 


wakhe. Wathi eqhamuka nje, wayekhangwa wuhuntshu lwemoto 
lumi phambi kwegalaji. Akathandanga ukungena ebaleni 
uSithole, kodwa wavele wama ngaphandle emgwaqweni. Kwathi 
ukuba uMtholephi ambone uyise, wasuka ngejubane eseqonde 
kuyena. Wathi efika nje kuyise umfana, wayethi: 

“Awungeni ngani endlini namhlanje baba?” Aqale athule 
uSithole, wabe esethatha ethi: 

“Ngekabani leya moto esebaleni?” 

“Ngekababa kaSisi Lerato. Bayadla endlini benomama.” 
Wafingqa imikhono yehembe uSithole. Waphuma emotweni, 
wadlwathizela egxathazela eqonde endlini. Wayehambisa 
okohlanya uqobo lwalo. Akabange esangqongqoza, wangena 
nezicabha. Wamfica uMoloi ehlezi etafuleni edla ngommese 
nemfoloko. UDumazile wathi nhla maqede wathi lacu, wathi 
pheshe endlini encane, washuda. USithole wasuka izithonto 
wahlala uMoloi ngobhongwana. Kwachitheka izishebo etafuleni. 
Wanklinkliza, wanklinkliza engqasha uMoloi waze wakweqa 
amehlo amhlophe. USithole wamdedela ngoba esembona ukuthi 
usephefumula kancane. Wathula isikhashana uMoloi elele phansi 
ngomhlane ubuso bubheke phezulu. USithole wamnyathela 
entanyeni ngesicathulo, wathatha wathi: 

“Ngizokubulala mina mfana wami! Ngokabani lo muzi 
ozithola sewudla amalantshi kuwona? Kusewotela lapha?” Athi 
qwebu uMoloi, bese ethi: 

“Mfowethu, masingabulalani ngenxa yomuntu wesifazane,” 
esho ngezwi elithambile lokuncenga. 

USithole walususa unyawokazi lwakhe olwalulokhu luthe nzi 
entanyeni kuMoloi. Wavuka-ke, wazithuntutha. Wazincengela 
kuSithole ukuba bangabe besaqhubeka nalo mdlalo ngoba 
uyingozi. USithole waphuma waqonda emotweni yakhe phandle. 
Wayidumisa, kwasuka amaphepha. 

UMoloi wanwabuluka naye waqonda kweyakhe imoto. 


Wafike wayivula, wangena, wahlala phansi. Indololwane yakhe 
yagqula phezu kwedolo, isihlathi sacamela entendeni yesandla 
wacabanga: 

“Yaze yangiklinya inja! Kuzofanele ngivuke kusasa 
ngiyobonana nodokotela. Ngifuna ukuba ake angibheke lapha 
emqaleni. Umminzo angisawuzwa nje kahle ukusebenza 
kwawo.”Wathi ethi uphakamisa amehlo uMoloi, wathola 
abantu sebethe ngu emotweni yakhe. Bathi bayambuza ukuthi 
kwenzenjani, kodwa wangathanda ukuphendula. Wakhuphula 
amawindi emoto wawavala ngci. 

UDumazile waphuma endlini encane selidume ledlula. 
Abantu base begcwele igceke lonke. Wayesangene ukusangana 
lokhu. Wasondela kuLerato, wathi: 

“Abalimazananga kodwa?” Lutho uLerato ukuphendula. 
Wayekhala mi izinyembezi, ezibhonqa phansi ebaleni. Kwaze 
kwasiza uMtholephi okunguyena owakwazi ukulandisa unina: 

“Eyi bewungabona! Bewungathi yile nto esasivame ukuyibona 
kuTV. UDaddy bewungathi uSuperman! Usuke izithonto wahlala 
emqaleni kubaba kaSisi Lerato. Eyi ngibone esephenqa amehlo 
amhlophe, bengithi useyagqashuka! Libe selithayima ithayima 
lami, lamdedela.” UDumazile wazama ukuya kuMoloi emotweni, 
kodwa wathi ethi gagaga, wayisusa imoto uMoloi. Wabe 
esehamba ebuza kunoma ngubani nje ahlangana naye ukuthi 
kwenzenjani. Abantu bazizwa becasuka nje ukubona uDumazile 
ezenza isiphukuphuku sohlanya. Wawuze uzwe abanye abantu 
sebethi: 

“Nx ! Kudala sabona ukuthi lo mfazi uzoshayanisa amadoda! 
Elakobani nje isoka lomfazi?” Babe sebehlakazeka abantu 
beNkosi beshiya uDumazile nenkinga yakhe. 

Akwaziwa ukuthi ngubani owaluma indlebe 
izintatheli ngoba kwathi kusa nje udaba lwabe selugcwele 
amaphephandaba: 


AMADODA AKLINYENE EBANGA UMFAZI WOMUNTU 

Kucishe kwaphuma isidumbu esigamekweni esenzeke 
kwelinye lamalokishi akhele iTheku. Abayizekayo le ndaba 
bathi la madoda alwa nje abebanga unina wezingane 
zawo. Umnumzane uZuma, okunguyena umnikazi 
womuzi, ubengekho ekhaya ngenkathi yesehlakalo lesi. 
Obekhulumela omakhelwane, nokho ongathandanga ukuba 
igama lakhe lidalulwe ngenxa yokwesabela impilo yakhe, 
uthe kade bayibona le nto ukuthi izokwenzeka. Wathi 
kufanele kubongwe iNkosi yamakhosi ngoba akuzange 
kuphume isidumbu. Abomndeni abathandanga ukuphawula 
ngalesi sehlakalo. Imizamo yokuthola uMtalaselwa Zuma, 
okunguyena umnikazi womuzi, yehlulekile kwaze kwashaya 
isikhathi sokushicilelwa kwephepha. 

Lolu daba luvela ephephandabeni nje, selwake lwafika 
ezindlebeni zikaMtalaselwa. Zase ziziningi izingcingo zimbikela 
ngokungaziphathi kahle komkakhe. Kwathi ngenkathi efunda 
iphephandaba, efica lolu daba, wacabanga masinyane ngesinqumo 
okufanele asithathe. Yayingasekho enye indlela ngaphandle 
kokuba amkhulule umkakhe. Wabe esehlela ukuthatha iholide 
eliphuthumayo ukuze akwazi ukubonana nabameli. 

Ngenkathi uMtalaselwa efika ekhaya, umkakhe wayeseqalile 
ukunyamalala. Washayela umphathi wesibhedlela ucingo ebuza 
ngomkakhe. Bamphendula bathi umkakhe uthathe inhlabakhefu 
engangenyanga; ngaleyo ndlela bemlandula. Kwacaca ukuthi 
uDumazile wayesebalekele kwamathanda-nhliziyo. Umsebenzi 
akabange esathanda ukuqhubeka nokusebenza ngenxa 
yokucikwa yilesi simo esikhona phakathi komuzi kaNxamalala. 
Kwadingeka ukuba uLerato aphume esikoleni ukuze abheke 
izingane zakwabo. USanele wayesadinga ukunakekelwa kakhulu. 

 Kuyo leyo nhlalo yokudideka kwabakwaZuma, kwatheleka 
ezembokodwebomvu zihlome zithe shi. 


“Yikhona kwaZuma lapha?” kubuza elinye lamaphoyisa. 

“Yebo!” kuvuma uMtalaselwa esehlahle amehlo okwenkomo 

izohlatshwa. 

“UDumazile yinkosikazi yalapha ekhaya?” 

“Yebo!” 

“Nguwena umyeni wakhe?” 

“Yebo!” 

“Uphi yena?” 

“Njengoba ngifika nje ngithola ukuthi umkami useshaye 
wachitha. Ngicabanga ukuthi ubalekele leli hlazo lakhe elivele 
lapha ephepheni,” esho ekhomba iphephandaba ayeliphethe 
ngesandla uMtalaselwa. Wayengasenamahloni okukhuluma 
ngamahlazo akwakhe. 

“Nathi kade sasimfuna. Umkhondo siwuthungathe sisuka 
eMzimkhulu waze wayosifaka e-Adams. Sifike lapho sabopha 
uMthovovo Mkhize owayeqapha isitolo sikaSithole. Usesikiti 
ngikhuluma nawe nje.”

 Kuvele kuhlwe emini kuMtalaselwa engazi ukuthi 
kukhulunywa ngani. 

“Lalela-ke, uzwe kahle ukuthi umkakho yena ungena kanjani 
ukuba simfune: Njengoba kwasha isitolo sikaSithole e-Adams, 
kunobufakazi obukhomba ukuthi umkakho uxhumene naleso 
sehlakalo.” Akhombise ukwethuka uMtalaselwa. Iphoyisa 
liqhubeke. 

“Izigebengu eziyizihlobo zomkakho zathengwa ngumnumzane 
uGwabinde, lona owathenga isitolo sikaSithole eMzimkhulu, 
ukuba kugqekezwe isitolo sikaSithole e-Adams bese kuphangwa 
impahla. UDumazile nguyena ungqondongqondo owaxhuma 
izintambo. Wahlela nephoyisa uMkhize ukuba kube lula ukwenza 
lo msebenzi. Umnumzane uGwabinde akazikhokhelanga 


izigebengu imali yazo. Zamdubula-ke zambulala. Uphenyo 
lwethu lumayelana naleso sehlakalo-ke.” Aphefumule kakhulu 
uMtalaselwa, bese ethi: 

“Sengathi nami ngizosizwa yinina ukuba simthungathe 
umkami.” 

UMtalaselwa wake wacabanga ukuba abikele omakhelwane 
bakhe lolu daba, kodwa wabuye wacabanga indlela abayiphilayo 
nabo. Yilowo nayilowo kwakuyinkomo idla yodwa, ungafunga 
ukuthi akwaziwana. Kwakungelula nje ukuba omunye aye 
emzini womunye ngaphandle uma kunesidingo esibalulekile 
esiphuthumayo. Wabuye wacabanga futhi ukuba ayobikela 
abazali bakhe ekhaya, kodwa waphathwa ngamahloni. Amazwi 
wokugcina kanina athi: “ Hamba juba bayokuchutha phambili,” 
ayesankeneneza ezindlebeni zakhe. 


ISAHLUKO SESHUMI 

Ngenkathi uMtalaselwa efika emzini wakhe eMlazi evela 
eMgungundlovu, wayevele esehlabekile yisifo simbe kodwa 
singakamqinisi. Ngemuva kwezindlebe kwakudumbe izindlala, 
ephethwe ngamathumba umzimba wonke. Wayengathandisisi 
kahle ukuya emtholampilo. Wayesaba ukuthi bazofike 
bamtshele ukuthi uguliswa yisifo esingalapheki. Wabona ukuthi 
uyosuke agule kakhulu-ke manje esephethwe yisifo sokwazi 
ukuthi uphethwe yisifo sini. Wabona kungcono ukulokhu edla 
imishanguzo yezinyanga. 

Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi ukufa kwaya ngokuya kudlonga. 
Kamuva nje wayesekhala ngokutshutshumba nokufutha 
kwezinyawo. Zaya ngokuya zivuvukala, zagcina seziphihlike 
izilonda. Izilonda zasabalala nomzimba wonke. Izindawo 
ezazigqame kakhulu kwakuyisezandleni, emlonyeni kanye 
nasezindaweni ezifudumalayo. Ukudla kwakungasadleki. Kwathi 
kusenjalo waxinwa yisifuba. Samphatha kambana-ke sona, 
ekhwehlela igazi. Umoya wawunqamuka kungaphefumuleki 
kahle. Kwenzeka konke lokhu nje isisu asimbekile phansi, 
siyamluma siyamhambisa. Imishanguzo yezinyanga yangabe 
isazwela. Baqala abantu ukunukana. Babesho idliso, umbhulelo, 
omamtsotsi nokunye okungamalutha. Kwayiwa kwabanamanga. 
Bathi kufanele enzelwe amagobongo. Enziwa, kodwa kwaba 
nhlanga zimuka nomoya. Kwathiwa indaba isemsamo, kufanele 
kulungiswe idlozi. Zahlatshwa izinkomo, kodwa ukufa kwadlonga 
kwadlondlobala. Wabuna, wagcina esengangabasemehlweni. 


Baqala abantu ukukhulumela phansi: 

“Nithi kodwa le ndoda ayiphethwe yilesi sifo samagama 
amathathu?” Bamncisha amehlo. 

Kwadingeka ukuba uMtalaselwa aphuthunyiswe esibhedlela. 
Imoto yashoboloza naye njalo yaze yayofika kulowo muzi 
wezimanga; umuzi oqoqela ndawonye abantu abaphethwe 
yizinhlobonhlobo zezifo. Ngenkathi efika, waficana nomnumzane 
uSithole kanye nephoyisa uMthovovo Mkhize. Iziguli lezi 
zazilaliswe egunjini lazo zodwa; igumbi labantu abagula kakhulu. 
UMaNzimande naye wayelaliswe egunjini labantu besibhuda. 
Naye wayebambekile impela. 

UDumazile wahlatshwa yisifo simbe maqede waphuthunyiswa 
esibhedlela kwaNongoma. Wayekade ebalekele esihlotsheni 
sakhe kuleyo ndawo. Walaliswa-ke esibhedlela. Abahlengikazi 
bamduduza ngokuthi uzosheshe alulame. Bamthatha bambeka 
egunjini lakhe yedwa ngoba isifo sasiya ngokuya simgabha. 
Ngenxa yesizungu, bamnikeza umsakazo. Wayekhonze ukulalela 
imidlalo, izindaba kanye nezimemezelo zemingcwabo. Kwathi 
ukuba abone ukuthi ukufa kuyamnqoba, wacela abahlengikazi 
ukuba babize abazali bakhe eMzimkhulu, umyeni wakhe eMlazi 
kanye nomfundisi. Nempela abahlengikazi benza njengoba 
beceliwe. Bazibhala-ke izincwadi. 

Ngokubona isimo esasingasesihle kuDumazile, kwasetshenziswa 
umfundisi kulaba abafika njalo esibhedlela ukuzokhulekela abantu 
abagulayo. Abahlengikazi bamcela ukuba asondele embhedeni 
kuDumazile ukuba baxoxisane naye. Nempela kwaba njalo. 
Umuntu weNkosi wavula izandla, wanikeza isiguli ithuba lokuba 
sizilahle eNkosini yaso. UDumazile wathatha wathi: 

“Ngenza iphutha phambi kukaNkulunkulu naphambi 
komhlaba. Umhlaba usuyangihlaba manje.”Wakhala. UMfundisi 
wamduduza, wakhuleka. Kwathi angaqeda, wathatha wathi: 

“UNkulunkulu owayekhona emandulo, osekhona 


nanamhlanje uzokuthethelela izono zakho uma uzivuma 
ngokuyisiminya. Kwasho yena uqobo wathi noma izono zibomvu 
njengegazi, kodwa uyozihlanza zibe mhlophe njengeqhwa.” 

UDumazile wazizwa efikelwa yithenjana. Wabona kufanele 
ukuba azivume izono zakhe. UMfundisi wasondeza indlebe yakhe 
kuyena. Waqala-ke ukuwuvula umlomo wakhe uDumazile: 

“Baba, ngaphula umthetho wesithupha uNkulunkulu 
awushiya kuMose. Angazi ukuthi ngawuphula kangaki.”Wathula 
uMfundisi. UDumazile wacabanga ukuthi akuzwakalanga kahle, 
kanti uMfundisi wathatha ngokuthi uDumazile usaqhubeka 
nokuvuma izono zakhe. UDumazile wayibeka ngenye indlela 
inkulumo kanjena: 

“Bengithi ngambatha namadoda abantu kaningana. Angazi 
noma uNkulunkulu uyokwazi yini ukungithethelela.” 

“Uma uzivuma kahle zonke izono zakho, uNkulunkulu 
akanamagqubu, uyathethelela.” 

“Ngelinye ilanga ngahlela ukuba kugqekezwe futhi kushiswe 
isitolo sikaSithole. Ngangiqonde ukuzuza mina kanye nezihlobo 
zami. Nganginethemba lokuthi isitolo siyobuye sakhiwe kabusha 
ngoba uSithole wayeyokhokhelwa ngumshuwalense. Ngeshwa 
elikhulu umshuwalense awuvumanga ukukhokha. USithole 
wagcina eyimpabanga ngenxa yami.”Wakhala. UMfundisi 
wakhuleka. Kwathi angaqeda, wamhlahlamelisa wamshiya. 

Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi uDumazile wayesehluleka 
ukuzivulela nokuzivalela umsakazo. Yingakho nje abahlengikazi 
base behlala bewuvulile njalo. Wayenganaki nokho ukulalela 
ezinye izinhlelo ngaphandle kwezindaba kanye nezimemezelo 
zemingcwabo. Ezindabeni zantambama ngalo lelo langa, 
umsakazi waqala ngokufunda izindaba ezingemnandi: 

“Ungqongqoshe wezempilo kwaZulu-Natali wexwayisa 
umphakathi ukuba uqaphele lesi sifo esichitheke umhlaba wonke. 
Sidla fumuka sidle silaza. Abantu bangazikhohlisi, alikatholakali 


ikhambi lokwelapha lolu bhubhane olungumashayabhuqe. 
Qikekelani ucansi olungaphephile. Ningathintani negazi noma 
uketshezi lomunye umuntu. Qaphelani insingo eke yasebenza 
komunye umuntu.” UDumazile wathula esazindla ngalezi zindaba. 

“Nakanjani kukhulunywa ngalesi sifo esingiphethe. Angingabazi 
ukuthi ngasithelelwa nguyise kaLerato. Awu Nkosi yami, wayeshilo 
kodwa ukuthi umkakhe washona esenciphile. Mina anginakanga 
ngoba ngimbona uMoloi eyitubesi. Mhlawumbe sengisitshalile 
nje lesi sifo kuyise kaSanele nakuyise kaMtholephi? Awu ngiyazisa 
Nkosi yami.” 

Kwathi ebusuku uDumazile walalela umsakazo kumenyezelwa 
amagama alabo abangasekho emhlabeni. Umsakazi waqala 
ngesikhulu isizotha lesi: 

“Nazi izimemezelo zemingcwabo umsakazo ozikhipha ngokukhulu 
ukudabuka. Umnumzane uMbhekeni Enock Sithole obengowase-
Adams Mission, ushone zingamashumi amabili nanye kuyo 
le nyanga. Ubeneminyaka engamashumi amahlanu ubudala. 
Uyongcwatshwa ngoMgqibelo ngehora lesibili emathuneni 
ase-Adams Mission ngemuva kwenkonzo eyokuba sehholo 
lomphakathi ngehora leshumi ekuseni. Sisho umnumzane 
uMbhekeni Enock Sithole.” UDumazile akaqhubekanga nokulalela 
umsakazo, kodwa wavele wakhihla isililo. Ngenkathi abahlengikazi 
bembona ekhala, baxakeka nje ukuthi kwenzenjani. Bacabanga 
ukuthi uphethwe yizinhlungu, bamlethela amaphilisi ukuba 
agwinye. Nakuba kwakungasagwinyeki kahle, bawabhucuza, 
bamnikeza, waphuza, walala. 

Ngelinye ilanga kade elele, waphaphama uhlelo lwezemingcwabo 
seluphakathi nendawo. Wezwa umsakazi esethi: 

“Akasekho emhlabeni unkosikazi uZenzile Cynthia Sithole, 
uMaNzimande. Ushone eneminyaka engamashumi amane 
nesishiyagalolunye. Uyofihlwa ngoMgqibelo emini emathuneni 


ase-Adams Mission. Ubeyinkosikazi kaMbhekeni Enock Sithole 
naye ongasekho. Sisho unkosikazi uZenzile Cynthia Sithole, 
uMaNzimande.” Ngalelo langa walulalela uhlelo lwaze lwaphela.
