Kwathi lungafika ekugcineni, wathandaza.

 Kwake kwaphela izinsukwana impela elokhu elulalela lolu 
hlelo kodwa bengaphumi abantu abaziyo. Kwathi engasazi nje 
kusihlwa, wezwa umsakazi esethi: 

“..., esokugcina: UMtalaselwa Goodman Zuma, obesebenza 
kuma-ambulense eMgungundlovu, akasekho emhlabeni. Umufi 
ubengumyeni kaDumazile Isabel Zuma ongumhlengikazi. 
Ushone eneminyaka engamashumi amathathu nesishiyagalombili. 
Uyofihlwa ngoMgqibelo emathuneni asekhaya kwaJilafohlo eMid-
Illovo. Sisho uMtalaselwa Goodman Zuma.”Wake wathi uzama 
ukuvuka embhedeni uDumazile, kwangavukeka. Kwenzeka konke 
lokhu nje abahlengikazi bayabuka. Babelizwile igama lomyeni 
kaDumazile limenyezwa ohleni lwezemingcwabo. Basondela 
kuyena, bamduduza. 

UDumazile wayengasathandisisi kahle ukulalela umsakazo. 
Wayewubona njengento emlethela izindaba ezibuhlungu 
empilweni yakhe. Wayefisa ukutshela abahlengikazi ukuba 
bawususe eduze kwakhe, kodwa kwakungasakhulumeki into 
ezwakalayo. Yena wayezwa ngezindlebe. Kwathi noma ethi 
uzokuwuziba umsakazo angawulaleli, kubuye kusho phela ukuthi 
indlebe ayinasimilo. Wazithola esezwa umsakazi esethi: 

“...uMthovovo Senzeni Mkhize obeyiphoyisa lasesitolo 
okwakungesikaSithole e-Adams Mission. Ushone ngesonto 
zingamashumi amabili nanhlanu. Ubeneminyaka engamashumi 
amahlanu nambili. Uyofihlwa ngoMgqibelo emini emathuneni 
aseSeventini eMlazi ngemuva kwenkonzo eyokuba eCinema 
ekuseni. Sisho uMthovovo Senzeni Mkhize. Umphakathi uyacelwa 
ukuba ungaziphathi izimbali.” UDumazile wasale eseqhubeka 
nokululalela uhlelo lwaze lwaphela. Wathi uzama ukuthandaza, 


unembeza walokhu ubalisile. Wayenamahloni ecabanga ukuthi 
abahlengikazi babezazi izindaba zakhe kanye nenkambo yakhe. 

Zahamba izinsuku isifo silokhu siqhubeka nokumudla 
uDumazile. Wayesephelile emzimbeni, eboqokile ebusweni. 
Amehlo ayesephumele ngaphandle. Izinzipho zazizikhumukela 
eminweni. Kwathi ebusuku elalele lona uhlelo lolo, umsakazi 
wathatha ngesizotha wathi: 

“UZitike Jeffrey Moloi obesebenzela inkampani 
yomshuwalense iNew Life, akasekho emhlabeni. Ushone 
zingamashumi amathathu kuyo le nyanga. Ubeneminyaka 
engamashumi amane nesikhombisa. Umufi wake wafundisa 
eZenzele High School eMbumbulu. Uyofihlwa ngoMgqibelo 
ligamenxe ihora lokuqala emini emathuneni ase-Avaloni, eGoli. 
Inkonzo yomngcwabo iyoqala ngehora leshumi ekuseni. Sisho 
uZitike Jeffrey Moloi.” Abahlengikazi bambona uDumazile 
ehlina sengathi uyakhala, kodwa kungaphumi lizwi. Abazange 
bamnake ngoba babethi useyahamba, becabanga ukuthi 
ukhaliswa wukwesaba ukufa. Nabo abahlengikazi base bemfisela 
uDumazile ukuba iNkosi isale seyenza isu layo imphumuze. 
Nokho insimbi nomzuzu kwakungakashayi. Laze laphela 
golokoqo isonto uDumazile esaphefumula. 

UDumazile wayesenesifiso sokuba aphume esibhedlela 
ayogulela ekhaya. Wayebona kuzifanela nje ukuhlala esibhedlela 
nokuhlala ekhaya. Wayengasanikwa mithi, engasanikwa maphilisi. 
Waziduduza ngokuthi ikhona indodakazi yakhe ezokumnakekela. 

Njengoba abazali bakaDumazile babebhalelwe incwadi, 
bayithola ngemuva kwesikhathi eside ngenxa yokungahambi 
kahle kweposi. Kwathi bangayithola, babona kufanele ukuba 
babikele abakwaZuma lapho uDumazile ayendele khona. 
Nebala kwaba njalo. Umthwalo waba sobhokweni sekuqondwe 
esibhedlela. Ngenkathi befika esibhedlela, abahlengikazi 
babakhombisa iwodi lapho kwakulele khona uDumazile. 
Bamfica ecimezile, kungabonakali noma usaphefumula yini. 


Unina wamnyakazisa. Wathi qwebu kancane ngamehlo akhathele, 
wacimeza futhi. UMaNdovela wabuka umyeni wakhe, bancishana 
amehlo. 

“Mnyakazise futhi mlingani, ” kusho uninazala kaDumazile. 
Nempela uMaNdovela wenza njalo. 

Wathi qwebu futhi uDumazile, wababona. Wasikhihla isililo. 
Kwakusakhala bani-ke kodwa! 

“Makoti!” 

“M…ma!” Izwi lingafuni ukugqashuka kahle. Izilonda 
zazigcwele ulimi, ziphihlike umlomo wonke. Ukuvula umlomo 
kuyena kwakusho ukuthunukala okwakumshiya nezinhlungu 
ezinzima. 

“Ngi…ngiya…xo…xolis…”Kwadlanga iphika. Ngokubona 
ukuthi ayingangabo, uMaNdovela wabiza umhlengikazi. Nebala 
wafika ngokuphazima kweso. UDumazile wakweqa amehlo. 
Akekho owabuza komunye ukuthi kwenzakalani manjena. 
Kwahenqwa. Umhlengikazi wabiza udokotela.

 Abazali bakaDumazile kanye nabalingani babo 
babonisana, bahlela ukuba umufi alandwe ngempelasonto 
elandelayo bese efihlwa emathuneni akwaJilafohlo lapho ayendele 
khona. Babuyela emuva-ke sebeyokwenza amalungiselelo 
omngcwabo. 

Kwathi kugamanxa ihora lesishiyagalolunye ekuseni, indlu 
yesonto yabe seyigcwele phama. Amalungu omphakathi ayegcwele 
ngothi lwawo. UMzimkhulu wawudilike wonke ukuzophelezela 
indodakazi kaNozulu. Kwakulokhu kuhlatshelelwa, iculo likhishwa 
ngelinye. Umphathi wohlelo wawuqala-ke umsebenzi wakhe: 

“Mndeni wakwaZuma, baba umfundisi nani nonke enikhona 


endlini ngiyanibingelela egameni elihle leNkosi yethu uJesu 
Krestu. Ngaphandle kokuchitha isikhathi, sizocela ubaba 
umfundisi asivulele ngomthandazo.” Asukume ngeculo 
umfundisi. Kwathi lingaphela, wacela indlu ukuba igebise 
amakhanda, ivale namehlo. Nempela kwaba njalo. Waqala-ke 
umuntu weNkosi, waqeqebula, kwagquma, kwancinciza wonke 
umuntu endlini. Wathi eyoqeda zase zigobhoza kwabaningi. 

Umfundisi wahlala phansi, kwasukuma umphathi wohlelo. 
Wathatha wathi: 

“Siyabonga kubaba umfundisi ngomkhuleko. Siyabonga 
kakhulu. Sengizothatha leli thuba ngilinikeze omunye 
ozokhulumela umndeni.” Kwasukuma uninazala kamufi, 
wathatha wathi: 

“Mphathi wohlelo, baba umfundisi nani nonke 
bantwana beNkosi ngiyanibingelela. Ngaphambi kokuba 
siqhubeke nomsebenzi weNkosi, ngithanda ukuba ngidlule 
enhlambulukweni bathandwa bakaThixo.” Asho maqede 
izinyembezi zigcwale amehlo. Akhicileke akhale. Kwabe 
sekuqalwa iculo. Ekupheleni kwalo, wathatha wathi: 

“UMaKheswa lo ngumalokazana wakwami ebengimthanda 
kabi. Ngeshwa lami bandla ubengangithandi yena. Ubekhombisa 
ngokusobala ukuthi yena akavundlanga kulesi sami isisu. 
Ngikhuluma nje wahamba kule ndawo enginukile ethi 
ngiyamthakatha; ethi ngithumela omantindane bami ukuba 
babulale ingane yakhe.” 

Akhale futhi. Kuqalwe iculo. Kwathi lapho liphela khona, 
wathatha wathi: 

“Nakuba kunjalo bathandwa beNkosi, angizange nakancane 
ngamzonda umfazi womntanami. Kuthe khona sesithola umbiko 
ngabalingani bethu wokuthi umalokazana wakwami uyagula 
esibhedlela, saphatheka kabuhlungu kabi. Asibange sisananaza 
sinomyeni wami, kodwa saphikelela khona. Samfica-ke umfazi 


womntanami. Okungithokozisayo bazalwane wukuthi 
wazixolisela ngomlomo wakhe kimina. Awu, babusisiwe labo 
abayokwazi ukuvuma izono zabo ngaphambi kokuba badlule 
kulo mhlaba. Nomalokazana wakwami waba naleyo nhlanhla.” 
Baqale iculo lokumbongela eNkosini. 

Kwathi lingaphela, uninazala waqhuba futhi: 

“Ezinyangeni ezimbalwa ezedlule, besifihla indodana yami 
uMtalaselwa khona lapha ekhaya. Akukapholi maseko, sesifihla 
umalokazana wakwami. Ngokusho kwemibiko yodokotela, isifo 
esabulala umntanami yiso kanye lesi esibulale umalokazana 
wakwami. Nokho-ke yiNkosi yodwa eyaziyo.” Akhale futhi, 
kuqhutshekwe neculo. Kwathi lingaphela, wathatha wathi: 

“Ngithanda ukuzwakalisa ilaka lami lokugcina kubalingani 
bami kanye nasemphakathini wonke lokuthi umfazi womntanami 
angizange mina ngamzonda. Nakuba kwakubuhlungu 
kuqaqamba enhliziyweni, kodwa ngimthethelele ngenhliziyo 
yami yonke. Angizimisele nakancane ukuba ngime endleleni 

yakhe noMdali wakhe. Ngiyabonga.” Ahlale phansi. 

Kwasukuma umphathi wohlelo, wathatha wathi: 

“Ngenxa yesikhathi bakwethu, sengizoshaya ngezimfuphi 
impela. Ngicela kusukume ozokhulumela abasekhweni.” 
Kwasukuma uKheswa ngeculo, weza ngaphambili. Kwathi 
angama, wathatha wathi: 

“Mphathi wohlelo, mfundisi nebandla, ngiyanibulisa! Ngizizwa 
ngimiwe ngamanzi emadolweni, akuvumi ukuba ngikhulume. 
Ngithi-ke kubalingani bami indodakazi yami buyihlulile ubukoti 
phakathi komuzi kaNxamalala. Nokho-ke kodwa bengingafuni 
ukuba sigxile kosekudlulile. Engithanda ukukubonga kubalingani 
bami wukubambisana okuhle kuze kube yimanje. Ngithi 
abakoNozulu babonga kakhulu.”Wahlala phansi. 

Umphathi wohlelo wabe esenikeza umfundisi ithuba lokuba 
avule inkonzo. Wasukuma ngeculo. Kwathi ekupheleni kwalo, 


wathatha wathi oweNkosi: 
“Bazalwane abathandekayo eNkosini, isifundo sokuqala 
sizosithola encwadini engcwele ngokukaJohane 11 : 25-26 lapho 
kufundeka khona kanje: UJesu wathi kuye: Mina ngingukuvuka 
nokuphila, okholwa yimi, noma efa, wophila. Nalowo ophila, 

akholwe yimi, kasoze afa naphakade. Uyakholwa yilokho na? 
Wabe esepheqapheqa iBhayibheli, wathatha wathi: 
“Isifundo sesibili sitholakala encwadini Amahubo 39 : 4-5 

lapho kufundeka khona kanje egameni leNkosi: 
Jehova, ngazise ukuphela kwami, nesilinganiso sezinsuku 
zami ukuthi siyini; mangazi ukuthi ngingodlulayo. 
Bheka, izinsuku zami wazenza zaba ngangobubanzi 
besandla; imihla yokuphila kwami akulutho kuwe; impela 
yilowo nalowo muntu ungumoya nje noma eqine kangakanani. 

INkosi mayibusise ukufundwa kwezwi layo. Ameni!” Abeke 
iBhayibheli phezu kwetafula, akhumule izibuko emehlweni, 
abheke ibandla. 

“Bathandekayo eNkosini, sihlangene lapha ngodadewethu 
obengomunye wezidalwa zikaThixo; isidalwa esakhiwa 
sabunjwa ngomfanekiso wakhe. Sihlangene lapha bakwethu, 
hhayi ukuzokhombana ngeminwe kumbe ukwahlulela, 
kodwa ukuzokhumbuzana ukuthi impilo yomuntu ozelwe 
ngowesifazane injengomhwamuko. Zithandwa zeNkosi yami, 
ngicela nazi ukuthi singabahambayo kulo mhlaba. Sifana nabantu 
abahlezi emthunzini ngaphansi kwesihlahla kodwa uhambo 
lona lulokhu lubalindile. Ngakho-ke akufanele ukuba sizitshele 
ukuthi sinekhaya lapha emhlabeni. Ikhaya lethu lisezulwini. 
Ngiyaninxusa bazalwane ukuba yilowo nalowo muntu aqondise 
indlela yakhe noThixo. Awu, bathandwa beNkosi! Ngithi uyeza 
uSimungunyagazi kusale amathambo! Akayalezi, ufika njengesela! 


Uma ekufica izindlela zakho zixabalazile, ngiyadabuka sihlobo 
sami ukusho ukuthi ngeke uwubone umbuso wezulu. Ngeke 
ubonane neNkosi uMsindisi wakho. Kuyihlazo mzalwane ukufa 
uphambene noMsindisi wakho. Kuyihlazo mfowethu nawe 
dadewethu ukufela ehlazweni, emanyaleni nasekungcoleni. INkosi 
enguMsindisi wethu yathi noma izono zibomvu njengegazi, kodwa 
yona iyozihlanza zibe mhlophe njengeqhwa. Ngakho-ke yithuba 
lakho leli sihlobo sami ukuba ulungise izindlela zakho usenganeno 
kwethuna. Akukho ukuphenduka ngalena kwethuna, kodwa 
sekungukwahlulelwa kuphela. Uma bewungahambisi kahle kulo 
mhlaba, umvuzo wukukhala nokugedla amazinyo. Uma uzinikela 
eNkosini manje, ayibheki ukuthi wayona kangaki. IyiNkosi 
enomusa nobubele, ayinamagqubu iyathethelela. Sondela-ke 
sihlobo sami uzodla ifa lasezulwini; ifa laphakade. Umntwana 
kaNkulunkulu akafi, kodwa uba nokuphila kwaphakade. Ameni!” 
Wahlala phansi. 

Kwabe sekungena umzala kaMtalaselwa ezolinganisa ubude 
nobubanzi bebhokisi. Watshela umphathi wohlelo ukuthi izinsizwa 
sezilungisa igumbi ethuneni. Kwathi angaqeda, umphathi wohlelo 
wathatha wathi: 

“Bathandekayo eNkosini, sesifike emaphethelweni alo 
msebenzi. Sengizocela ukuba sonke sikhuleke eNkosini ukuba 
ihambe nodadewethu lo esesiyomtshala.” Nempela basukuma. 
Bathandaza bonke kanye kanye. Kwathi bangaqeda, umphathi 
wohlelo wathatha wathi: 

“Ngokuyalwa ngabomndeni, umufi ngeke abonwe. 
Kuzodingeka-ke bakwethu ukuba sisihloniphe isicelo sabomndeni. 
Ngiyabonga.”Wacela omame ababili ukuba bathathe izimbenge 
ukuba kufakwe kuzo umnikelo. Umphathi wohlelo wabe esethi: 

“Uma seniphuma ngomnyango bakwethu, siyacela bandla 
ukuba niphonse lapho esitsheni. Sibusisiwe isandla esiphayo 
kunaleso esamukelayo. Ukufaka kwakho esitsheni kuyolekelela 
kakhulu kwabomndeni. Ngiyabonga.” Umfundisi waxolisa 


ngokuthi ngeke esaya emathuneni. Wabika ukuthi kukhona 
enye indawo okwakufanele aphuthume kuyona. Kwaqalwa iculo 
lokuphuma sekubhekwe khona emathuneni. Baphuma. 

Kwathi sebeqedile ukungcwaba, umfowabo kamnumzane 
uZuma wabonga kakhulu kubantu ngokubasingatha ngaloluya 
hlobo. Wathi bangaphezi nangomuso ukwenzela nabanye 
abagutshezelwe yifu elimnyama. Wacela-ke ukuba abantu 
badlule ekhaya basule izandla. Nempela kwaba njalo.
